    </w/index.php?title=S%C3%A8ng-keng_(Kong-h%C5%8De)/Chh%C3%B2ng-s%C3%A8-k%C3%AC&action=edit&section=1>]
    Kòan 1

 1. Gôan-khí-thâu Siōng-tè chhòng-chō thiⁿ kap tōe.
 2. Tōe sī khang-khang hūn-tūn; chhim-ian ê bīn-chiūⁿ o͘-àm; Siōng-tè ê
    Sîn ūn-tōng tī chúi-bīn.
 3. Siōng-tè kóng, Tio̍h ū kng, chiū ū kng.
 4. Siōng-tè khòaⁿ kng, sī hó; Siōng-tè chiong kng àm pun-khui.
 5. Siōng-tè kiò hit ê kng chòe Ji̍t, kiò àm chòe Mî. Ū ê-hng ū chá-khí,
    sī thâu chi̍t-ji̍t.
 6. Siōng-tè kóng, Chiah ê chúi ê tiong-kan tio̍h ū kiong-chhong, chiong
    chúi kap chúi pun-khui.
 7. Siōng-tè chiū chō kiong-chhong, lâi hun-khui kiong-chhong-ē ê chúi
    kap kiong-chhong-téng ê chúi; chiū ū án-ni.
 8. Siōng-tè kiò kiong-chhong chòe Thiⁿ. Ū ê-hng ū chá-khí, sī tē-jī ji̍t.
 9. Siōng-tè kóng, Thiⁿ-ē chiah ê chúi tio̍h chū-chi̍p kàu chi̍t só͘-chāi,
    ta-tōe tio̍h chhut-hiān; chiū ū án-ni.
10. Siōng-tè kiò ta-tōe chòe Tōe; kiò chū-chi̍p ê chúi chòe Hái; Siōng-tè
    khòaⁿ-i sī hó.
11. Siōng-tè kóng, Tōe tio̍h hoat-chháu, í-ki̍p kiat-chí ê chhài-soe, kap
    chiàu-lūi siⁿ ké-chí ê chhiū, hit lāi-bīn ū i ê chí, tī tōe-chiūⁿ;
    chiū ū án-ni.
12. Tōe chiū hoat-chháu, kap chiàu-lūi kiat-chí ê chhài-soe, kap
    chiàu-lūi siⁿ ké-chí ê chhiū, lāi-bīn ū i ê chí; Siōng-tè khòaⁿ-i sī hó.
13. Ū ê-hng ū chá-khí, sī tē-saⁿ ji̍t.
14. Siōng-tè kóng, Thiⁿ-ni̍h ê kiong-chhong tio̍h ū hoat-kng ê thé, lâi
    hun-piat ji̍t-mî; iā thang chòe tiāu-thâu, sù-kùi, ji̍t, nî;
15. ia̍h hō͘ in chòe kng-thé tī thiⁿ ê kiong-chhong, chiò-kng tī
    tōe-chiūⁿ; chiū ū án-ni.
16. Siōng-tè chiū chō tōa ê kng-thé nn̄g-ê; tōa ê kng-thé lâi kóan
    ji̍t-sî, sòe ê kng-thé lâi kóan mî-sî; iā chō chhiⁿ-sîn.
17. Siōng-tè hē in tī thiⁿ-ni̍h ê kiong-chhong, hō͘ in chiò kng tī tōe-ni̍h;
18. iā beh kóan ū ji̍t mî, hun-piat kng àm. Siōng-tè khòaⁿ-i sī hó.
19. Ū ê-hng ū chá-khí, sī tē-sì ji̍t.
20. Siōng-tè kóng, Chúi tio̍h siⁿ-thòaⁿ chōe-chōe ū o̍ah-miā ê tōng-bu̍t;
    chiáu pe tī tōe ê téng-bīn, thiⁿ-ni̍h ê kiong-chhong.
21. Siōng-tè chiū chhòng-chō hái-ni̍h ê tōa-hî, í-ki̍p chúi só͘ siⁿ
    chōe-chōe ū o̍ah-miā ê tōng-bu̍t, kok chiàu i ê lūi, koh chhòng-chō
    ta̍k-iūⁿ ê pe-chiáu, chiàu i ê lūi; Siōng-tè khòaⁿ-i sī hó.
22. Siōng-tè sù-hok in, kóng, Tio̍h siⁿ-thòaⁿ ke-thiⁿ chin-chōe,
    chhiong-móa tī hái-ni̍h ê chúi, iā hō͘ chiáu-chiah siⁿ-thòaⁿ
    chōe-chōe tī tōe-ni̍h.
23. Ū ê-hng ū chá-khí, sī tē-gō͘ ji̍t.
24. Siōng-tè kóng, Tōe tio̍h siⁿ ū o̍ah-miā ê tōng-bu̍t, chiàu i ê lūi,
    cheng-siⁿ, thâng-thōa, tōe-chiūⁿ ê cháu-siù, chiàu i ê lūi; chiū ū
    án-ni.
25. Siōng-tè chiū chō tōe-chiūⁿ ê cháu-siù chiàu i ê lūi, cheng-siⁿ
    chiàu i ê lūi, tōe-chiūⁿ it-chhè ê thâng-thōa chiàu i ê lūi;
    Siōng-tè khòaⁿ-i sī hó.
26. Siōng-tè kóng, Lán tio̍h chō lâng chhin-chhiūⁿ lán ê siōng, chiàu lán
    ê khóan; hō͘ in kóan-lí hái-ni̍h ê hî, thiⁿ-ni̍h ê chiáu, kap
    cheng-siⁿ, kap chôan-tōe, í-ki̍p tōe-chiūⁿ teh sô ê thâng-thōa.
27. Siōng-tè chiū chhòng-chō lâng chhin-chhiūⁿ I ka-kī ê siōng, chiàu
    Siōng-tè ê siōng chhòng-chō i; chhòng-chō in lâm-ê lú-ê.
28. Siōng-tè sù-hok in; Siōng-tè koh tùi in kóng, Tio̍h siⁿ-thòaⁿ
    chin-chōe, chhiong-móa tī tōe-chiūⁿ, lâi khah-iâⁿ i; iā tio̍h tī-lí
    hái-ni̍h ê hî, thiⁿ-ni̍h ê chiáu, kap tōe-chiūⁿ it-chhè só͘ tín-tāng ê
    o̍ah-mi̍h.
29. Siōng-tè kóng, Góa ū hō͘ lín piàn tōe-chiūⁿ it-chhè kiat-chí ê
    chhài-soe, koh it-chhè ê chhiū, kî-tiong ū kiat-chí ê chhiū ê
    ké-chí; lóng hō͘ lín chòe chia̍h-mi̍h.
30. Lūn-kàu tōe-chiūⁿ it-chhè ê cháu-siù, thiⁿ-tiong it-chhè ê chiáu,
    kap tōe-chiūⁿ it-chhè ōe tín-tāng ū o̍ah-miā ê mi̍h, Góa chiong
    it-chhè chhiⁿ-chháu hō͘ in chòe chia̍h-mi̍h; chiū ū án-ni.
31. Siōng-tè khòaⁿ I it-chhè só͘ chō-ê, khòaⁿ ah, chin-hó. Ū ê-hng ū
    chá-khí, sī tē-la̍k ji̍t.

    Kòan 10


    [siu-kái
    </w/index.php?title=S%C3%A8ng-keng_(Kong-h%C5%8De)/Chh%C3%B2ng-s%C3%A8-k%C3%AC&action=edit&section=11>]
    Iáu-boē choán-oāⁿ

CHHONG3-SE3-KI3 (1)

[1] Goan5-khi2-thau5 Siong7-te3 chhong3-cho7 thi* kap toe7. Toe7 si7
khang-khang hun7-tun7; chhim-ian e5 bin7-chiu*7 oo-am3; Siong7-te3 e5
Sin5 un7-tong7 ti7 chui2-bin7. 3). Siong7-te3 kong2, Tioh8 u7 kng, chiu7
u7 kng. 4). Siong7-te3 khoa*3 kng, si7 ho2; Siong7-te3 chiong kng am3
pun-khui. 5). Siong7-te3 kio3 hit e5 kng choe3 Jit8, kio3 am3 choe3 Mi5.
U7 e5-hng u7 cha2-khi2, si7 thau5 chit8-jit8.

6). Siong7-te3 kong2, Chiah e5 chui2 e5 tiong-kan tioh8 u7 kiong-chhong,
chiong chui2 kap chui2 pun-khui. 7). Siong7-te3 chiu7 cho7 kiong-chhong,
lai5 hun-khui kiong-chhong-e7 e5 chui2 kap kiong-chhong-teng2 e5 chui2;
chiu7 u7 an2-ni. 8). Siong7-te3 kio3 kiong-chhong choe3 Thi*. U7 e5-hng
u7 cha2-khi2, si7 te7-ji7 jit8.

9). Siong7-te3 kong2, Thi*-e7 chiah e5 chui2 tioh8 chu7-chip8 kau3 chit8
soo2-chai7, ta-toe7 tioh8 chhut-hian7; chiu7 u7 an2-ni. 10). Siong7-te3
kio3 ta-toe7 choe3 Toe7; kio3 chu7-chip8 e5 chui2 choe3 Hai2; Siong7-te3
khoa*3--i si7 ho2. 11). Siong7-te3 kong2, Toe7 tioh8 hoat-chhau2,
i2-kip8 kiat-chi2 e5 chhai3-soe, kap chiau3-lui7 si* ke2-chi2 e5 chhiu7,
hit lai7-bin7 u7 i e5 chi2, ti7 toe7-chiu*7; chiu7 u7 an2-ni. 12). Toe7
chiu7 hoat-chhau2, kap chiau3-lui7 kiat-chi2 e5 chhai3-soe, kap
chiau3-lui7 si* ke2-chi2 e5 chhiu7, lai7-bin7 u7 i e5 chi2; Siong7-te3
khoa*3--i si7 ho2. 13). U7 e5-hng u7 cha2-khi2, si7 te7-sa* jit8.

14). Siong7-te3 kong2, Thi*--nih e5 kiong-chhong tioh8 u7 hoat-kng e5
the2, lai5 hun-piat jit8-mi5; 15). ia7 thang choe3 tiau7-thau5,
su3-kui3, jit8, ni5; iah8 hoo7 in choe3 kng-the2 ti7 thi* e5
kiong-chhong, chio3-kng ti7 toe7-chiu*7; chiu7 u7 an2-ni. 16).
Siong7-te3 chiu7 cho7 toa7 e5 kng-the2 nng7-e5; toa7 e5 kng-the2 lai5
koan2 jit8--si5, soe3 e5 kng-the2 lai5 koan2 mi5--si5; ia7 cho7
chhi*-sin5. 17). Siong7-te3 he7 in ti7 thi*--nih e5 kiong-chhong, hoo7
in chio3 kng ti7 toe7--nih; 18). ia7 beh koan2 u7 jit8 mi5, hun-piat kng
am3. Siong7-te3 khoa*3--i si7 ho2. 19). U7 e5-hng u7 cha2-khi2, si7
te7-si3 jit8.

20). Siong7-te3 kong2, Chui2 tioh8 si*-thoa*3 choe7-choe7 u7 oah8-mia7
e5 tong7-but8; chiau2 pe ti7 toe7 e5 teng2-bin7, thi*--nih e5
kiong-chhong. 21). Siong7-te3 chiu7 chhong3-cho7 hai2--nih e5 toa7-hi5,
i2-kip8 chui2 soo2 si* choe7-choe7 u7 oah8-mia7 e5 tong7-but8, kok
chiau3 i e5 lui7, koh chhong3-cho7 tak8-iu*7 e5 pe-chiau2, chiau3 i e5
lui7; Siong7-te3 khoa*3--i si7 ho2. 22). Siong7-te3 su3-hok in, kong2,
Tioh8 si*-thoa*3 ke-thi* chin-choe7, chhiong-moa2 ti7 hai2--nih e5
chui2, ia7 hoo7 chiau2-chiah si*-thoa*3 choe7-choe7 ti7 toe7--nih. 23).
U7 e5-hng u7 cha2-khi2, si7 te7-goo7 jit8.

24). Siong7-te3 kong2, Toe7 tioh8 si* u7 oah8-mia7 e5 tong7-but8, chiau3
i e5 lui7, cheng-si* thang5-thoa7, toe7-chiu*7 e5 chau2-siu3, chiau3 i
e5 lui7; chiu7 u7 an2-ni. 25). Siong7-te3 chiu7 cho7 toe7-chiu*7 e5
chau2-siu3 chiau3 i e5 lui7, cheng-si* chiau3 i e5 lui7, toe7-chiu*7
it-chhe3 e5 thang5-thoa7 chiau3 i e5 lui7; Siong7-te3 khoa*3--i si7 ho2.
26). Siong7-te3 kong2, Lan2 tioh8 cho7 lang5 chhin-chhiu*7 lan2 e5
siong7, chiau3 lan2 e5 khoan2; hoo7 in koan2-li2 hai2--nih e5 hi5,
thi*--nih e5 chiau2, kap cheng-si*, kap choan5-toe7, i2-kip8 toe7-chiu*7
teh so5 e5 thang5-thoa7. 27). Siong7-te3 chiu7 chhong3-cho7 lang5
chhin-chhiu*7 I ka-ki7 e5 siong7, chiau3 Siong7-te3 e5 siong7
chhong3-cho7 i; chhong3-cho7 in lam5--e5 lu2--e5. Siong7-te3 su3-hok in;
28). Siong7-te3 koh tui3 in kong2, Tioh8 si*-thoa*3 chin-choe7,
chhiong-moa2 ti7 toe7-chiu*7, lai5 khah-ia*5 i; ia7 tioh8 ti7-li2
hai2--nih e5 hi5, thi*--nih e5 chiau2, kap toe7-chiu*7 it-chhe3 soo2
tin2-tang7 e5 oah8-mih8. 29). Siong7-te3 kong2, Goa2 u7 hoo7 lin2 pian3
toe7-chiu*7 it-chhe3 kiat-chi2 e5 chhai3-soe, koh it-chhe3 e5 chhiu7,
ki5-tiong u7 kiat-chi2 e5 chhiu7 e5 ke2-chi2; long2 hoo7 lin2 choe3
chiah8-mih8. 30). Lun7-kau3 toe7-chiu*7 it-chhe3 e5 chau2-siu3,
thi*-tiong it-chhe3 e5 chiau2, kap toe7-chiu*7 it-chhe3 oe7 tin2-tang7
u7 oah8-mia7 e5 mih8, Goa2 chiong it-chhe3 chhi*-chhau2 hoo7 in choe3
chiah8-mih8; chiu7 u7 an2-ni. 31). Siong7-te3 khoa*3 I it-chhe3 soo2
cho7--e5, khoa*3 ah, chin-ho2. U7 e5-hng u7 cha2-khi2, si7 te7-lak8 jit8.


[2] Thi* toe7 kap i it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5 i2-keng choe3-oan5. Ti7
te7-chhit jit8, Siong7-te3 oan5 I soo2 cho7 e5 kang; chiu7 ti7 te7-chhit
jit8 hioh I it-chhe3 soo2 cho7 e5 kang. 3). Siong7-te3 su3-hok ti7
te7-chhit jit8, teng7 choe3 seng3-jit8; in-ui7 ti7 chit-jit8 Siong7-te3
theng5 I it-chhe3 chhong3-cho7 e5 kang, chiu7 an-hioh.

4). Thi* toe7 chhong3-cho7 e5 lai5-lek8, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 cho7
toe7 kap thi* e5 jit8, chhin-chhiu*7 e7-toe2. 5). Soa*-ia2 it-chhe3 e5
chhau2-bak8 be7 u7 ti7 toe7--nih; soa*-ia2 it-chhe3 e5 chhai3-soe be7 u7
hoat; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 bo5 loh8-hoo7 ti7 toe7--nih, ia7 bo5
lang5 thang cheng3-choh hit e5 thoo2-toe7. 6). Chong2-si7 u7 bu7 tui3
toe7 khi2, lun7-tek8 pian3 toe7-bin7. 7). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 eng7
toe7-chiu*7 e5 thoo5-hun2 chhiau choe3 lang5, pun5 oah8 e5 khi3 jip8 i
e5 phi*7-khang; lang5 chiu7 chia*5-choe3 oah8 e5 leng5-hun5. 8).
Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 ti7 tang-hng, ti7 Ai-tian5, cheng3 chit8 e5 hng5;
chiong soo2 cho7 e5 lang5 he7 ti7-hia. 9). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 hoo7
tak8-iu*7 e5 chhiu7 tui3 toe7--nih hoat--khi2-lai5, ho2-khoa*3 ia7
ho2-chiah8; ti7 hng5 e5 tiong-kan koh u7 oah8-mia7 e5 chhiu7, kap
hun-piat ho2-phai*2 e5 chhiu7. 10). Ai-tian5 u7 ho5 lau5-chhut lai5
koan3-ak hit e5 hng5; tui3-hia hun-khui choe3 si3-tiau5. 11).
Thau5-chit8-tiau5 mia5-kio3 Pi2-sun3; chiu7-si7 seh8-lau5 ti7
Hap-hui-lah8 choan5-toe7--e5; 12). ti7-hia u7 chhut kim; hit-ui7 e5 kim
si7 chin-ho2; iah8 chhut chin-chu phek-gek8. 13). Te7-ji7-tiau5 mia5
kio3 Ki-hun3, chiu7-si7 seh8-lau5 ti7 Koo2-sit8 choan5-toe7--e5. 14).
Te7-sa*-tiau5 mia5-kio3 Hi-ti2-kiat, chiu7-si7 lau5 ti7 A-sut8 e5
tang--si3-e5. Te7-si3-tiau5 chiu7-si7 Pek-lat. 15). Ia5-ho5-hoa
Siong7-te3 chiong hit e5 lang5 he7 ti7 Ai-tian5 hng5, lai5 cheng3-choh
koo3-siu2. 16). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 hoan-hu3 hit e5 lang5 kong2,
Hng5-lai7 tak8-ho7 chhiu7 e5 ke2-chi2, thang sui5-i3 lai5 chiah8. 17).
Chong2-si7 hun-piat ho2-phai*2 e5 chhiu7, i e5 ke2-chi2 m7-thang chiah8;
in-ui7 chiah8 e5 jit8 li2 tek-khak si2.

18). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 kong2, Lang5 toa*-sin ka-ki7 toa3 m7-ho2;
Goa2 beh ka7 i cho7 chit8 e5 pang-chan7--e5, lai5 phit-phoe3 i. 19).
Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 eng7 thoo5 choe3 soa*-ia2 tak8-iu*7 e5
chau2-siu3, i2-kip8 khong-tiong tak8-iu*7 e5 pe-chiau2; chhoa7 kau3
hit-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, khoa*3 i beh chheng in sim2-mih8 mia5;
ki*3-na7 i soo2 chheng tak8-iu*7 oah8-mih8--e5, chiu7 choe3 hit e5 mih8
e5 mia5. 20). Hit e5 lang5 chiu7 ka7 it-chhe3 e5 cheng-si*, kap
khong-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, kap soa*-ia2 it-chhe3 e5 chau2-siu3 long2 ho7
mia5; chong2-si7 chhe7 bo5 chit8-e5 thang choe3 hit lang5 e5 pang-chan7,
lai5 phit-phoe3 i. 21). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 hoo7 hit e5 lang5 khun3
tang7-bin5, i chiu7 khun3; chiu7 theh8 i e5 hiap8-kut chit8-ki, pau-bat8
i e5 bah. 22). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 chiu7 chiong tui3 hit-lang5 soo2
theh8-chhut e5 hiap8-kut, cho7-chia*5 chit8 e5 cha-boo2-lang5, chhoa7
lai5 chiu7-kun7 hit-lang5. 23). Hit-lang5 kong2, Ta* chit-e5 si7 goa2
kut-lai7 e5 kut, bah-lai7 e5 bah; beh chheng-choe3 cha-boo2-lang5;
in-ui7 i si7 tui3 ta-poo-lang5 theh8-chhut. 24). Soo2-i2 lang5 beh
li7-khui i e5 pe7-bu2, kiat-lian5 i e5 boo2, in chiu7 chia*5-choe3
chit8-the2. 25). Ang-boo2 nng7-lang5 pi*5-pi*5 thng3-pak-theh, ia7 bo5
kian3-siau3.


[3] Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 soo2 cho7 soa*-ia2 it-chhe3 e5 oah8-mih8,
choa5 si7 pi2 in khah kau2-khiat. Choa5 tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2,
Siong7-te3 kiam2 u7-ia*2 kong2, Hng5-lai7 it-chhe3 e5 chhiu7, lin2 long2
m7-thang chiah8 mah? 2). Hu7-jin5-lang5 tui3 choa5 kong2, Hng5-lai7
chhiu7--nih e5 ke2-chi2 goan2 thang chiah8; chi2-u7 hng5 tiong-ng hit
chang5 chhiu7 e5 ke2-chi2 Siong7-te3 bat kong2, Lin2 m7-thang chiah8--i,
iah8 m7-thang bong, kia*-liau2 oe7 si2. 4). Choa5 tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5
kong2, Lin2 bo5 tek-khak oe7 si2. 5). In-ui7 Siong7-te3 chai lin2 chiah8
e5 jit8, lin2 e5 bak8-chiu chiu7 oe7 khui, lin2 beh chhin-chhiu*7
Siong7-te3, oe7 hun-piat ho2-phai*2. 6). Hu7-jin5-lang5 khoa*3 hit
chang5 chhiu7, ho2-chiah8 iah8 kah-bak8; koh hit chang5 chhiu7 si7 thang
him-boo7, hoo7 lang5 u7 ti3-hui7; chiu7 ban2 i e5 ke2-chi2 chiah8 i,
soa3 hoo7 i e5 tiong7-hu, i iah8 chiah8 i. 7). In nng7-lang5 e5
bak8-chiu chiu7 khui, chiah chai in si7 thng3-pak-theh; chiu7 pin2
bu5-hoa-ko2 hioh8, ui7 ka-ki7 choe3 kun5. 8). Jit8 liang5-leng2 e5 si5,
Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 kia*5-iu5 ti7 hng5-lai7; thia*-ki*3 I e5 sia*,
hit-lang5 kap i e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 bih ti7 hng5-lai7 e5
chhiu7-tiong, lai5 siam2-pi7 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 e5 bin7. 9).
Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 kio3 hit-lang5, tui3 i kong2, Li2 ti7 tah-loh8?
10). I chiu7 kong2, Goa2 thia*-ki*3 Li2 e5 sia* ti7 hng5-lai7, goa2
chiu7 kia*, in-ui7 goa2 thng3-pak-theh; chiu7 ka-ki7 bih. 11). Kong2,
Chi7-chui7 ka7 li2 kong2, li2 thng3-pak-theh? Goa2 hoan-hu3 li2 m7-thang
chiah8 hit chang5 chhiu7, li2 chiah8 i mah? 12). Hit-lang5 kong2, Li2
soo2 hoo7 goa2 choe3-phoa*7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5, i eng7 hit chang5 chhiu7
e5 ke2-chi2 hoo7 goa2, goa2 chiu7 chiah8 i. 13). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3
tui3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, Li2 soo2 choe3 si7 sim2-mih8 su7?
Hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, Choa5 in2-iu2 goa2, goa2 chiu7 chiah8. 14).
Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 tui3 choa5 kong2, Li2 i2-keng choe3 chit-e5,
soo2-i2 li2 siu7 chiu3-choo2, pi2 it-chhe3 e5 cheng-si*, kap soa*-ia2
it-chhe3 e5 chau2-siu3, khah-tang7; li2 beh eng7 pak-too2 kia*5, it-seng
chiah8 thoo5-hun2. 15). Goa2 beh hoo7 li2 kap hu7-jin5-lang5 kiat
oan-siu5, li2 e5 hoo7-e3 kap i e5 hoo7-e3 iah8 kiat oan-siu5; i beh
siong li2 e5 thau5-khak, li2 beh siong i e5 kha-au7-ti*. 16). Koh tui3
hu7-jin5-lang5 kong2, Goa2 tek-khak toa7-toa7 ke-thi* li2 hoai5-in7 e5
kan-khoo2; li2 beh kan-khoo2 si*-kia*2; li2 beh loan5-boo7 li2 e5
tiong7-hu, i beh koan2-hat li2. 17). Ia7 tui3 A-tong kong2, Li2 i2-keng
thia*-than3 li2 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 oe7, lai5 chiah8 Goa2 soo2 hoan-hu3
li2 kong2, Li2 m7-thang chiah8--i e5; soo2-i2 thoo2-toe7 in-ui7 li2 e5
ian5-koo3, siu7 chiu3-choo2; li2 chit8-si3-lang5 lo5-khoo2, chiah tui3 i
tit-tioh8 chiah8. 18). Thoo2-toe7 beh ui7-tioh8 li2 hoat chhi3-phe3 kap
chek8-le5; li2 ia7 beh chiah8 hng5--nih e5 chhai3-soe. 19). Li2 beh
koa*7-lau5 moa2-bin7 chiah thang tit-tioh8 chiah8, kau3 li2 kui thoo2;
in-ui7 li2 si7 tui3 thoo5 theh8--chhut-lai5; li2 pun2 si7 thoo5-hun2,
ia7 beh kui ti7 thoo5-hun2. 20). Hit-lang5 ka7 i e5 boo2 ho7 mia5, kio3
Ha7-oa; in-ui7 i choe3 cheng3-lang5 e5 lau7-bu2. 21). Ia5-ho5-hoa
Siong7-te3 ui7-tioh8 hit-lang5 kap i e5 boo2 eng7 phe5 choe3 i-hok8,
hoo7 in chheng7.

22). Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 kong2, Khoa*3 ah, chit-lang5 i2-keng kap
lan2 sa* chhin-chhiu*7, oe7 hun-piat ho2-phai*2; ta* kia*-liau2 i
chhun-chhiu2 koh tui3 oah8-mia7 chhiu7 ban2, lai5 chiah8 chiu7 oah8 kau3
eng2-oan2; 23). soo2-i2 Ia5-ho5-hoa Siong7-te3 kah i chhut Ai-tian5
hng5, lai5 cheng3-choh hit e5 thoo5, chiu7-si7 i soo2 tui3 i chhut e5.
24). Soo2-i2 koa*2 hit e5 lang5 chhut; ia7 ti7 Ai-tian5 hng5 e5
tang--si3 an-ti3 Ki-loo7-peng kap si3-bin7 tng2-seh8 hoat he2-iam7 e5
kiam3, lai5 hong5-siu2 oah8-mia7 chhiu7 e5 loo7.


[4] Hit-lang5 kap i e5 boo2 Ha7-oa tang5-pang5; Ha7-oa chiu7 hoai5-in7
si* Kai-un2, kong2, Goa2 tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa pi3-iu7 tit-tioh8 kia*2. 2).
Koh si* i e5 sio2-ti7 A-pek. A-pek si7 koo3-iu*5--e5, Kai-un2 si7
choh-chhan5--e5. 3). Kau3 jit8-au7, Kai-un2 chiong thoo2-san2 choe3
le2-mih8 hian3 hoo7 Ia5-ho5-hoa. 4). A-pek ia7 chiong iu*5-kun5-tiong
thau5-chiu*7-si* e5 iu*5 kap i e5 iu5 theh8--lai5 hian3. Ia5-ho5-hoa
koan3-koo3 A-pek kap i e5 le2-mih8; 5). chong2-si7 bo5 koan3-koo3
Kai-un2 kap i e5 le2-mih8. Kai-un2 chiu7 toa7 siu7-khi3, pi*3-bin7. 6).
Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Kai-un2 kong2, Li2 sia*2-su7 siu7-khi3? li2 sia*2-su7
pi*3-bin7? 7). Li2 na7 kia*5-ho2, kiam2 bo5 tit-tioh8 kam3-lap8? na7 bo5
kia*5-ho2, choe7-giat8 bai5-hok8 ti7 mng5-khau2; i beh loan5-boo7 li2,
li2 beh koan2-hat i. 8). Kai-un2 ka7 i e5 sio2-ti7 kong2. I2-au7 in ti7
soa*--nih e5 si5, Kai-un2 kong-kek i e5 sio2-ti7 A-pek, ka7 i thai5-si2.
9). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Kai-un2 kong2, Li2 e5 sio2-ti7 A-pek ti7 tah-loh8?
I kong2, M7-chai; goa2 kiam2-si7 koo3-siu2 goa2 e5 sio2-ti7--e5 mah?
10). I kong2, Li2 u7 choe3 sim2-mih8? Lin2 sio2-ti7 e5 huih e5 sia* tui3
toe7--nih au5-kio3 Goa2. 11). Toe7 u7 khui-chhui3 tui3 li2 e5 chhiu2
lai5 chiap-siu7 lin2 sio2-ti7 e5 huih, ta* li2 tui3 chit e5 toe7 siu7
chiu3-choo2. 12). Li2 cheng3-choh, toe7 bo5 beh chhut thoo2-san2 hoo7
li2; li2 beh si3-koe3 chau2, phiau-liu5 toe7-chiu*7. 13). Kai-un2 tui3
Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 e5 heng5-hoat8 thai3-tang7, ke3-thau5 ti7 goa2
soo2 oe7-tng--e5. 14). Li2 kin-a2-jit8 koa*2 goa2 li7-khui chit e5
toe7-bin7, bo5 thang toa3 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; goa2 si3-koe3 chau2
phiau-liu5 toe7-chiu*7; ki*3-na7 tu2-tioh8 goa2 e5 beh thai5-si2 goa2.
15). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 i kong2, In-ui7 an2-ni, ki*3-na7 thai5-si2 Kai-un2
e5, beh siu7 chhit-pe7 e5 po3-eng3. Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 ka7 Kai-un2 lip8
chit8 e5 ki3-ho7, bian2-tit tu2-tioh8 i e5 thai5-si2 i.

16). Kai-un2 chiu7 li7-khui Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5, khi3 ti7
Ai-tian5 e5 tang--si3, Lo5-tek e5 toe7, khia7-khi2. 17). Kai-un2 kap i
e5 boo2 tang5-pang5; i e5 boo2 hoai5-in7 si* I2-lok8; Kai-un2 khi2
sia*5, chiu7 chiau3 i e5 kia*2 e5 mia5 chheng hit e5 sia*5 e5 mia5 choe3
I2-lok8. 18). I2-lok8 si* I2-na2; I2-na2 si* Bi2-hoo7-nga2-li7;
Bi2-hoo7-nga2-li7 si* Ma2-thoo2-sat-li7; Ma2-thoo2-sat-li7 si*
Lah8-bek8. 19). Lah8-bek8 chhoa7 nng7 e5 boo2; chit8-e5 mia5 A-tai7,
chit8-e5 mia5 Se2-lah8. 20). A-tai7 si* Nga2-pat; i choe3 khia7-khi2
poo3-pi*5 chhi7 cheng-si* e5 lang5 e5 choo2. 21). I e5 sio2-ti7 mia5
Iu5-pat; i si7 choe3 it-chhe3 toa*5-khim5 pun5-siau e5 lang5 e5 choo2.
22). Se2-lah8 ia7 si* Thoo2-pat-kai-un2; i chiu7-si7 che3-cho7 tak8-iu*7
tang5 thih lai7-khi3 e5; Thoo2-pat-kai-un2 e5 chi2-be7 chiu7-si7
Na2-ma2. 23). Lah8-bek8 tui3 i nng7 e5 boo2 kong2,

A-tai7 kap Se2-lah8 ah, tioh8 thia* goa2 e5 sia*,

Lah8-bek8 e5 boo2 ah, tioh8 ti3-i3 thia* goa2 e5 oe7;

Lang5 siong goa2, goa2 thai5 i,

Siau3-lian5 lang5 hai7 goa2, goa2 thai5 i.

24). Kai-un2 e5 sin-oan na7 si7 chhit-pe7,

Chiu7 Lah8-bek8 e5 sin-oan tek-khak chhit-chap8-chhit pe7.

25). A-tong koh kap i e5 boo2 tang5-pang5; i e5 boo2 si*-kia*2,
piau2-mia5 kio3 Siat; si7 kong2, Siong7-te3 koh ka7 goa2 siat-lip8 chit8
e5 kia*2 lai5 thoe3 A-pek, in-ui7 Kai-un2 ka7 i thai5--si2. 26). Siat
ia7 si*-kia*2, piau2-mia5 I2-lo5-su7; hit-si5 lang5 chiah khi2-thau5
kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5.


[5] A-tong e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2. Tng Siong7-te3 chhong3-cho7 lang5
e5 jit8, si7 chiau3 Siong7-te3 e5 khoan2-sit lai5 cho7 i; 2).
chhong3-cho7 in ta-poo kap cha-boo2; ti7 in siu7 chhong3-cho7 e5 jit8,
su3 in hok-khi3, chheng in e5 mia5 kio3 Lang5. 3). A-tong chit8-pah
sa*-chap8 he3 si*-kia*2 chiau3 i e5 khoan2, chhin-chhiu*7 i e5 siong7,
piau2 mia5 kio3 Siat. 4). A-tong si* Siat liau2-au7 koh lek8-ke3
poeh-pah ni5; ki*5-tiong iau2 u7 si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2. 5). A-tong
ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 kau2-pah sa*-chap8 he3, chiah si2.

6). Siat chit8-pah lian5 goo7 he3, si* I2-lo5-su7. 7). Siat si*
I2-lo5-su7 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 poeh-pah lian5 chhit ni5; ki5-tiong u7
koh si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2. 8). Siat ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 kau2-pah
it-chap8-ji7 he3, chiah si2.

9). I2-lo5-su7 kau2-chap8 he3, si* Kai-lam5. 10). I2-lo5-su7 si*
Kai-lam5 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 poeh-pah it-chap8-goo7 ni5; ki5-tiong u7
koh si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2. 11). I2-lo5-su7 ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7
kau2-pah lian5 goo7 he3, chiah si2.

12). Kai-lam5 chhit-chap8 he3, si* Ma2-lek8-liat8. 13). Kai-lam5 si*
Ma2-lek8-liat8 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 poeh-pah si3-chap8 ni5; ki5-tiong
u7 koh si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2. 14). Kai-lam5 ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7
kau2-pah it-chap8 he3, chiah si2.

15). Ma2-lek8-liat8 lak8-chap8 goo7 he3, si* Nga2-liat8. 16).
Ma2-lek8-liat8 si* Nga2-liat8 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 poeh-pah sa*-chap8
ni5; ki5-tiong u7 koh si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2. 17). Ma2-lek8-liat8
ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 poeh-pah kau2-chap8 goo7 he3, chiah si2.

18). Nga2-liat8 chit8-pah lak8-chap8 ji7 he3, si* I2-lok8. 19).
Nga2-liat8 si* I2-lok8 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 poeh-pah ni5; ki3-tiong7
u7 koh si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2. 20). Nga2-liat8 ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7
kau2-pah lak8-chap8 ji7 he3, chiah si2.

I2-lok8 lak8-chap8 goo7 he3, si* Ma2-thoo2-sat-lah8. 22). I2-lok8 si*
Ma2-thoo2-sat-lah8 e5 liau2-au7 kap Siong7-te3 sa*-kap kia*5 sa*-pah
ni5; ki5-tiong u7 koh si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2. 23). I2-lok8 ke3-kiong7
hiong2-siu7 sa*-pah lak8-chap8 goo7 he3. 24). I2-lok8 kap Siong7-te3
sa*-kap kia*5, Siong7-te3 chiap i khi3; i chiu7 bo5 ti7-teh.

25). Ma2-thoo2-sat-lah8 chit8-pah poeh-chap8 chhit he3, si* Lah8-bek8.
26). Ma2-thoo2-sat-lah8 si* Lah8-bek8 e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 chhit-pah
poeh-chap8 ji7 ni5; ki5-tiong u7 koh si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2. 27).
Ma2-thoo2-sat-lah8 ke3-kiong7 hiong2-siu7 kau2-pah lak8-chap8 kau2 he3,
chiah si2.

28). Lah8-bek8 chit8-pah poeh-chap8 ji7 he3, si* chit8 e5 kia*2,
piau2-mia5 kio3 Na2-a, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa bat chiu3-choo2 toe7, hoo7
lan2 choe3 kang lo5-khoo2; ta* chit e5 kia*2 beh an-ui3 lan2. 30).
Lah8-bek8 si* Na2-a e5 liau2-au7 iau2 oah8 goo7-pah kau2-chap8 goo7 ni5;
ki5-tiong u7 koh si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2. 31). Lah8-bek8 ke3-kiong7
hiong2-siu7 chhit-pah chhit-chap8-chhit he3, chiah-si2.

32). Na2-a goo7-pah he3; si* Siam2, Ham5, Nga2-hut.


[6] Lang5 ti7 toe7-chiu*7 na2 khah-choe7, ia7 si* cha-boo2-kia*2 e5 si5,
2). Siong7-te3 e5 kia*2 khoa*3-ki*3 lang5 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 sui2, chiu7
chiau3 in soo2 ai3, chhoa7 in choe3 boo2. 3). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Lang5
ki3-jian5 siok8 ti7 jiok8-the2, Goa2 e5 Sin5 bo5 beh eng2-oan2 tiam3 ti7
in; na7-si7 in e5 jit8-chi2 beh kau3 chit8-pah ji7-chap8 ni5. 4). Ti7
hit-si5 u7 toa7-han3 lang5 ti7 toe7-bin7-chiu*7; au7-lai5 Siong7-te3 e5
kia*2 kap lang5 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 tang5-pang5, in chiu7 si* kia*2,
chiu7-si7 tui3 koo2-cha2 eng-hiong5 u7 mia5-sia* e5 lang5.

5). Ia5-ho5-hoa khoa*3-ki*3 lang5 ti7 toe7-chiu*7, choe7-ok chin toa7,
sim-lai7 soo2 siu*7 e5 liam7-thau5 tak8-jit8 long2 si7 phai*2. 6).
Ia5-ho5-hoa the3-hoe2 I cho7 lang5 ti7 se3-kan; sim-lai7 iu-bun7. 7).
Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 beh tui3 toe7-chiu*7 chau5-biat8 Goa2 soo2
chhong3-cho7 e5 lang5; chiong lang5 kap chau2-siu3, thang5-thoa7,
pe-chiau2, long2 chau5-biat8; in-ui7 Goa2 cho7 in liau2 u7 the3-hoe2.
8). Chi2-u7 Na2-a tit-tioh8 un-tian2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5.

9). Na2-a e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2. Na2-a si7 gi7-lang5; ti7 hit
se3-tai7 e5 tiong-kan si7 oan5-choan5 e5 lang5; Na2-a kap Siong7-te3
sa*-kap kia*5. 10). Na2-a si* sa* e5 kia*2, chiu7-si7 Siam2, Ham5,
Nga2-hut. 11). Se3-kai3 pai7-hoai7 ti7 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7-cheng5;
se3-kai3 chhiong-moa2 kiong5-po7. 12). Siong7-te3 khoa*3 se3-kai3 long2
pai7-hoai7; in-ui7 ki*3 u7 jiok8-the2--e5 in ti7 se3-kai3 e5 kia*5-choe3
long2 si7 pai7-hoai7.

13). Siong7-te3 tui3 Na2-a kong2, Ki*3 u7 jiok8-the2--e5 goa2 khoa*3 in
e5 boat8-ki5 i2-keng kau3, in-ui7 in e5 kiong5-po7 chhiong-moa2 ti7
se3-kai3; li2 khoa*3, Goa2 beh chiong in kap toe7 choe3 chit8-e7
hui2-biat8. 14). Li2 tioh8 eng7 chheng5-peh-chha5 choe3 toa7-chun5,
chun5-lai7 tioh8 keh pang5-keng, lai7-goa7 eng7 lek8-chhi*-iu5 koo5 i.
15). Toa7-chun5 e5 cho7-hoat si7 an2-ni; tng5 sa*-pah tiu2, khoah
goo7-chap8 tiu2, koai*5 sa*-chap8 tiu2. 16). Chun5 tioh8 choe3 thang-a2,
koai*5 chit8 tiu2; mng5 tioh8 he7 ti7 chun5-pi*; chun5 tioh8 choe3
sa*-chan5, hun siong7, tiong, ha7. 17). Li2 khoa*3, Goa2, Goa2 beh hoo7
toa7 chui2 hoan3-lam7 ti7 toe7-chiu*7, lai5 hui2-biat8 thi*-e7 ki*3-na7
u7 oah8-khi3 e5 jiok8-the2; ki*3-na7 ti7 toe7-chiu*7--e5 long2 oe7 si2.
18). Chong2-si7 Goa2 beh kap li2 lip8 Goa2 e5 iok. Li2 kap li2 e5 kia*2,
li2 e5 boo2, li2 e5 sim-pu7, long2 tioh8 jip8 toa7-chun5. 19). Ki*3-na7
u7 oah8-khi3 e5 jiok8-the2, tak8-iu*7 chit8-tui3, chit8-chiah kang--e5,
chit8-chiah bu2--e5, li2 tioh8 toa3 in jip8 toa7-chun5, kap li2 sa*-kap
po2-choan5 oah8-mia7. 20). Pe-chiau2 kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, cheng-si* kok
chiau3 i e5 lui7, toe7-chiu*7 e5 thang5-thoa7 kok chiau3 i e5 lui7,
tak8-iu*7 chit8-tui3 beh kau3 li2 hia lai5 po2-choan5 in e5 oah8-mia7.
21). Li2 tioh8 theh8 tak8-iu*7 e5 chiah8-mih8 chek-chu7--teh, thang
choe3 li2 kap in e5 chiah8-mih8. 22). Na2-a chiu7 an2-ni kia*5; chiau3
Siong7-te3 long2-chong2 soo2 beng7-leng7--e5 khi3 kia*5.


[7] Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Na2-a kong2, Li2 kap li2 choan5-ke long2 tioh8 jip8
toa7-chun5; in-ui7 ti7 chit se3-tai7 e5 tiong-kan Goa2 khoa*3-ki*3 li2
ti7 Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 si7 gi7-lang5. 2). Ki*3-na7 chheng-khi3 e5
cheng-si*, li2 tioh8 toa3 chhit-chiah kang--e5, chhit-chiah bu2--e5; bo5
chheng-khi3 e5 cheng-si*, li2 tioh8 toa3 chit8-chiah kang--e5,
chit8-chiah bu2--e5. 3). Thi*--nih e5 chiau2 ia7 tioh8 toa3, chhit-chiah
kang--e5, chhit-chiah8 bu2--e5, thang lau5 in e5 cheng2 oah8 ti7
choan5-toe7. 4). In-ui7 koh ke3 chhit-jit8, Goa2 beh loh8-hoo7 ti7
toe7-chiu*7, si3-chap8 jit8 si3-chap8 mi5; chiong Goa2 soo2 cho7
tak8-ho7 e5 oah8-mih8 long2 tui3 toe7-chiu*7 chau5-biat8. 5). Na2-a
chiu7 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa soo2 beng7-leng7 i e5, it-chin7 khi3 kia*5.

6). Tng toa7-chui2 hoan3-lam7 ti7 toe7 chiu*7 e5 si5, Na2-a lak8-pah
he3. 7). Na2-a chiu7 kap i e5 kia*2, i e5 boo2, i e5 sim-pu7, long2 jip8
toa7-chun5, siam2-pi7 toa7-chui2. 8). Chheng-khi3 e5 cheng-si*, kap bo5
chheng-khi3 e5 cheng-si*, pe-chiau2, kap toe7-chiu*7 it-chhe3 e5
thang5-thoa7, long2 chit8-tui3 chit8-tui3, u7 kang--e5 u7 bu2--e5, kau3
Na2-a hia, chin3-jip8 toa7-chun5, chiau3 Siong7-te3 beng7-leng7 Na2-a
e5. 10). Ke3 hiah e5 chhit-jit8 toa7-chui2 hoan3-lam7 ti7 toe7-chiu*7.
11). Tng Na2-a lak8-pah he3, ji7-geh8 chap8-chhit jit8, hit-jit8
chhim-ian e5 chui2-gôan long2 lih8-khui, thi* ia7 phoa3-khiah. 12).
Si3-chap8 jit8 si3-chap8 mi5 loh8-hoo7 ti7 toe7-bin7-chiu*7. 13).
Tu2-tu2 hit-jit8 Na2-a kap i e5 kia*2, Siam2, Ham5, Nga2-hut, kap Na2-a
e5 boo2, kap i e5 sa* e5 sim-pu7, long2 jip8 toa7-chun5; 14). in kap
pah-siu3 kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, it-chhe3 e5 cheng-si* kok chiau3 i e5

it-chhe3 u7-sit8-e5 kok chiau3 i e5 lui7, it-chhe3 e5 pe-chiau2 kok
chiau3 i e5 lui7, long2-chong2 chin3-jip8 toa7-chun5. 15). Ki*3-na7
jiok8-the2 lai7-bin7 u7 oah8-khi3--e5, long2 chit8-tui3 chit8-tui3, kau3
Na2-a hia, jip8 toa7-chun5. 16). Ki*3-na7 jip8 toa7-chun5--e5, si7 u7
kang u7 bu2 e5 jiok8-the2, chiau3 Siong7-te3 soo2 beng7-leng7 i--e5;
Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 ka7 i koai*--teh. 17). Chui2 hoan3-lam7 ti7
toe7-chiu*7 si3-chap8-jit8; chui2 tiong3 na2 koai*5, hoo7 toa7-chun5
chheng3-phu5, chun5 chiu7 li7 toe7. 18). Chui2-se3 chin-toa7, ti7
toe7-chiu*7 tit8-tit8 tiong3--khi2-lai5; chun5 phiau-liu5 ti7
chui2-bin7. 19). Chui2-se3 ti7 toe7-chiu*7 kek8-ki5 toa7; thi*-e7 e5
koai*5-soa* long2 hoo7 i im-bat8. 20). Chui2-se3 pi2 soa* ke-tiong3
koai*5 chap8-goo7 tiu2; soa* long2 hoo7 i im-bat8. 21). Ki*3-na7 ti7
toe7-chiu*7 u7 jiok8-the2 e5 tong7-but8, chiu7-si7 pe-chiau2, cheng-si*,
chau2-siu3, kap it-chhe3 so5 ti7 toe7-chiu*7 e5 thang5-thoa7, i2-kip8
soo2 u7 e5 cheng3-lang5, long2 si2. 22). Ki*3-na7 ti7 ta-toe7 u7
phi*7-khang chhoan2-khui3 e5 seng-leng5 long2 si2. 23). Ki*3-na7
toe7-chiu*7 it-chhe3 e5 oah8-mih8 long2 chau5-biat8; lang5 kap
cheng-si*, thang5-thoa7, i2-kip8 thi*-tiong e5 pe-chiau2, in long2 tui3
toe7-chiu*7 siu7 chau5-biat8; chi2-u7 Na2-a chham hiah-e5 kap i ti7
chun5-nih--e5 lau5-teh. 24). Chui2-se3 chin-toa7 ti7 toe7-chiu*7,
lek8-ke3 chit8-pah goo7-chap8-jit8.


[8] Siong7-te3 ki3-tit Na2-a, kap it-chhe3 e5 oah8-mih8, i2-kip8 kap i
ti7 toa7-chun5 it-chhe3 e5 cheng-si*; Siong7-te3 hoo7 hong chhe toe7,

Chui2 tui3 toe7-chiu*7 tit8-tit8 the3; chit8-pah goo7-chap8 jit8 au7,

khoa3 ti7 A-lah8-liap8 e5 soa*. 5). Chui2 koh chiam7-chiam7 siau,
tit8-tit8 kau3 chap8-geh8. Chap8-geh8 chhoe-it jit8, soa*-thau5 chiah

15). Siong7-te3 tui3 Na2-a kong2, 16). Li2 kap li2 e5 boo2, li2 e5
kia*2, li2 e5 sim-pu7, long2 tioh8 chhut toa7-chun5. 17). Ti7 li2 hia

20). Na2-a ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2 chit8 cho7 toa*5; tui3 tak8-iu*7
chheng-khi3 e5 cheng-si*, tak8-iu*7 chheng-khi3 e5 pe-chiau2, chhu2 lai5

18). Na2-a e5 kia*2, chhut toa7-chun5--e5, chiu7-si7 Siam2, Ham5,
