Sa-lah8 liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 si3-pah lian5 sa* ni5, koh u7 si* kia*2
cha-boo2-kia*2.

14). Sa-lah8 sa*-chap8 he3 si* Hi-pek. 15). Sa-lah8 si* Hi-pek
liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 si3-pah lian5 sa* ni5, koh u7 si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2.

16). Hi-pek sa*-chap8-si3 he3 si* Hoat-lek8 . 17). Hi-pek si* Hoat-lek8
liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 si3-pah sa*-chap8 ni5, koh u7 si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2.

18). Hoat-lek8 sa*-chap8 he3 si* lah8-ngoo5. Hoat-lek8 si* Lah8-ngoo5
liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 nng7-pah lian5 kau2 ni5, koh u7 si* kia*2
cha-boo2-kia*2.

20). Lah8-ngoo5 sa*-chap8 ji7 he3 si* Se-lok8. Lah8-ngoo5 si* Se-lok8
liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 nng7-pah lian5 chhit ni5, koh u7 si* kia*2
cha-boo2-kia*2.

22). Se-lok8 sa*-chap8 he3 si* Na2-hok8. 23). Se-lok8 si* Na2-hok8
liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 nng7-pah ni5, koh u7 si* kia*2 cha-boo2-kia*2.

24). Na2-hok8 ji7-chap8 kau2 he3 si* Tha-lah8. 25). Na2-hok8 si*
Tha-lah8 liau2-au7, iau2 oah8 chit8-pah chap8-kau2 ni5, koh u7 si* kia*2
cha-boo2-kia*2.

26). Tha-lah8 chhit-chap8 he3 si* A-pek-lan5, Na2-hok8, Hap-lan5.

27). Tha-lah8 e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2. Tha-lah8 si* A-pek-lan5,
Na2-hok8, Hap-lan5; Hap-lan5 si* Lo5-tek. 28). Hap-lan5 si2 ti7 i e5
lau7-pe7 Tha-lah8 e5 bin7-cheng5, ti7 i e5 pun2-toe7 Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 Ji*2
sia*5. 29). A-pek-lan5, Na2-hok8, kok u7 chhoa7-boo2. A-pek-lan5 e5 boo2
mia5 kio3 Sat-lai7; Na2-hok8 e5 boo2 mia5-kio3 Bit8-ka, si7 Hap-lan5 e5
cha-boo2-kia*2; Hap-lan5 si7 Bit8-ka e5 lau7-pe7, iah8 si7 I2-su7-ka e5
lau7-pe7. 30). Sat-lai7 bo5 hoai5-in7, bo5 kia*2.

31). Tha-lah8 chhoa7 i e5 kia*2 A-pek-lan5, kap i e5 sun Lo5-tek,
chiu7-si7 Hap-lan5 e5 kia*2, i2-kip8 i e5 sim-pu7 Sat-lai7, chiu7-si7 i
e5 kia*2 A-pek-lan5 e5 boo2, in sa*-kap chhut Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 Ji*2 sia*5;
beh khi3 Ka-lam5 toe7; in kau3 Hap-lan5 chiu7 toa3 ti7-hia. 32).
Tha-lah8 hiong2-siu7 nng7-pah lian5 goo7 he3; Tha-lah8 si2 ti7 Hap-lan5.


[12] Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lan5 kong2, Li2 tioh8 li7-khui pun2-toe7,
pun2-chok8, lau7-pe7 e5 ke, khi3 Goa2 soo2 beh chi2-si7 li2 e5 toe7. 2).
Goa2 beh hoo7 li2 chia*5-choe3 toa7-kok, Goa2 beh su3-hok li2, hoo7 li2
e5 mia5 choe3 toa7, li2 iah8 beh hoo7 lang5 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3; 3).
chiok-hok li2--e5, Goa2 beh su3-hok hoo7 in; chiu3-choo2 li2--e5, Goa2
beh chek-hoat8 i; toe7-chiu*7 ban7-chok8 beh in-ui7 li2 tit-tioh8
hok-khi3. 4). A-pek-lan5 chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hoan-hu3 e5 oe7, chiu7 khi3;
Lo5-tek iah8 kap i khi3. A-pek-lan5 chhut Hap-lan5 e5 si5
chhit-chap8-goo7 he3. 5). A-pek-lan5 toa3 i e5 boo2 Sat-lai7, kap i e5
tit8-a2 Lo5-tek; i2-kip8 in ti7 Hap-lan5 soo2 chek-chu7 e5 chai5-but8,
soo2 tit-tioh8 e5 lang5-giah8; in chiu7 chhut-khi3 beh khi3 Ka-lam5
toe7; in chiu7 kau3 Ka-lam5 toe7. 6). A-pek-lan5 keng-ke3 hit e5 toe7,
kau3 ti7 Si7-kiam3 e5 soo2-chai7, kau3 Moo5-li2 e5 siong7-chhiu7;
hit-si5 Ka-lam5 chok8 iau2 teh toa3. 7). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lan5
chhut-hian7 kong2, goa2 beh chiong chit e5 toe7-hng siu*2-su3 li2 e5
hoo7-e3; i chiu7 ti7-hia ui7-tioh8 tui3 i chhut-hian7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa
khi2 chit8 cho7 toa*5. 8). Tui3 hia i soa2 kau3 Pek-tek8-li7 tang--si3
e5 soa*, tah poo3-pi*5; sai--si3 si7 Pek-tek8-li7, tang--si3 si7 Ai;
ti7-hia ui7-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2 chit8 cho7 toa*5, kiu5-kio3
Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5. 9). A-pek-lan5 chiam7-chiam7 soa2--khi3 lam5--si3
e5 toe7.

10). Hit e5 toe7 tu2-tioh8 ki-hng, A-pek-lan5 loh8--khi3 Ai-kip8, beh
ti7-hia chiam7-si5 khia7-khi2; in-ui7 hit e5 toe7 ki-hng chin toa7. 11).
chiong-kun7 jip8 Ai-kip8, chiu7 tui3 i e5 boo2 Sat-lai7 kong2, Goa2 chai
li2 si7 bin7-mau7 ho2-khoa*3 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5; 12). Ai-kip8 lang5
khoa*3-ki*3 li2 e5 si5 beh kong2, Chit-e5 si7 i e5 boo2, in beh
thai5-si2 goa2, lai5 lau5 li2 oah8--teh. 13). Kiu5 li2 tioh8 kong2, li2
si7 goa2 e5 sio2-be7, hoo7 goa2 in-ui7 li2 tit-tioh8 peng5-an; goa2 e5
si*3-mia7 iah8 tui3 li2 lai5 tit-tioh8 oah8. 14). A-pek-lan5 kau3
Ai-kip8 e5 si5, Ai-kip8 lang5 khoa*3-ki*3 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 kek8-ki5
sui2. 15). Hoat-lo2 e5 jin5-sin5 khoa*3-ki*3 i, chiu7 tui3 Hoat-lo2
o-lo2 i; hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 hoo7 lang5 toa3 i jip8 Hoat-lo2 e5
ong5-kiong. 16). Hoat-lo2 in-ui7 chit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 ho2
khoan2-thai7 A-pek-lan5; A-pek-lan5 chiu7 tit-tioh8 iu*5, gu5, kang e5
lu5, loo5-pok8, lu2-pi7, bu2 e5 lu5, i2-kip8 lok8-to5. 17). Ia5-ho5-hoa
in-ui7 A-pek-lan5 e5 boo2 Sat-lai7 e5 ian5-koo3, kang3 toa7 chai-e7 ti7
Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 choan5-ke. 18). Hoat-lo2 chiu7 kio3 A-pek-lan5 lai5
kong2, Li2 tui3 goa2 soo2-choe3--e5 si7 sim2-mih8 su7? sia*2-su7 bo5 ka7
goa2 kong2 i si7 li2 e5 boo2? 19). Sia*2-su7 chheng i choe3 sio2-be7?
ti3-kau3 goa2 chiong i chhoa7 lai5 choe3 goa2 e5 boo2; ta* li2 e5 boo2
ti7-chia, thang chhoa7 i, choe3 li2 khi2. 20). Tui3 hit-tiap8 Hoat-lo2
ui7-tioh8 i lai5 hoan-hu3 lang5; in chiu7 chiong i kap i e5 boo2 kap i
soo2-u7--e5, long2 sang3 i khi3.


[13] A-pek-lan5 tui3 Ai-kip8 chiu*7--khi3, i kap i e5 boo2 kap i soo2
u7--e5, lian5 Lo5-tek, long2 khi3 Lam5-toe7. 2). A-pek-lan5 e5 gu5,
gun5, kim chin-choe7. 3). I tui3 Lam5-toe7 chaim7-chiam7 khi3
Pek-tek8-li7, kau3 Pek-tek8-li7 kap Ai e5 tiong-kan, cha2-cheng5 tah
poo3-pi*5 e5 soo2-chai7; kau3 i khi2-thau5 khi2 toa*5 e5 soo2-chai7;
A-pek-lan5 ti7-hia kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5. 5). Kap A-pek-lan5
tang5 kia*5 e5 Lo5-tek iah8 u7 iu*5-kun5, gu5-kun5, poo3-pi*5. 6). Hit
e5 toe7 chiu7 boe7 iong5-un2--tit in sa*-kap khia7; in-ui7 in e5
chai5-but8 choe7, in chiah boe7-oe7 sa*-kap khia7. 7). A-pek-lan5 e5
bok8-chia2 kap Lo5-tek e5 bok8-chia2 sa*-chi*; tng-si5 Ka-lam5 lang5 kap
Pi2-li7-se2 lang5 ti7 hit e5 toe7 khia7-khi2. 8). A-pek-lan5 ka7 Lo5-tek
kong2, Li2 goa2 m7-thang oan-ke, li2 e5 bok8-chia2 kap goa2 e5
bok8-chia2 iah8 m7-thang oan-ke; in-ui7 lan2 si7 kut-jiok8 e5 chhin. 9).
Choan5-toe7 kiam2 bo5 ti7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 mah? chhia*2 li2
li7-khui goa2; li2 to3-peng5, goa2 chiu7 chia*3-peng5; li2 chia*3-peng5,
goa2 chiu7 to3-peng5. 10). Lo5-tek kiah8-bak8 khoa*3 Iok-tan3 ho5
it-phian3 e5 Pi*5-iu*5, tit8-kau3 So2-ji*2 e5 loo7, long2 chin
lun7-tek8; hit e5 toe7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa be7 biat8 Soo2-to-ma2
Go5-moo5-lah8 i2-cheng5, chhin-chhiu*7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 hng5, iah8
chhin-chhiu*7 Ai-kip8 e5 toe7. 11). Tui3 an2-ni Lo5-tek keng2 Iok-tan3
ho5 it-phian3 e5 Pi*5-iu*5, chhian-soa2 khi3 tang--si3; in chiu7 tai7-ke
pun-khui. 12). A-pek-lan5 khia7-khi2 Ka-lam5 toe7, Lo5-tek khia7-khi2
Pi*5-iu*5 chiah e5 sia*5; soa2 i e5 poo3-pi*5 kau3 Soo2-to-ma2. 13).
Soo2-to-ma2 lang5 kek8-phai*2, toa7-toa7 tek-choe7 Ia5-ho5-hoa.

14). Lo5-tek li7-piat8 liau2-au7, Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lan5 kong2, Li2
kiah8-bak8, tui3 li2 soo2 tiam3 e5 soo2-chai7, ng3 tang sai lam5 pak
lai5 khoa*3; 15). in-ui7 li2 soo2 khoa*3-ki*3 it-chhe3 e5 toe7, Goa2
long2 beh hoo7 li2, kap li2 e5 hoo7-e3, tit8-kau3 eng2-oan2. 16). Goa2
iah8 beh hoo7 li2 e5 hoo7-e3 chhin-chhiu*7 toe7-chiu*7 e5 thoo5-soa;
lang5 na7 oe7 sng3 toe7-chiu*7 e5 thoo5-soa, chiah oe7 sng3 li2 e5
hoo7-e3. 17). Li2 khi2-lai5 pian3-kia*5 chit e5 toe7 e5 hoai*5-tit8,
in-ui7 Goa2 beh chiong chit e5 toe7 hoo7 li2. 18). A-pek-lan5 chiu7
poa*-soa2 poo3-pi*5 kau3 Hi-pek-lun5, oa2 Ban7-li7 hiah e5 siong7-chhiu7
khia7-khi2; ti7-hia ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa khi2 chit8 cho7 toa*5.


[14] Tng Am3-lah8-hui choe3 Si7-na2 ong5, A-liok8 choe3 I2-lah8-sat
ong5, Ki-tai7-lo2-ma2 choe3 I2-lan5 ong5, The5-tat8 choe3 Ko-in3 ong5 e5
si5, 2). in lai5 kong-kek Soo2-to-ma2 ong5 Pi2-lah8, Go5-moo5-lah8 ong5
Pi2-sa, Ap-ma2 ong5 Si7-lap8, Se2-phian ong5 Si7-bi2-piat8, i2-kip8
Pi2-lah8 ong5 (Pi2-lah8 chiu7-si7 So2-ji*2). 3). In long2 chu7-hoe7 ti7
Se-teng5 e5 soa*-kok; Se-teng5 soa*-kok chiu7-si7 Iam5-hai2. 4). In
hok8-sai7 Ki-tai7-lo2-ma2 chap8-ji7 ni5 ku2; kau3 chap8-sa*--ni5
poe7-poan7. 5). Chap8-si3--ni5 Ki-tai7-lo2-ma2, kap tang5 hoe7-beng5
chiah e5 ong5, long2 lai5, ti7 A-tek8-lut8-ka-leng5 thai5-ia*5
Li2-hoat8-im lang5, ti7 Ham5 Soo-se lang5, ti7 Sa-bi5-ki-liat8-teng5
I2-bi2 lang5, ti7 Ho5-li7 lang5 e5 Se-ji*2 soa* Ho5-li7 lang5, kau3 kun7
ti7 khong3-ia2 e5 I2-lek8-pa-lan5. 7). In to3-tng2 kau3 An-bit8-pa,
chiu7-si7 Ka-te-su, kong-kek A-ma2-lek8 choan5-toe7, kap khia7-khi2 ti7
Hap-se2-sun7-tha-ma2 e5 A-moo5-li7 lang5. 8). Tui3 hit-tiap8 Soo2-to-ma2
ong5, Go5-moo5-lah8 ong5, Ap-ma2 ong5, Se2-phian ong5, Pi2-lah8 ong5,
(Pi2-lah8 chiu7-si7 So2-ji*2), long2 chhut-lai5 ti7 Se-teng5 e5 soa*-kok
pai5-tin7, kap in kau3-chian3; 9). chiu7-si7 kap I2-lan5 ong5
Ki-tai7-lo2-ma2, Ko-in3 ong5 The5-tat8, Si7-na2 ong5 Am3-lah8-hui,
I2-lah8-sat ong5 A-liok8 kau-chian3; si3 e5 ong5 tui3-tek8 goo7 e5 ong5.
10). Se-teng5 soa*-kok long2 si7 chioh8-iu5 khi*; Soo2-to-ma2
Go5-moo5-lah8 chiah e5 ong5 to5-chau2, poah8 ti7-hia; ki5-u5--e5 chau2
chiu*7-soa*. 11). In chiu7 chiong Soo2-to-ma2 Go5-moo5-lah8 e5
chai5-but8, i2-kip8 in e5 kan-niu5 long2 chhiu*2, choe3 in khi3. 12).
Koh chiong A-pek-lan5 e5 tit8 Lo5-tek, kap i e5 chai5-but8 chhiu*2-khi3;
hit-si5 Lo5-tek toa3 ti7 Soo2-to-ma2.

13). U7 chit8 e5 to5-chau2 e5 lang5 lai5 ka7 Hi-pek-lai5 lang5
A-pek-lan5 kong2; hit-si5 A-pek-lan5 khia7-khi2 ti7 A-moo5-li7 lang5
Ban7-li7 e5 siong7-chhiu7 hit soo2-chai7, Ban7-li7 kap I2-sit8-kok kap
A-nai2 long2 si7 hia*-ti7, u7 kap A-pek-lan5 lian5-beng5. 14).
A-pek-lan5 thia*-ki*3 i e5 tit8 hoo7 lang5 liah8--khi3, chiu7 chhoa7
seng-iong2 ti7 i e5 ke--nih cheng-lian7 e5 chong3-teng, sa*-pah
chap8-poeh lang5, tui-jip kau3 Tan3. 15). I kap i e5 loo5-pok8 thau3-mi5
pun-tui7, kong-kek--in; tui kau3 Tai7-ma2-sek to3-peng5 e5 Ho5-pa. 16).
Chiong it-chhe3 e5 chai5-but8 chhiu*2 to3-tng2, lian5 i e5 tit8-a2
Lo5-tek kap i e5 chai5-but8, i2-kip8 hu7-lu2 peh-si*3, iah8 long2
chhiu*2 to3-tng2.

17). A-pek-lan5 thai5-ia*5 Ki-tai7-lo2-ma2, i2-kip8 kap i choe3-tin7
chiah e5 ong5, to3--lai5 e5 si5, Soo2-to-ma2 ong5 chhut-lai5, kau3
Sa-bi2 e5 soa*-kok, ngia5-chih i; Sa-bi2 e5 soa*-kok chiu7-si7 Ong5 e5
soa*-kok. 18). Iah8 u7 Sat-leng2 ong5 Bek8-ki-se2-tek toa3 pia*2 kap
chiu2 chhut-lai5; i si7 Chi3-koai*5 Siong7-te3 e5 che3-si; 19).
chiok-hok i kong2, Goan7 thi*-toe7 e5 Chu2, Chi3-koai*5 e5 Siong7-te3
su3-hok A-pek-lan5. 20). Chi3-koai*5 e5 Siong7-te3 chiong tui3-tek8 kau
ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, eng-kai o-lo2 I. A-pek-lan5 chiong long2-chong2 soo2
tit-tioh8--e5, chap8-hun7 theh8 chit8-hun7 hoo7 i. 21). Soo2-to-ma2 ong5
ka7 A-pek-lan5 kong2, Chiong lang5 kui goa2; mih8 long2 hoo7 li2. 22).
A-pek-lan5 ka7 Soo2-to-ma2 ong5 kong2, Goa2 u7 ki2 thi*-toe7 e5 Chu2
Chi3-koai*5 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa lai5 chiu3-choa7, 23). hoan7-na7
li2 e5 mih8, chiu7 chit8 tiau5 soa*3 chit8 tiau5 oe5-toa3, goa2 long2
m7-theh8, bian2-tit li2 kong2, Goa2 hoo7 A-pek-lan5 ho2-giah8; 24).
chi2-u7 siau3-lian5 lang5 soo2 chiah8 e5, i2-kip8 kap goa2 tang5-kia*5
e5 lang5 A-nai2, I2-sit8-kok, Ban7-li7, soo2 eng3-tit e5 hun7-giah8,
thang chhut-chai7 in theh8.


[15] Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 liau2-au7, Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 oe7 ti7
i*7-siong7-tiong lim5-kau3 A-pek-lan5, kong2, A-pek-lan5 ah, li2
m7-bian2 kia*, Goa2 si7 li2 e5 tin5-pai5, si7 li2 kek8-toa7 e5
po3-siu*2. 2). A-pek-lan5 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 beh hoo7 goa2
sim2-mih8, goa2 i2-keng bo5 kia*2; seng5-chiap goa2 e5 ke-giap8--e5,
chiu7-si7 Tai7-ma2-sek lang5 I2-li7-i2-sia7? 3). A-pek-lan5 koh kong2,
Li2 bo5 hoo7 goa2 u7 hoo7-e3, hit e5 si* ti7 goa2 ke-lai7--e5 si7 goa2
e5 hoo7-su5. 4). Ia5-ho5-hoa koh lim5-kau3, ka7 i kong2, Chit-lang5
m7-si7 beh choe3 li2 e5 hoo7-su5; tui3 li2 pun2-sin chhut--e5, chiah si7
choe3 li2 e5 hoo7-su5. 5). Chiu7 chhoa7 i chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7 kong2,
Li2 khoa*3 thi*, sng3 hiah e5 chhi*, li2 sng3 oe7 liau2 a2-boe7; koh
tui3 i kong2, Li2 e5 hoo7-e3 iah8 beh chhin-chhiu*7 an2-ni. 6).
A-pek-lan5 sin3 Ia5-ho5-hoa; I chiu7 ka7 i sng3 choe3 gi7. 7). Koh tui3
i kong2, Goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa, bat chhoa7 li2 chhut Ka-lek8-ti2 e5 Ji*2
sia*5, ui7-tioh8 beh chiong chit e5 toe7 hoo7 li2 choe3-giap8. 8).
A-pek-lan5 kong2, Chu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 chai*2-iu*7 oe7 chai beh
tit-tioh8 chit e5 toe7 choe3-giap8 ah? 9). I ka7 i kong2, Li2 ka7 Goa2
chhu2 chit8-chiah sa*-ni5 bu2 e5 gu5, chit8-chiah sa*-ni5 bu2 e5
soa*-iu*5, chit8-chiah sa*-ni5 kang e5 mi5-iu*5, chit8-chiah ka-chui,
chit8-chiah chi*2-a2. 10). I chiu7 chhu2 chiah e5 mih8 lai5, tak8-iu*7
tui3-tiong phoa3-khui choe3 nng7-peng5, chit-peng5 kap hit-peng5 pai5
sa*-tui3; chi2-u7 chiau2 bo5 phoa3-khui. 11). U7 eng-chiau2 loh8--lai5
ti7 si2 e5 cheng-si* e5 teng2-bin7; A-pek-lan5 chiu7 koa*2 i khi3. 12).
Jit8 beh loh8 e5 si5, A-pek-lan5 khun3 tang7-bin5; hut-jian5 u7 chin
oo-am3 e5 toa7 kia*-hia*5 kau3 ti7 i. 13). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lan5
kong2, Li2 tek-khak tioh8 chai, li2 e5 hoo7-e3 beh chhut-goa7 ti7
pat8-lang5 e5 toe7, koh hok8-sai7 hit-ui7 e5 lang5; hit-ui7 e5 lang5 beh
khoo2-chhoo2 in si3-pah ni5. 14). In soo2 beh hok8-sai7 e5 kok, Goa2 beh
pan7 in; au7-lai5 in beh toa3 choe7-choe7 chai5-but8 tui3-hia
chhut-lai5. 15). Li2 beh an-jian5 to3-choo2, chiah8 tng5-he3-siu7, hoo7
lang5 bai5-chong3. 16). Kau3 te7-si3 tai7, in beh to3--lai5 chia; in-ui7
A-moo5-li7 chok8 e5 choe7 iau2-be7 koan3-boan2. 17). Jit8-loh8 thi*-am3,
u7 chhut ian e5 loo5, kap teh-toh8 e5 he2-pe2, tui3 hiah e5 phoa3-peng5
e5 bah keng-ke3. 18). Tng hit-jit8 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap A-pek-lan5 lip8-iok,
kong2 Goa2 u7 chiong chit e5 toe7, tui3 Ai-kip8 ho5 kau3 hit e5
toa7-ho5, chiu7-si7 Pek-lat ho5, hoo7 li2 e5 hoo7-e3; 19). chiu7-si7
Ki-ni5, Ki-ni5-se2, Kah-moo5-ni5, Hek, Pi2-li7-se2, Li2-hoat8-im,
A-moo5-li7, Ka-lam5, Kek-ka-sat, Ia5-poo3-su, chiah e5 chok8 e5 toe7.


[16] A-pek-lan5 e5 boo2 Sat-lai7 bo5 ka7 i si*-kia*2; i u7 chit8 e5
lu2-pi7 mia5 Ha7-kah; si7 Ai-kip8 lang5. 2). Sat-lai7 ka7 A-pek-lan5
kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa kim3 goa2 si*-kia*2; chhia*2 li2 kap goa2 e5 lu2-pi7
tang5-pang5; kiam2-chhai2 goa2 thang tui3 i tit-tioh8 gin2-a2.
A-pek-lan5 thia*-than3 Sat-lai7 e5 oe7. 3). Tui3 hit-tiap8 A-pek-lan5 e5
boo2 Sat-lai7 chiong i e5 lu2-pi7 Ai-kip8 lang5 Ha7-kah hoo7 i tiong7-hu
A-pek-lan5 choe3-boo2; hit-si5 A-pek-lan5 i2-keng toa3 Ka-lam5 chap8
ni5. 4). I kap Ha7-kah tang5-pang5, Ha7-kah chiu7 hoai5-in7; i chai
ka-ki7 u7-sin, chiu7 khoa*3-khin chu2-bu2. 5). Sat-lai7 ka7 A-pek-lan5
kong2, Goa2 e5 oan-ong2 kui ti7 li2; goa2 chiong goa2 e5 lu2-pi7 he7 ti7
li2 e5 sim-hoai5-tiong; i khoa*3 ka-ki7 u7-sin, chiu7 khoa*3-khin goa2;
goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan phoa*3-toan3. 6). A-pek-lan5
tui3 Sat-lai7 kong2, Li2 e5 lu2-pi7 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, li2 thang sui5-i3
khoan2-thai7 i. Sat-lai7 khoo2-chhoo2 i, i chiu7 tui3 Sat-lai7 e5
bin7-cheng5 to5-chau2. 7). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 tu2-tioh8 i ti7
khong3-ia2 e5 chui2-choa*5-pi*; hit e5 chui2-choa*5 ti7 Su-ji*2 e5
loo7-chiu*7. 8). Tui3 i kong2, Sat-lai7 e5 lu2-pi7 Ha7-kah, li2 tui3
tah-loh8 lai5? beh tah-loh8 khi3? I kong2, Goa2 tui3 goa2 e5 chu2-bu2
Sat-lai7 e5 bin7-cheng5 chau2--chhut-lai5. 9). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2
tui3 i kong2, Li2 to3--khi3 li2 e5 chu2-bu2 hia, hang5-hok8 ti7 i e5
chhiu2-e7. 10). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 koh tui3 i kong2, Goa2 beh hoo7
li2 e5 hoo7-e3 kek8-ki5 choe7, sim7-chi3 boe7-sng3--tit. 11).
Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 koh tui3 i kong2, Li2 ta* hoai5-in7, beh si*
chit8 e5 kia*2, tioh8 ka7 i ho7 mia5 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa
thia*-ki*3 li2 e5 khoo2-cheng5. 12). I choe3 lang5 beh chhin-chhiu*7
ia2-lu5, i e5 chhiu2 beh kong-kek cheng3-lang5, cheng3-lang5 e5 chhiu2
beh kong-kek i; i beh khia7-khi2 ti7 cheng3 hia*-ti7 e5 thau5-cheng5.
18). Ha7-kah chiu7 chheng hit e5 tui3 i kong2 oe7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5
kong2, Li2 si7 khoa*3-ki*3 tak8-hang7 e5 Siong7-te3; in-ui7 kong2, Lian5
ti7-chia goa2 iah8 khoa*3-ki*3 hit e5 khoa*3-ki*3 goa2 e5 mah? 14).
Soo2-i2 chit e5 chi*2 mia5-kio3 Pi2-ji*2-lah8-hai2-lai5, chiu7-si7
Ka-te-su kap Pa-liat8 e5 tiong-kan. 15). Au7-lai5 Ha7-kah ka7 A-pek-lan5
si* chit8 e5 kia*2; A-pek-lan5 ka7 i e5 kia*2 ho7 mia5 kio3
I2-sit8-ma2-li7, chiu7-si7 Ha7-kah soo2 si*--e5. 16). Ha7-kah ka7
A-pek-lan5 si* I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 si5, A-pek-lan5 poeh-chap8-lak8 he3.


[17] A-pek-lan5 kau2-chap8-kau2 he3 e5 si5, Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 A-pek-lan5
hian2-hian7, ka7 i kong2, Goa2 si7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3, li2 ti7
Goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5 kia*5-choe3 tioh8 oan5-choan5. 2). Goa2 beh kap li2
lip8 Goa2 e5 iok, hoo7 li2 e5 hoo7-e3 kek8-ki5 choe7. 3). A-pek-lan5
chiu7 phak-loh8 ti7 toe7--nih; Siong7-te3 koh kap i kong2-oe7, kong2,
4). Goa2 kap li2 lip8 Goa2 e5 iok, li2 beh choe3 choe7-choe7 kok e5 pe7.
5). Tui3 ta* i2-au7, li2 e5 mia5 bo5 koh kio3-choe3 A-pek-lan5, si7 beh
kio3-choe3 A-pek-lah8-han2, in-ui7 Goa2 i2-keng lip8 li2 choe3
choe7-choe7 kok e5 pe7. 6). Goa2 beh hoo7 li2 e5 hoo7-e3 kek8-ki5 choe7,
kok-too7 tui3 li2 lai5 lip8, kun-ong5 tui3 li2 lai5 chhut. 7). Goa2 beh
kap li2, i2-kip8 li2 lek8-tai7 e5 hoo7-e3, siat-lip8 Goa2 e5 iok choe3
eng2-oan2 e5 iok; si7 beh choe3 li2 kap li2 e5 hoo7-e3 e5 Siong7-te3.
8). Goa2 beh chiong li2 hian7-chai7 chhut-goa7 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7
Ka-lam5 choan5-toe7, siu*2-su3 li2 kap li2 e5 hoo7-e3, choe3 eng2-oan2
e5 giap8; Goa2 iah8 beh choe3 in e5 Siong7-te3. 9). Siong7-te3 koh tui3
A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Li2 kap li2 e5 hoo7-e3 tioh8 lek8-tai7 chun-siu2
Goa2 e5 iok. 10). Lin2 tiong-kan soo2 u7 e5 ta-poo--e5, long2 tioh8 siu7
kat-le2; che chiu7-si7 Goa2 kap li2 i2-kip8 li2 e5 hoo7-e3 soo2 lip8 e5
iok, si7 lin2 soo2 tioh8 chun-siu2--e5. 11). Lin2 tioh8 koah lin2
iong5-but8 e5 phe5; che si7 beh choe3 Goa2 kap lin2 soo2 lip8 e5 iok e5
ki3-ho7. 12). Lin2 lek8-tai7 e5 ta-poo--e5, bo5-lun7 ke-lai7 si*--e5,
a2-si7 li2 e5 hoo7-e3 i2-goa7, eng7 gun5 tui3 goa7-bin7 lang5 boe2--e5,
i2-keng chhut-si3 poeh-jit8, long2 tioh8 siu7 kat-le2. 13). Li2 ke-lai7
si*--e5, kap li2 eng7 gun5 boe2--e5, long2 tek-khak tioh8 siu7 kat-le2;
an2-ni Goa2 e5 iok beh he7 ti7 lin2 e5 sin-chiu*7, choe3 eng2-oan2 e5
iok. 14). Bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 ta-poo--e5, i sin-khu ki3-jian5 bo5 siu7
kat-le2, si7 poe7 Goa2 e5 iok; tek-khak tui3 peh-si*3 e5 tiong-kan
tu5--khi3.

15). Siong7-te3 koh tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Li2 e5 boo2 Sat-lai7,
m7-thang koh kio3 i e5 mia5 Sat-lai7; i e5 mia5 beh kio3-choe3 Sat-lah8.
16). Goa2 beh su3-hok i, goa2 iah8 beh hoo7 li2 tui3 i tit-tioh8 chit8
e5 kia*2; Goa2 beh su3-hok i, i iah8 beh choe3 liat8-kok e5 lau7-bu2;
beh u7 pang-kok e5 ong5 tui3 i chhut. 17). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiu7
phak--teh chhio3, sim-lai7 kong2, Chit8-pah he3 e5 lang5 iau2 oe7
si*-kia*2 mah? Sat-lah8 i2-keng kau2-chap8 he3, iau2 oe7 seng-iong2 mah?
18). A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3 Siong7-te3 kong2, Tan7 goan7 I2-sit8-ma2-li7
oah8 ti7 Li2 e5 bin7-cheng5. 19). Siong7-te3 kong2, M7-si7 lah, li2 e5
boo2 Sat-lah8 beh ka7 li2 si* chit8 e5 kia*2, li2 beh ka7 i ho7-mia5
kio3 I2-sat; Goa2 beh kap i siat-lip8 Goa2 e5 iok, choe3 i e5 hoo7-e3
eng2-oan2 e5 iok. 20). Lun7-kau3 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, Goa2 iah8 thia* li2
kiu5; li2 khoa*3, Goa2 i2-keng su3-hok i, beh hoo7 i heng-ong7, ke-thi*
kek8-ki5 choe7. I beh si* chap8-ji7 e5 chok8-tiu*2, Goa2 iah8 beh hoo7 i
chia*5-choe3 toa7-kok. 21). Kau3 me5-ni5 chit-si5, Sat-lah8 beh ka7 li2
si* I2-sat; Goa2 beh kap i siat-lip8 Goa2 e5 iok. 22). Siong7-te3 kap
A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2 soah, chiu7 li7-khui i chiu*7--khi3. 23). Tu2-tu2
hit-jit8, A-pek-lah8-han2 chiau3 Siong7-te3 soo2 ka7 i kong2--e5, ka7 i
e5 kia*2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7, kap A-pek-lah8-han2 ke-lai7 it-chhe3 e5
ta-poo-lang5, bo5-lun7 ti7 ke--nih si*--e5, a2-si7 eng7 i e5 gun5
boe2--e5 long2 kia*5 kat-le2. 24). A-pek-lah8-han2 siu7 kat-le2 e5 si5
kau2-chap8-kau2 he3; 25). i e5 kia*2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 siu7 kat-le2 e5 si5
chap8-sa* he3. 26). Tu2-tu2 hit jit8 A-pek-lah8-han2 kap i e5 kia*2
I2-sit8-ma2-li7 tang5 siu7 kat-le2. 27). Ke-lai7 soo2-u7 e5 lang5,
bo5-lun7 ti7 ke--nih si*--e5, a2-si7 eng7 gun5 tui3 goa7-bin7 lang5
boe2--e5, long2 kap i tang5 siu7 kat-le2.


[18] Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 Ban7-li7 e5 siong7-chhiu7 hia, tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2
chhut-hian7; hit-si5 jit8 tng joah8; A-pek-lah8-han2 che7 ti7 poo3-pi*5
mng5-khau2; 2). kiah8-bak8 khi2-lai5 khoa*3, khoa*3-ki*3 sa* lang5 ti7
tui3-bin7 teh khia7; i chit8-e7 khoa*3-ki*3, chiu7 tui3 poo3-pi*5
mng5-khau2, chau2 khi3 ngia5-chih in, phak ti7 toe7--nih, kong2, goa2 e5
chu2, goa2 na7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, kiu5 li2
m7-thang li7-khui loo5-pok8 choe3 li2 khi3; 4). iong5-un2 theh8
tam7-poh8 chui2, hoo7 lin2 soe2-kha; chhia*2 hioh-khun3 ti7 chhiu7-kha;
5). goa2 koh theh8 tam7-poh8 pia*2, hoo7 lin2 tiam2-sim; jian5-au7
chin3-cheng5 khi3; in-ui7 lin2 si7 ui7-tioh8 an2-ni, chiah kau3 lin2 e5
loo5-pok8 chia. In kong2, Thang chiau3 li2 e5 oe7 khi3 kia*5. 6).
A-pek-lah8-han2 koa*2-kin2 jip8 poo3-pi*5, ki*3 Sat-lah8 kong2, Li2
kin2-kin2 eng7 sa* se3-a e5 mi7-hun2, noa2 choe3 pia*2. 7).
A-pek-lah8-han2 koh chau2 kau3 gu5-kun5 e5 soo2-chai7, khan chit8 chiah
chi*2 koh ho2 e5 gu5-a2 lai5; kau hoo7 loo5-pok8, i chiu7 koa*2-kin2
khi3 pi7-pan7. 8). A-pek-lah8-han2 koh theh8 lin-iu5 kap lin, kap soo2
pi7-pan7 e5 gu5-a2 lai5, pai5 ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5; ka-ki7 ti7
chhiu7-kha khia7 ti7 in e5 sin-pi*; in chiu7 chiah8. 9). In ka7 i kong2,
Li2 e5 boo2 Sat-lah8 ti7 tah-loh8? I kong2, Ti7 poo3-pi*5-lai7. 10). In
tiong-kan chit8-e5 kong2, Kau3-ki5 Goa2 tek-khak beh koh lai5 li2 chia;
li2 e5 boo2 Sat-lah8 beh si* chit8 e5 kia*2. Sat-lah8 ti7 au7-bin7,
poo3-pi*5 mng5-khau2, teh thia*. 11). A-pek-lah8-han2 kap Sat-lah8
ni5-he3 i2-keng lau7; Sat-lah8 e5 geh8-keng i2-keng choat8. 12).
Sat-lah8 sim-lai7 chhio3 kong2, Goa2 i2-keng soe-lam2, goa2 e5 chu2 iah8
lau7--lah; kiam2 iau2 u7 chit-ho7 e5 hoa*-hi2? 13). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3
A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Sat-lah8 ui7 sia*2-su7 chhio3, kong2, Goa2
i2-keng lau7, ko2-chin oe7 si*-kia*2 mah? 14). Kiam2 Ia5-ho5-hoa u7
choe3-boe7-lai5 e5 su7 mah? Kau3-ki5, me5-ni5 chit-si5, Goa2 beh koh
lai5 li2 chia, Sat-lah8 beh si* chit8 e5 kia*2. 15). Sat-lah8 kia*,
m7-jin7, kong2, Goa2 bo5 chhio3. Hit-lang5 kong2, Bo5-ia*2; li2
sit8-chai7 u7 chhio3.

16). Hiah e5 lang5 chiu7 tui3 hia khi2--lai5, ng3 Soo2-to-ma2 khi3;
A-pek-lah8-han2 ia7 kap in sa*-kap kia*5, beh sang3 in chit8-cham7. 17).
Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 soo2 beh choe3 e5 su7, kiam2 thang tui3
A-pek-lah8-han2 un2-khng3 mah? 18). In-ui7 A-pek-lah8-han2 tek-khak beh
chia*5-choe3 kiong5-toa7 e5 kok, toe7-chiu*7 ban7-kok beh in-ui7 i lai5
tit-tioh8 hok-khi3. 19). Goa2 bat i, si7 beh hoo7 i beng7-leng7 i e5
kia*2 kap i e5 ke-koan3; hoo7 in tng5-tng5 siu2 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 to7-li2,
peng2-kong kia*5-gi7; ti3-kau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa chi2 A-pek-lah8-han2 soo2
kong2 e5 oe7, long2 kui hoo7 i. 20). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Soo2-to-ma2,
Go5-moo5-lah8 hoah-hiam3 e5 sia* chin-toa7, in e5 choe7-ok sit8-chai7
tang7. 21). Goa2 ta* beh loh8--khi3, khoa*3 in soo2 kia*5--e5, ko2-jian5
it-chin7 chiau3 Goa2 soo2 thia* e5 sia* a2 bo5; na7 bo5 an2-ni, Goa2
iah8 oe7 chai.

22). Hiah e5 lang5 tui3-hia oat8-tng2-sin, ng3 Soo2-to-ma2 khi3;
A-pek-lah8-han2 iau2 khia7 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5. 23).
A-pek-lah8-han2 kun7-cheng5 lai5 kong2, Ho2-lang5 kap phai*2-lang5, Li2
long2 beh chau5-biat8 mah? 24). Siat-su2 sia*5-lai7 u7 goo7-chap8 e5
ho2-lang5, Li2 iu5-gôan beh chau5-biat8 hit soo2-chai7 mah? bo5-beh
ui7-tioh8 sia*5-lai7 chi2 goo7-chap8 e5 ho2-lang5, lai5 sia3-bian2 in
mah? 25). Goan7 Li2 koat-toan3 bo5 an2-ni kia*5, chiong ho2-lang5 kap
phai*2-lang5 choe3-chit8-e7 hai7-si2; ti3-kau3 ho2-lang5 kap
phai*2-lang5 sa*-tang5; goan7 Li2 koat-toan3 bo5 an2-ni kia*5;
sim2-phoa*3 choan5-toe7 e5 Chu2 kiam2 bo5 kia*5 kong-gi7 mah? 26).
Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Goa2 na7 ti7 Soo2-to-ma2 sia*5-lai7 tu2-tioh8 u7
goo7-chap8 e5 ho2-lang5, Goa2 chiu7 ui7-tioh8 in e5 ian5-koo3
khoan-iong5 hit soo2-chai7. 27). A-pek-lah8-han2 in3 kong2, Goa2
sui-jian5 si7 he2-hu thoo5-hun2, iau2-ku2 ka*2 tui3 Chu2 kong2-oe7;
siat-su2 chiah e5 goo7-chap8 e5 ho2-lang5 khiam3 goo7-e5; Li2 chiu7
in-ui7 khiam3 goo7-e5, chau5-biat8 choan5-sia*5 mah? I kong2, Goa2
ti7-hia na7 tu2-tioh8 u7 si3-chap8-goo7 e5, iah8 bo5 beh chau5-biat8.
29). A-pek-lah8-han2 koh tui3 I kong2, Siat-su2 ti7-hia tu2-tioh8
si3-chap8-e5--nih? I kong2, Ui7-tioh8 chiah e5 si3-chap8-e5 e5
ian5-koo3, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh choe3 chit e5 su7. 30). I koh kong2, Kiu5
Chu2 boh8-tit siu7-khi3, goa2 beh koh kong2; siat-su2 ti7-hia na7
tu2-tioh8 sa*-chap8-e5--nih? I kong2, Goa2 ti7-hia na7 tu2-tioh8 u7
sa*-chap8-e5, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh choe3 chit e5 su7. 31). I kong2, Goa2
iau2-ku2 ka*2 tui3 Chu2 kong2; siat-su2 ti7-hia tu2-tioh8 u7
ji7-chap8-e5--nih? I kong2, Ui7-tioh8 chiah e5 ji7-chap8-e5 e5
ian5-koo3, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh chau5-biat8. 32). I kong2, Kiu5 Chu2
boh8-tit siu7-khi3, goa2 koh kong2 chi2 chit8-pai2; siat-su2 ti7-hia
tu2-tioh8 u7 chap8-e5--nih? I kong2, Ui7-tioh8 chiah e5 chap8-e5 e5
ian5-koo3, Goa2 iah8 bo5 beh chau5-biat8. 33). Ia5-ho5-hoa kap
A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2 beng5-pek8, chiu7 chiu*7--khi3. A-pek-lah8-han2
iah8 to3-khi3 i e5 soo2-chai7.


[19] Jit8-am3, hit nng7 e5 su3-chia2 kau3 Soo2-to-ma2; Lo5-tek che7 ti7
Soo2-to-ma2 sia*5-mng5--nih; Lo5-tek khoa*3-ki*3 in, chiu7 khi2-lai5
ngia5-chih in; kiok-kiong bin7 ng3 toe7, kong2, 2). Goa2 e5 chu2 ah,
chhia*2 oat lai5 loo5-pok8 e5 chhu3 hioh-mi5, soe2-kha;
bin5-a2-cha2-khi2 khi2-lai5, kia*5 lin2 e5 loo7. In kong2, M7-bian2;
goan2 beh ti7 toa7 koe-bin7 ke3-mi5. 3). Lo5-tek chhiat-chhiat chhia*2
in; in chiah oat8-tng2-kha, oat-jip8 i e5 chhu3; Lo5-tek ui7 in pi7-pan7
ian5-siah8, pek bu5-ka*3-pia*2; in chiu7 chiah8. 4). In iau2-be7 khi3
khun3, sia*5-lai7 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 Soo2-to-ma2 lang5, tui3
siau3-lian5 kau3 lau7, si3-bin7 lai5 ui5 i e5 chhu3; 5). kio3 Lo5-tek
kong2, Kin-am3 kau3 li2 chia e5 lang5 ti7 tah-loh8? hoo7 in chhut-lai5,
chiau3 goan2 soo2 ai3 choe3. 6). Lo5-tek chhut-khi3 kau3 mng5-goa7,
cheng3-lang5 hia, chiu7 chiong mng5 koai*--teh; 7). kong2, Hia*-ti7 ah,
chhia*2 lin2 boh8-tit choe3 chit-ho7 phai*2; li2 khoa*3, goa2 u7 nng7 e5
cha-boo2-kia*2, iau2 si7 chai7-sek-lu2; iong5-un2 goa2
chhoa7--chhut-lai5, chhut-chai7 lin2 soo2 ai3 lai5 kia*5; tok8-tok8 chi2
nng7-lang5, i2-keng kau3 goa2 e5 chhu3, m7-thang tui3 in choe3
sim2-mih8. 9). Cheng3-lang5 kong2, Li2 the3--khi3. Koh kong2, Chit-lang5
kia3-ku ti7-chia, soa3 beh koan2-hat goan2 mah? ta* goan2 beh hai7 li2
pi2 hai7 in khah siong-tiong7. Chiu7 oe-khoeh Lo5-tek, chin3-cheng5 beh
kong-phoa3 i e5 mng5. 10). Chong2-si7 hit nng7-lang5 chhun-chhiu2 khan
Lo5-tek jip8 chhu3, chiong mng5 koai*--khi3. 11). Koh hoo7 nng7-goa7 e5
lang5, tui3 soe3 kau3 toa7, bak8-chiu ian-ng7, long2 boe7 khoa*3-ki*3;
chhe7 kau3 sian7 chhe7 bo5 mng5.

12). Hit nng7-lang5 tui3 Lo5-tek kong2, Li2 ti7-chia iau2 u7 sim2-mih8
lang5? hek8-si7 kia*2-sai3, hek8-si7 kia*2, hek8-si7 cha-boo2-kia*2,
i2-kip8 sia*5-lai7 it-chhe3 siok8 li2 e5 lang5; li2 tioh8 hoo7 in long2
chhut chit soo2-chai7. 13). In-ui7 goan2 beh chau5-biat8 chit e5
soo2-chai7, si7 ui7-tioh8 in hoah-hiam3 e5 sia* ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5
bin7-cheng5 chin-toa7; Ia5-ho5-hoa chhe goan2 lai5 beh chau5-biat8--i.
14). Lo5-tek chhut-khi3, tui3 chhoa7 i e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 e5 kia*2-sai3
kong2, Lin2 khi2-lai5, li7-khui chia; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh biat8-bo5
chit e5 sia*5; i e5 kia*2-sai3 liah8-choe3 i si7 kong2-chhio3. 15).
Thi*-kng su3-chia2 chhui-pek Lo5-tek kong2, Khi2--lai5, chhoa7 li2 e5
boo2, i2-kip8 li2 ti7-chia nng7 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 khi3; kia*-liau2 kap
chit e5 sia*5 e5 choe7-ok sa*-kap siu7 biat8-bo5. 16). Lo5-tek
ian5-chhian5; hit nng7-lang5, in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa lin5-bin2 Lo5-tek,
chiu7 khan i e5 chhiu2, kap i e5 boo2 e5 chhiu2, kap i nng7 e5
cha-boo2-kia*2 e5 chhiu2, chiong i chhoa7-chhut, an-ti3 ti7 sia*5-goa7.

17). Chhoa7 in chhut-khi3 liau2, kong2, Li2 tioh8 to5-mia7, m7-thang
oat8-thau5 khoa*3, iah8 m7-thang toa3 ti7 Pi*5-iu*5; tioh8 chau2--khi3
soa*--nih, kia*-liau2 siu7 biat8-bo5. 18). Lo5-tek tui3 in kong2, Goa2
e5 chu2 ah, m7-thang an2-ni. 19). Li2 khoa*3, li2 e5 loo5-pok8 i2-keng
tit-tioh8 un-tian2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, li2 iah8 tui3 goa2
hian2-chhut kek8-toa7 e5 jin5-chu5, kiu3 goa2 e5 si*3-mia7; goa2
boe7-oe7 chau2 kau3 soa*--nih, kia*-liau2 chit e5 chai-e7 kau3 ti7 goa2,
goa2 chiu7 si2. 20). Li2 khoa*3, chit e5 sia*5 kun7-kun7 thang
to5-chau2, iah8 si7 soe3; chhia*2 iong5-un2 goa2 to5-siam2 ti7-hia, lai5
po2-choan5 goa2 e5 oah8-mia7; chit e5 sia*5 kiam2 m7-si7 soe3--e5 mah?
21). I tui3 i kong2, Chit e5 tai7-chi3, goa2 iah8 un2-chun2 li2; li2
soo2 kong2 e5 sia*5, goa2 bo5 beh chhia-to2. 22). Li2 tioh8 kin2-kin2
chau2-khi3 hia; in-ui7 li2 iau2-be7 kau3 hia, goa2 boe7-oe7 choe3
sim2-mih8. In-ui7 an2-ni hit e5 sia*5 mia5-kio3 So2-ji*2. 23). Lo5-tek
kau3 So2-ji*2, jit8 i2-keng chhut. 24). Hit si5 Ia5-ho5-hoa chiong
jiu5-ng5 kap he2, tui3 thi*-teng2, tui3 Ia5-ho5-hoa hia, kang3-loh8 ti7
Soo2-to-ma2 kap Go5-moo5-lah8. 25). Chiong hiah e5 sia*5, i2-kip8 choan5
Pi5-iu*5, kap sia*5-lai7 soo2-u7 e5 peh-si*3, lian5 toe7-bin7-chiu*7
seng-tiong2--e5, long2 hui2-hoai7. 26). Lo5-tek e5 boo2 ti7 au7-bin7,
chit8-e7 oat8-thau5 khoa*3, chiu7 pi*3-choe3 chit8 ki iam5-thiau7. 27).
A-pek-lah8-han2 thau3-cha2 khi2--lai5, kau3 i cheng5-jit8 khia7 ti7
Ia5-ho5-hoa bin7-cheng5 hit-ui7; 28). ng3 Soo2-to-ma2 Go5-moo5-lah8, kap
Pi*5-iu*5 e5 choan5-toe7 lai5 khoa*3; khoa*3-ki*3 hit soo2-chai7 he2-ian
chheng3-koai*5, chhin-chhiu*7 he2-loo5 e5 ian.

29). Tng Siong7-te3 chau5-biat8 Pi*5-iu*5 chiah e5 sia*5 e5 si5,
Siong7-te3 siau3-liam7 A-pek-lah8-han2; tu2-tu2 ti7 chhia-to2 Lo5-tek
soo2 khia7-khi2 e5 sia*5 e5 si5, chiu7 kah Lo5-tek tui3 chhia-to2 e5
tiong-kan chhut-khi3.

30). Lo5-tek tiam3 ti7 So2-ji*2 kia*-hia*5; chiu7 kap i nng7 e5
cha-boo2-kia*2 tui3 So2-ji*2 chiu*7--khi3 tiam3 ti7 soa*--nih; i kap
nng7 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 tiam3 ti7 chit8 e5 tong7-lai7. 31). Toa7
cha-boo2-kia*2 tui3 soe3 cha-boo2-kia*2 kong2, Lan2 e5 lau7-pe7
lau7--lah, toe7-chiu*7 koh bo5 lang5 kap lan2 choe3 phit-phoe3, lai5
chiau3 jin5-to7. 32). Lai5--lah, thang hoo7 lau7-pe7 lim chiu2, kap i
sa*-kap khun3; an2-ni lan2 ho2 thang tui3 i liu5-chun5 hoo7-e3. 33).
Hit-mi5 in hoo7 lau7-pe7 lim chiu2; toa7 cha-boo2-kia*2 chiu7 jip8--khi3
kap lau7-pe7 sa*-kap khun3; i sim2-mih8 si5 khi3 khun3, sim2-mih8 si5
khi2--lai5, lau7-pe7 long2 m7-chai. 34). Ke3-jit8 toa7 cha-boo2-kia*2
ka7 soe3 cha-boo2-kia*2 kong2, Goa2 cha7-mi5 kap lau7-pe7 sa*-kap khun3;
kin-am3 lan2 koh hoo7 i lim chiu2, li2 thang jip8--khi3 kap i sa*-kap
khun3. An2-ni, lan2 ho2 thang tui3 lau7-pe7 liu5-chun5 hoo7-e3. 35).
Hit-mi5 in koh hoo7 lau7-pe7 lim chiu2, soe3 cha-boo2-kia*2 khi2--lai5
khi3 kap i khun3; i sim2-mih8 si5 khi3 khun3, sim2-mih8 si5 khi2--lai5,
lau7-pe7 iah8 long2 m7-chai. 36). An2-ni Lo5-tek nng7 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2
long2 tui3 in lau7-pe7 lai5 hoai5-in7. 37). Toa7--e5 si* kia*2, kio3 i
e5 mia5 Moo5-ap, chiu7-si7 hian7-kim Moo5-ap lang5 e5 choo2. 38).
Soe3--e5 iah8 si*-kia*2, kio3 i e5 mia5 Pian7-a2-bi2, chiu7-si7
hian7-kim A-bun5 lang5 e5 choo2.


[20] A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3-hia cham7-cham7 ng3 lam5-hng soa3-khi3; toa3
ti7 Ka-te-su kap Su-ji*2 e5 tiong-kan, kia3-ku ti7 Ki-lah8-ji*2. 2).
A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2 kau3 i e5 boo2 Sat-lah8, chiu7 kong2, Si7 goa2 e5
sio2-be7; Ki-lah8-ji*2 ong5 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 chhe lang5 chiong Sat-lah8
chhoa7--khi3. 3). Mi5-si5, bin5-bang7-tiong, Siong7-te3 lai5 ka7
A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kong2, Li2 si7 kai si2 e5 lang5, in-ui7 li2 soo2 chhoa7
hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 si7 lang5 e5 boo2. 4). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 iau2-be7
chhin-kun7 i, chiu7 kong2, Chu2 ah, kia*5-gi7 e5 peh-si*3, Li2 iah8 beh
biat8 i mah? 5). Hit-lang5 kiam2 m7-si7 pun2-sin tui3 goa2 kong2, I si7
goa2 e5 sio2-be7 mah? Chiu7 hu7-jin5-lang5 iah8 pun2-sin kong2, I si7
goa2 e5 hia*; goa2 choe3 chit e5 su7, si7 sim toan-cheng3, chhiu2
chheng-khi3. 6). Siong7-te3 ti7 bang7-tiong tui3 i kong2, Goa2 pun2 chai
li2 choe3 chit e5 su7, si7 sim-tiong toan-cheng3; Goa2 chiah choo2-tong3
li2, bian2-tit li2 tek-choe7 Goa2; soo2-i2 Goa2 bo5 iong5-un2 li2
bong--tioh8 i. 7). Ta* li2 tioh8 chiong chit lang5 e5 boo2 heng5--i,
in-ui7 i si7 sian-ti; i beh thoe3 li2 ki5-to2, li2 chiah oe7 oah8; li2
na7 m7 heng5--i, li2 tioh8 chai, li2 kap li2 soo2 u7 e5 lang5 long2
tit-beh si2. 8). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 thau3-cha2 khi2-lai5, kio3 cheng3
loo5-pok8 lai5, chiong chiah e5 tai7-chi3 long2 kong2 hoo7 in thia*;
hiah e5 lang5 long2 chin kia*. 9). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kio3 A-pek-lah8-han2
lai5, tui3 i kong2, Li2 tui3 goan2 soo2 kia*5--e5 si7 sim2-mih8 su7?
goa2 u7 sim2-mih8 tek-choe7 li2, li2 keng2-jian5 hoo7 goa2 kap goa2
kok-lai7 e5 lang5 ham7-loh8 tang7-choe7? li2 tui3 goa2 kia*5 m7 eng-kai
kia*5 e5 su7. 10). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 koh tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Li2
khoa*3-ki*3 sim2-mih8, chiah choe3 chit e5 su7? 11). A-pek-lah8-han2
kong2, Goa2 phah-sng3 chit soo2-chai7 e5 lang5 long2 bo5 kia*
Siong7-te3; in beh ui7-tioh8 goa2 e5 boo2 e5 ian5-koo3 thai5-si2 goa2.
12). Koh i iah8 sit8-chai7 si7 goa2 e5 sio2-be7, siang5-pe7 koh-bu2,
au7-lai5 choe3 goa2 e5 boo2. 13). Tng Siong7-te3 kah goa2 li7-khui
lau7-pe7 e5 ke, si3-koe3 kia*5 e5 si5, goa2 ka7 i kong2, chiong-lai5
lan2 soo2 kau3 e5 soo2-chai7, chhia*2 li2 chheng goa2 kong2, I si7 goa2
e5 hia*; che chiu7-si7 li2 khoan2-thai7 goa2 e5 un. 14). A-pi2-bi2-lek8
chiong iu*5, gu5, loo5-pok8, lu2-pi7, hoo7 A-pek-lah8-han2; koh chiong i
e5 boo2 Sat-lah8 heng5--i. 15). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 koh kong2, Li2 khoa*3,
goa2 e5 toe7 long2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, li2 thang sui5-i3 khia7-khi2.
16). Koh ka7 Sat-lah8 kong2, Goa2 hoo7 li2 e5 hia* chit8 chheng gun5,
ka7 li2 tui3 choan5-ke choe3 jia bak8-chiu--e5; ta* li2 ti7 it-chhe3
long2 bo5 put-si7. 17). A-pek-lah8-han2 ki5-to2 Siong7-te3; Siong7-te3
chiu7 i-ho2 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kap i e5 boo2 kap lu2-pi7, in chiu7 oe7 si*
kia*2. 18). In-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ui7-tioh8 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 boo2
Sat-lah8 e5 ian5-koo3, i2-keng hoo7 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 ke-lai7 e5
hu7-jin5-lang5 boe7-oe7 si*-kia*2.


[21] Ia5-ho5-hoa chiau3 I cheng5 e5 oe7 koan3-koo3 Sat-lah8; tui3 an2-ni
Ia5-ho5-hoa chiau3 I soo2 kong2--e5 ka7 Sat-lah8 choe3-chia*5. 2).
A-pek-lah8-han2 ni5-lau7 e5 si5, Sat-lah8 hoai5-in7; kau3 Siong7-te3
tui3 i kong2 e5 jit8-ki5, chiu7 ka7 i si* chit8 e5 kia*2. 3).
A-pek-lah8-han2 ka7 Sat-lah8 soo2 si* e5 kia*2, ho7 mia5 kio3 I2-sat.
4). I2-sat chhut-si3 poeh-jit8, A-pek-lah8-han2 chiau3 Siong7-te3 soo2
hoan-hu3-e5, ka7 i e5 kia*2 kia*5 kat-le2. 5). I e5 kia*2 I2-sat
chhut-si3 e5 si5, A-pek-lah8-han2 chit8-pah he3. 6). Sat-lah8 kong2,
Siong7-te3 hoo7 goa2 hoa*-hi2 chhio3; ki*3-na7 thia*-ki*3--e5, beh kap
goa2 tang5 hoa*-hi2 chhio3. 7). Koh kong2, Chi7-chui7 oe7 tai7-seng ka7
A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Sat-lah8 beh hoo7 e*-a2 suh-leng? in-ui7 ti7 i
ni5-lau7 e5 si5, goa2 ka7 i si* chit8 e5 kia*2.

8). Gin2-a2 chiam7-chiam7 toa7, chiu7 tng7-leng; I2-sat tng7-leng e5
jit8, A-pek-lah8-han2 pai5-siat toa7 ian5-siah8. 9). Tng-si5 Ai-kip8
lang5 Ha7-kah ka7 A-pek-lah8-han2 soo2 si* e5 kia*2 teh leng2-chhio3,
hoo7 Sat-lah8 khoa*3-ki*3; 10). chiu7 tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Tioh8
koa*2-chhut chit e5 lu2-pi7 kap i e5 kia*2; in-ui7 lu2-pi7 e5 kia*2
boe7-thang kap goa2 e5 kia*2 I2-sat tang5 choe3 hoo7-su5. 11).
A-pek-lah8-han2 in-ui7 i e5 kia*2 e5 ian5-koo3 put-chi2 iu-bun7. 12).
Siong7-te3 ka7 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Li2 m7-thang ui7-tioh8 chit e5
gin2-a2 i2-kip8 li2 e5 lu2-pi7 iu-bun7; ki*3-na7 Sat-lah8 tui3 li2 kong2
e5, li2 long2 tioh8 thia*; in-ui7 tui3 I2-sat si*--e5, chiah beh
chheng-choe3 li2 e5 hoo7-e3. 13). Lun7-kau3 lu2-pi7 e5 kia*2, Goa2 iah8
beh hoo7 i chia*5-choe3 chit8-kok, in-ui7 i iah8 si7 li2 si*--e5. 14).
A-pek-lah8-han2 cha2-cha2 khi2-lai5, theh8 pia*2 kap chit8 phe5-te7 e5
chui2 hoo7 Ha7-kah; he7 ti7 i e5 keng-thau5-teng2; lian5 gin2-a2 soa3
kah i khi3; i chiu7 khi3, kau3 Piat8-si7-pa e5 khong3-ia2 chiu7 kia*5
bo5 loo7. 15). Phe5-te7 lai7 e5 chui2 eng7-liau2, Ha7-kah chiu7 chiong
gin2-a2 pang3 ti7 soe3 chang5 chhiu7 kha. 16). Pun2-sin kia*5-khui,
iok-liok8 choh8 chit8 ki chi*3 e5 hng7, sa*-tui3-bin7 teh che7; kong2,
Goa2 put-jim2 khoa*3 gin2-a2 si2; chiu7 sa*-tui3-bin7 che7, chhut-sia*
toa7 thi5-khau3. 17). Siong7-te3 thia*-ki*3 gin2-a2 e5 sia*; Siong7-te3
e5 su3-chia2 tui3 thi*--nih kio3 Ha7-kah kong2, Ha7-kah, li2 u7
sim2-mih8 tai7-chi3? m7-bian2 kia*; Siong7-te3 i2-keng thia*-ki*3
gin2-a2 ti7-hia e5 sia*. 18). Khi2-lai5, iah8 hoo7 gin2-a2 khi2--lai5,
khan ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2; Goa2 beh hoo7 i chia*5-choe3 toa7-kok. 19).
Siong7-te3 khui i e5 bak8-chiu, i chiu7 khoa*3-ki*3 chui2-chi*2; chiu7
chiong phe5-te7 khi3 jip8-chui2 kau3 moa2-moa2, soa3 hoo7 gin2-a2 lim.
20). Siong7-te3 kap gin2-a2 ti7-teh, i chiu7 chiam7-chiam7 toa7; tiam3
ti7 khong3-ia2, chia*5-choe3 sia7-chi*3 e5 lang5. 21). I khia7-khi2 ti7
Pa-lan5 e5 khong3-ia2; i e5 lau7-bu2 tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7 ka7 i chhoa7
chit8 e5 boo2.

22). Tng hit-si5 A-pi2-bi2-lek8, kap i e5 kun-tiu*2 Hui-kok, tui3
A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Ki*3-na7 li2 soo2 kia*5 e5 su7, Siong7-te3 kap
li2 ti7-teh. 23). Ta* li2 ti7-chia tioh8 ki2 Siong7-te3 kap goa2
chiu3-choa7, m7-thang khi-hu7 goa2, kap goa2 e5 kia*2, i2-kip8 goa2 e5
sun; goa2 an3-chai*2-iu*7 ho2 khoan2-thai7 li2, li2 iah8 tioh8 chiau3
an2-ni khoan2-thai7 goa2, i2-kip8 li2 soo2 kia3-ku e5 toe7-hng. 24).
A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Goa2 beh chiu3-choa7. 25). Cheng5 A-pi2-bi2-lek8
e5 loo5-pok8 pa3-chiam3 chit8 khau2 chui2-chi*2, A-pek-lah8-han2 ui7
chit e5 su7 hiam5 A-pi2-bi2-lek8. 26). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kong2, Chi7-chui7
choe3 chit e5 tai7-chi3, goa2 m7-chai; li2 iah8 be7 u7 ka7 goa2 kong2,
kau3 kin-a2-jit8 goa2 chiah thia*-ki*3. 27). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong iu*5
kap gu5 hoo7 A-pi2-bi2-lek8; nng7-lang5 chiu7 sa*-kap lip8-iok. 28).
A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong chhit chiah bu2 e5 iu*5-ko leng7-goa7 pang3 ti7
chit8 soo2-chai7. 29). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 mng7 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Li2
chiong chhit chiah bu2 e5 iu*5-ko leng7-goa7 pang3 ti7 chit8 soo2-chai7,
si7 sim2-mih8 i3-su3? 30). In3 kong2, Li2 tioh8 tui3 goa2 e5 chhiu2 siu
chi2 chhit chiah bu2 e5 iu*5-ko, choe3 goa2 khui chit khau2 chi*2 e5
cheng3-ku3. 31). Soo2-i2 mia5 hit soo2-chai7 kio3 Piat8-si7-pa, in-ui7
in nng7-lang5 ti7-hia u7 chiu3-choa7.

32). In ti7 Piat8-si7-pa lip8-iok; A-pi2-bi2-lek8 chiu7 kap i e5
kun-tiu*2 Hui-kok khi2-sin to3--khi3 Hui-li7-su7 toe7. 33).
A-pek-lah8-han2 ti7 Piat8-si7-pa chai chit8 chang5 sui5-si-liu2 chhiu7;
koh ti7-hia kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa eng2-eng2 ti7-teh Siong7-te3 e5 mia5.
34). A-pek-lah8-han2 ti7 Hui-li7-su7 lang5 e5 toe7 kia3-ku choe7-choe7 jit8.


[22] Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 i2-au7, Siong7-te3 chhi3 A-pek-lah8-han2, kio3 i
kong2, A-pek-lah8-han2; i in3 kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia. 2). Siong7-te3
kong2, Li2 toa3 li2 e5 kia*2, chiu7-si7 li2 tok8-si* e5 kia*2, li2 soo2
thia*3 e5 I2-sat, khi3 Moo5-li7-a e5 toe7, Goa2 soo2 beh chi2-si7 li2 e5
soa*; ti7-hia chiong i hian3-choe3 sio-che3. 3). A-pek-lah8-han2
thau3-cha2 khi2--lai5, pi7-pan7 lu5, toa3 i e5 nng7 e5 siau3-lian5
lang5, kap i e5 kia*2 I2-sat; iah8 phoa3 sio-che3 e5 chha5; chiu7
khi2-sin khi3 Siong7-te3 soo2 chi2-si7 i e5 toe7. 4). Kau3 te7-sa* jit8,
A-pek-lah8-han2 kiah8-bak8 hng7-hng7 khoa*3 hit e5 soo2-chai7. 5).
A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3 i e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 kong2, Lin2 kap lu5 tiam3
chia theng3-hau7, goa2 kap gin2-a2 khi3 hia keng3-pai3, chiu7 to3--lai5
lin2 chia. 6). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong sio-che3 e5 chha5 he7 ti7 i e5
kia*2 I2-sat e5 sin-chiu*7, ka-ki7 e5 chhiu2 kiah8 he2 kap to; tui3
hit-tiap8 nng7-lang5 sa*-kap kia*5. 7). I2-sat ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7
A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Pe7 ah; i kong2, Goa2 e5 kia*2, goa2 ti7-chia. I
kong2, Li2 khoa*3, he2 kap chha5 long2 u7; chong2-si7 sio-che3 e5
iu*5-a2 ti7 tah-loh8? 8). A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, Goa2 e5 kia*2,
Siong7-te3 beh ka-ki7 pi7-pan7 sio-che3 e5 iu*5-a2; tui3 hit-tiap8
nng7-lang5 sa*-kap kia*5.

9). In kau3 Siong7-te3 chi2-si7 i e5 soo2-chai7; A-pek-lah8-han2 ti7-hia
khi2 toa*5, chiong chha5 pai5-ho2, pak8 i e5 kia*2 I2-sat, he7 ti7
toa*5--nih e5 chha5-teng2. 10). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiu7 chhun-chhiu2
kiah8-to, beh thai5 i e5 kia*2. 11). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 tui3 thi*
kio3 i kong2, A-pek-lah8-han2, A-pek-lah8-han2; i in3 kong2, Goa2
ti7-chia. 12). Su3-chia2 kong2, Li2 m7-thang ti7 chit e5 gin2-a2 e5
sin-chiu*7 he7-chhiu2, iah8 m7-thang tui3 i chai*2-iu*7 choe3; in-ui7
goa2 ta* chai li2 si7 keng3-ui3 Siong7-te3, iah8 bo5 chiong li2 e5
kia*2, chiu7-si7 li2 tok8-si*--e5, lau5--teh, m7-hoo7 goa2. 13).
A-pek-lah8-han2 kiah8-bak8 khoa*3, khoa*3-ki*3 au7-bin7 u7 chit8 chiah
iu*5-kang2, kak ti*5 ti7 kui-pho7 e5 chhiu7-a2; A-pek-lah8-han2 chiu7
khi3 liah8 hit chiah iu*5-kang2 lai5, hian3 choe3 sio-che3, lai5 thoe3 i
e5 kia*2. 14). A-pek-lah8-han2 mia5 hit e5 soo2-chai7 kio3
Ia5-ho5-hoa-i2-lek8; kau3 kin-a2-jit8 lang5 iau2 teh kong2, Ti7
Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 soa* beh pi7-pan7. 15). Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 su3-chia2 te7-ji7
pai2 tui3 thi* kio3 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2, 16). Ia5-ho5-hoa kong2, Li2
i2-keng kia*5 chit e5 su7, bo5 lau5 li2 e5 kia*2, chiu7-si7 li2 tok8-si*
e5 kia*2, Goa2 chiu7 ki2 ka-ki7 chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 su3-hok beh
su3-hok li2, ke-thi* beh ke-thi* li2 e5 hoo7-e3, chhin-chhiu*7
thi*-teng2 e5 chhi*, hai2-pi* e5 soa; li2 e5 hoo7-e3 beh tit-tioh8 chiah
e5 tui3-tek8 e5 koan-ai3. 18). Koh toe7-chiu*7 ban7-pang beh in-ui7 li2
e5 hoo7-e3 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3; in-ui7 li2 thia*-than3 Goa2 e5 oe7. 19).
Tui3 hit-tiap8 A-pek-lah8-han2 to3--lai5 i hiah e5 siau3-lian5 lang5
hia; in chiu7 sa*-kap khi2-sin khi3 Piat8-si7-pa. A-pek-lah8-han2 chiu7
tiam3 ti7 Piat8-si7-pa.

20). Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 liau2-au7, u7 lang5 ka7 A-pek-lah8-han2 kong2,
Bit8-ka ka7 li2 e5 sio2-ti7 Na2-hok8 si*-kia*2; toa7-e5 OO-su, 21).
sio2-ti7 Poo3-su, kap A-lan5 e5 lau7-pe7, Ki-boo2-li7; 22). kap Ki-siat,
Hap-so2, Pit-tat8, Ek-lah8, Pi2-thoo2-li7, (Pi2-thoo2-li7 si*
Li7-pek-ka). 23). Chi2 poeh-lang5 long2 si7 Bit8-ka ka7 A-pek-lah8-han2
e5 sio2-ti7 Na2-hok8 si*--e5. 24). Na2-hok8 e5 soe3-i5, mia5 Liu5-ma2,
si* The5-pat, Ka-ham5, Tha-hat, kap Ma2-ka.


[23] Sat-lah8 hiong2-siu7 chit8-pah ji7-chap8-chhit he3; che si7
Sat-lah8 it-seng e5 ni5-he3. 2). Sat-lah8 si2 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5
Ki-liat8-a-pa, chiu7-si7 Hi-pek-lun5; A-pek-lah8-han2 lai5, ui7-tioh8
Sat-lah8 ai-siong thi5-khau3. 3). Au7-lai5 A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3
si2-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 khi2--lai5, ka7 Hek-lang5 kong2, 4). Goa2 ti7
lin2 tiong-kan si7 kia3-ku e5 chhut-goa7 lang5; kiu5 lin2 ti7-chia hoo7
goa2 chit8 e5 soo2-chai7 choe3 thiong2-toe7, thang bai5-chong3 goa2 e5
si2-lang5, hoo7 goa2 bo5 koh khoa*3-ki*3 i. 5). Hek-lang5 in3
A-pek-lah8-han2, ka7 i kong2, 6). Goa2 e5 chu2, chhia*2 thia*; li2 ti7
goan2 tiong-kan choe3 Siong7-te3 e5 bok8-pek; chhut-chai7 li2 ti7 goan2
e5 thiong2-toe7-lai7 keng2 te7-it-ho2--e5, lai5 bai5-chong3 li2 e5
si2-lang5; goan2 bo5 chit8-lang5 m7 iong5-un2 li2 ti7 i e5
thiong2-toe7-lai7 bai5-chong3 li2 e5 si2-lang5. 7). A-pek-lah8-han2
khi2--lai5, tui3 hit soo2-chai7 e5 lang5, chiu7-si7 Hek-chok8, a*3-io.
8). Tui3 in kong2, Lin2 na7 u7 i3-su3 beh hoo7 goa2 bai5-chong3 goa2 e5
si2-lang5, hoo7 goa2 bo5 koh khoa*3-ki*3 i, chiu7 chhia*2 thia* goa2,
thoe3 goa2 kiu5 So2-hat e5 kia*2 I2-hut-lun5, chiong i e5 chhan5-thau5
Bek8-pi2-lah8 e5 hiat8 hoo7 goa2; i thang chiau3 chiok-giah8 e5 ke3-soo3
boe7 hoo7 goa2; hoo7 goa2 ti7 lin2 tiong-kan u7 giap8 thang choe3
bong7-toe7. 10). Tng-si5 I2-hut-lun5 che7 ti7 Hek-lang5 e5 tiong-kan;
tui3 hit-tiap8 Hek-lang5 I2-hut-lun5 ti7 it-chhe3 jip8 i e5 sia*5-mng5
e5 Hek-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, in3 A-pek-lah8-han2, kong2, 11). M7-bian2,
goa2 e5 chu2 thia* goa2; goa2 beh sang3 li2 hit khu chhan5, lian5 hit
lai7-bin7 e5 hiat8 iah8 hoo7 li2; ti7 goa2 tang5-chok8 e5 lang5 e5
bin7-cheng5, goa2 hoo7 li2, thang bai5-chong3 li2 e5 si2-lang5. 12).
A-pek-lah8-han2 chiu7 ti7 hit soo2-chai7 e5 peh-si*3 e5 bin7-cheng5
a*3-io; 13). ti7 hit soo2-chai7 peh-si*3 e5 bin7-cheng5, tui3
I2-hut-lun5 kong2, Li2 na7 kheng2, chhia*2 thia* goa2; goa2 beh chiong
chhan5 e5 ke3-chi*5 hoo7 li2, li2 tioh8 siu; hoo7 goa2 thang ti7-hia
bai5-chong3 goa2 e5 si2-lang5. 14). I2-hut-lun5 in3 A-pek-lah8-han2
kong2, 15). Goa2 e5 chu2, chhia*2 thia* goa2; chhan5 tat8-tit gun5
si3-pah sia3-khek-lek8, ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan, beh sng3 sim2-mih8?
choe3 li2 bai5-chong3 li2 e5 si2-lang5. 16). A-pek-lah8-han2 thia*
I2-hut-lun5 e5 oe7, chiau3 i ti7 Hek-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 soo2
kong2--e5, chiong boe2-boe7 thong-eng7 e5 gun5, pheng5 si3-pah
sia3-khek-lek8 hoo7 I2-hut-lun5.

17). Tui3 hit-tiap8 I2-hut-lun5 e5 chhan5, ti7 Bek8-pi2-lah8, Ban7-li7
e5 thau5-cheng5; hit khu chhan5 kap hi2 lai7-bin7 e5 hiat8, kap
chhan5-lai7 i2-kip8 si3-ui5 it-chhe3 e5 chhiu7-bak8, 18). ti7 Hek-chok8
lang5 kap it-chhe3 jip8 i e5 sia*5-mng5 e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5, long2
tia*7-tioh8 kui hoo7 A-pek-lah8-han2 choe3 giap8. 19). Au7-lai7
A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong i e5 boo2 Sat-lah8 bai5-chong3 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7
Ban7-li7 thau5-cheng5 e5 Bek8-pi2-lah8 chhan5--nih e5 hiat8; Ban7-li7
chiu7-si7 Hi-pek-lun5. 20). Tui3 an2-ni hit khu chhan5 kap chhan5--nih
e5 hiat8, tui3 Hek-lang5 tia*7-tioh8 kui hoo7 A-pek-lah8-han2 choe3
giap8, lai5 choe3 bong7-toe7.


[24] A-pek-lah8-han2 he3-siu7 tng5, ni5-lau7; Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 it-chhe3
e5 su7 long2 su3-hok hoo7 A-pek-lah8-han2. 2). A-peh-lah8-han2 tui3 i
ke-lai7 koan2-li2 choan5-giap8 e5 lau7 loo5-pok8 kong2, Chhia*2 chiong
li2 e5 chhiu2 he7 ti7 goa2 e5 toa7-thui2-e7, goa2 beh kah li2 ki2
Ia5-ho5-hoa, chiu7-si7 thi* e5 Siong7-te3, toe7 e5 Siong7-te3, lai5
chiu3-choa7, goa2 khia7-khi2 Ka-lam5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, li2 m7-thang
ka7 goa2 e5 kia*2 chhoa7 in e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 choe3 boo2. 4). Li2 tioh8
khi3 goa2 e5 pun2-toe7 pun2-chok8, ka7 goa2 e5 kia*2 I2-sat chhoa7 chit8
e5 boo2. 5). Loo5-pok8 in3 i kong2, Siat-su2 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 m7-kheng2
te3 goa2 lai5 chit soo2-chai7, goa2 chiu7 tioh8 chiong li2 e5 kia*2 toa3
to3--khi3 li2 soo2 tui3 hia chhut-lai5 e5 toe7 mah? 6). A-pek-lah8-han2
ka7 i kong2, Li2 tioh8 kin2-sin7, m7-thang chhoa7 goa2 e5 kia*2
to3--khi3 hia; 7). thi* e5 Siong7-te3, Ia5-ho5-hoa, bat chhoa7 goa2
li7-khui lau7-pe7 e5 ke, kap pun2-chok8 e5 toe7, tui3 goa2 kong2-oe7,
iah8 tui3 goa2 chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 beh chiong chit e5 toe7 siu*2-su3
li2 e5 hoo7-e3; I beh chhe I e5 su3-chia2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; li2
chiu7 thang tui3 hia ka7 goa2 e5 kia*2 chhoa7 chit8 e5 boo2. 8).
Siat-su2 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 m7-kheng2 te3 li2 lai5, goa2 kah li2 chiu3 e5
choa7 chiu7 kap li2 bo5 kan-siap8; tok8-tok8 m7-thang toa3 goa2 e5 kia*2
to3--khi3 hia. 9). Loo5-pok8 chiu7 chiong i e5 chhiu2 he7 ti7 chu2-lang5
A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 toa7-thui2-e7; ui7-tioh8 chit e5 su7 tui3 i chiu3-choa7.

10). Hit e5 loo5-pok8 tui3 i chu2-lang5 e5 lok8-to5-tiong, chhu2
chap8-chiah lok8-to5, soa3 toa3 i chu2-lang5 tak8-iu*7 e5 chai5-po2;
khi2-sin khi3 Bi2-soo2-pho-tai7-bi2, kau3 Na2-hok8 e5 sia*5. 11). Jit8
beh am3, cheng3 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 chhut-lai5 chhiu*7 chui2; i chiu7 hoo7
lok8-to5 kui7 ti7 sia*5-goa7 e5 chi*2-pi*. 12). I kong2, Goa2 e5
chu2-lang5 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, kiu5 Li2 si-un
hoo7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 A-pek-lah8-han2, hoo7 goa2 kin-a2-jit8 u7 ho2
cho-gu7. 13). Goa2 ta* khia7 ti7 chi*2-pi*, sia*5-lai7 lang5 e5
cha-boo2-gin2-a2 teh chhut-lai5 chhiu*7 chui2; 14). goa2 beh tui3 chit8
e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 kong2, Chhia*2 pang3-loh8 li2 e5 chui2-pan5, hoo7
goa2 lim chui2, i na7 kong2, Chhia*2 lim, goa2 iah8 beh hoo7 li2 e5
lok8-to5 lim; goan7 hit e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 si7 Li2 soo2 tia*7-tioh8
hoo7 li2 e5 loo5-pok8 I2-sat choe3-boo2; an2-ni goa2 chiu7 chai Li2
si-un hoo7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5. 15). Oe7 iau2 kong2 be7 soah, Li7-pek-ka
keng-thau5 pe7 chui2-pan5 chhut-lai5, i si7 Pi2-thoo2-li7 si*--e5;
Pi2-thoo2-li7 si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 sio-ti7 Na2-hok8 e5 boo2 Bit8-ka e5
kia*2. 16). Hit e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 bin7-mau7 kek8-ki5 sui2, iau2 si7
chai7-sek-lu2, iah8 be7-bat u7 lang5 chhin-kun7 i; i loh8-khi3
chi*2-pi*, chhiu*7-moa2 i e5 pan5 chiu7 khi2-lai5. 17). Loo5-pok8 chau2
chin3-cheng5 ngia5-chih i kong2, Kiu5 li2 chiong pan5-lai7 e5 chui2
tam7-poh8-a2 goa2 lim. 18). Cha-boo2-gin2-a2 kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2,
chhia*2 lim; chiu7 koa*2-kin2 pang3 chui2-pan5 loh8-lai5, khoa3 ti7
chhiu2--nih, hoo7 i lim. 19). Hoo7 i lim beng5-pek8, koh kong2, Goa2
iah8 beh ka7 li2 e5 lok8-to5 chhiu*7 chui2, hoo7 in lim kau3-giah8. 20).
I chiu7 koa*2-kin2 chiong pan5-lai7 e5 chui2 pia*3 ti7 cho5--nih; koh
chau2 kau3 chi*2--nih chhiu*7 chui2 chiu7 ka7 i soo2 u7 e5 lok8-to5
chhiu*7. 21). Hit e5 lang5 chu3-bak8 khoa*3--i, tiam7-tiam7 bo5
kong2-oe7, ai3 chai Ia5-ho5-hoa siu*2-su3 i sun7-su7 e5 loo7 a2-bo5.
22). Lok8-to5 lim beng5-pek8, hit-lang5 chiu7 theh8 chit8 e5 kim-khoan5,
tang7 poa*3 sia3-khek-lek8, nng7 e5 kim chhiu2-khoan5, tang7 chap8
sia3-khek-lek8 hoo7 hit e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2; 23). kong2, Li2 si7
chi7-chui7 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2? chhia*2 ka7 goa2 kong2; lin2 lau7-pe7 e5
ke, u7 soo2-chai7 thang hoo7 goan2 hioh a2-bo5? 24). I chiu7 ka7 i
kong2, Goa2 si7 Bit8-ka tui3 Na2-hok8 soo2 si* e5 kia*2, Pi2-thoo2-li7
e5 cha-boo2-kia*2. 25). I koh tui3 i kong2, Goan2 u7 chhau2-liau7
bi2-niu5 chhiong-chiok; iah8 u7 soo2-chai7 thang hioh. 26). Hit-lang5
chiu7 a*3-thau5 keng3-pai3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, kong2, 27). Tioh8 o-lo2 goa2 e5
chu2 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa; I eng7 chu5-ai3
seng5-sit8 khoan2-thai7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5, long2 bo5 theng5-chi2;
lun7-kau3 goa2, Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 loo7-chiu*7 in2-chhoa7 goa2 kau3 goa2 e5
chu2-lang5 hia*-ti7 e5 ke. 28). Cha-boo2-gin2-a2 chau2 to3--khi3, chiau3
chiah e5 oe7 ka7 in lau7-bu2 thong-ke e5 lang5 kong2. 29). Li7-pek-ka u7
chit8 e5 hia*, mia5 kio3 Lah8-pan, i chhut-khi3 khi3 chi*2-pi*7,
chiu7-kun7 hit-lang5. 30). I khoa*3-ki*3 hit e5 khoan5, koh khoa*3-ki*3
chhiu2-khoan5 ti7 in sio2-be7 e5 chhiu2; iah8 thia*-ki*3 in sio2-be7
Li7-pek-ka e5 oe7, kong2, Hit-lang5 tui3 goa2 kong2 an2-ni, an2-ni; i
chiu7 khi3 hit-lang5 hia, khoa*3-ki*3 hit-lang5 iau2 khia7 ti7 lok8-to5
pi*, oa2-kun7 chui2-chi*2. 31). Chiu7 ka7 i kong2, Li2 chit e5 tit-tioh8
Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok--e5, chhia*2 jip8--lai5, sia*2-su7 khia7 ti7
goa7-bin7? Goa2 i2-keng pi7-pan7 chhu3, kap lok8-to5 e5 soo2-chai7. 32).
Hit-lang5 chiu7 jip8 i e5 chhu3, i chiu7 thau2 lok8-to5 soo2 chai3-e5,
koh eng7 chhau2-liau7 bi2-niu5 chhi7 lok8-to5; phang5 chui2 hoo7
hit-lang5 i2-kip8 kun-te3 e5 lang5 soe2 kha. 33). Chiong chiah8-mih8
pai5 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5, hoo7 i chiah8; chong2-si7 i kong2, Goa2 bo5
beh chiah8, theng3-hau7 goa2 kong2-beng5 goa2 e5 su3-beng7. Lah8-pan
kong2, Chhia*2 li2 kong2. 34). I chiu7 kong2, Goa2 si7 A-pek-lah8-han2
e5 loo5-pok8. 35). Ia5-ho5-hoa toa7-toa7 su3-hok ti7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5,
hoo7 i heng-ong7, koh hoo7 i iu*5, gu5, gun5, kim, loo5-pok8, lu2-pi7,
lok8-to5 kap lu5. 36). Goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 e5 boo2 Sat-lah8, ni5-lau7 e5
si5, ka7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 si* chit8 e5 kia*2; goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 iah8
chiong it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5 hoo7 chit e5 kia*2. 37). Goa2 e5 chu2-lang5
kah goa2 chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 khia7-khi2 Ka-lam5 lang5 e5 toe7, li2
m7-thang ka7 goa2 e5 kia*2 chhoa7 in e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 choe3 boo2. 38).
Li2 tioh8 khi3 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, goa2 pun2-chok8 hia, ka7 goa2 e5
kia*2 chhoa7 chit8 e5 boo2. 39). Goa2 tui3 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 kong2,
Kia*-liau2 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 m7-kheng2 te3 goa2 lai5. 40). I chiu7 ka7
goa2 kong2, Goa2 soo2 hok8-sai7 e5 Ia5-ho5-hoa beh chhe I e5 su3-chia2
kap li2 sa*-kap khi3, hoo7 li2 sun7-su7 e5 loo7, li2 chiu7 thang tui3
goa2 e5 chong-chok8, goa2 e5 pe7 e5 ke, ka7 goa2 e5 kia*2 chhoa7 chit8
e5 boo2; 41). tok8-tok8 ai3 li2 kau3 goa2 pun2-chok8 hia, goa2 kah li2
soo2 chiu3 e5 choa7, chiu7 kap li2 bo5 kan-giap8; in na7 m7 hoo7 li2,
goa2 kah li2 chiu3 e5 choa7, iah8 kap li2 bo5 kan-siap8. 42).
Kin-a2-jit8 goa2 kau3 chi*2-pi*, kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2-lang5
A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 na7 hoo7 goa2 soo2
kia*5 e5 loo7 sun7-su7; 43). goa2 ta* khia7 ti7 chui2-chi*2-pi*, tui3
chit8 e5 chhut-lai5 chhiu*7 chui2 e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 kong2, Chhia*2 li2
chiong li2 pan5--nih e5 chui2 tam7-poh8 hoo7 goa2 lim; 44). i na7 kong2,
Choe3 li2 lim, goa2 iah8 beh ka7 li2 e5 lok8-to5 chhiu*7 chui2; goan7
hit e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 choe3 Ia5-ho5-hoa soo2 tia*7-tioh8 hoo7 goa2 e5
chu2-lang5 e5 kia*2 choe3 boo2--e5. 45). Goa2 sim-lai7 e5 oe7 iau2 kong2
be7 liau2, Li7-pek-ka chiu7 chhut-lai5, keng-thau5-teng2 pe7 chui2-pan5;
loh8-khi3 chi*2-pi* chhiu*7 chui2; goa2 chiu7 ka7 i kong2, Chhia*2 li2
hoo7 goa2 lim. 46). I chiu7 koa*2-kin2 tui3 keng-thau5-teng2 pang3-loh8
chui2-pan5, kong2, Chhia*2 lim, goa2 iah8 hoo7 li2 e5 lok8-to5 lim; goa2
chiu7 lim, i iah8 hoo7 goa2 e5 lok8-to5 lim. 47). Goa2 koh mng7 i kong2,
Li2 si7 chi7-chui7 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2? I in3 kong2, Goa2 si7 Bit8-ka tui3
Na2-hok8 soo2 si* e5 kia*2, Pi2-thoo2-li7, e5 cha-boo2-kia*2; goa2 chiu7
chiong khoan5 koa3 ti7 i e5 phi*7, chhiu2-khoan5 koa3 ti7 i e5 chhiu2.
48). Goa2 chiu7 a*3-thau5 pai3 Ia5-ho5-hoa, o-lo2 goa2 e5 chu2
A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3 Ia5-ho5-hoa; in-ui7 I chhoa7 goa2 kia*5
tu2-ho2 e5 loo7, hoo7 goa2 tit-tioh8 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 sio2-ti7 e5
cha-boo2-sun lai5 hoo7 i e5 kia*2. 49). Ta* lin2 na7 beh eng7 chu5-ai3
seng5-sit8 khoan2-thai7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5, chiu7 ka7 goa2 kong2; na7
m7, iah8 ka7 goa2 kong2; hoo7 goa2 ho2 thang ng3-cho2 a2-si7 ng3-iu7.
50). Lah8-pan kap Pi2-thoo2-li7 in3 kong2, Tai7-chi3 chhut ti7
Ia5-ho5-hoa, goan2 boe7-oe7 tui3 li2 kong2 ho2 a2 phai*2. 51). Li2
khoa*3, Li7-pek-ka ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, thang chiong i chhoa7--khi3,
hoo7 li2 e5 chu2-lang5 e5 kia*2 choe3 boo2, chiau3 Ia5-ho5-hoa soo2
kong2. 52). A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 loo5-pok8 thia*-ki*3 in chiah e5 oe7,
chiu7 ng3 Ia5-ho5-hoa phak ti7 toe7--nih. 53). Hit-tiap8 loo5-pok8
theh8-chhut gun5-khi3 kim-khi3 kap i-hok8 sang3 Li7-pek-ka; koh chiong
po2-mih8 sang3 i e5 hia* kap i e5 lau7-bu2. 54). Loo5-pok8 kap te3 i e5
lang5 lim-chiah8 hioh-mi5; thau3-cha2 khi2-lai5, chiu7 kong2, Chhia*2
chhe goa2 to3-khi3 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 hia. 55). Li7-pek-ka e5 hia* kap i
e5 lau7-bu2 kong2, Iong5-un2 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 kap goan2 tiam3 kui2-jit8,
siang7-chio2 chap8-jit8, jian5-au7 i thang khi3. 56). I tui3 in kong2,
M7-thang choo2-tong3 goa2, Ia5-ho5-hoa i2-keng hoo7 goa2 sun7-su7 e5
loo7; chhia*2 chhe goa2 khi3, hoo7 goa2 to3-khi3 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5 hia.
57). In kong2, Goan2 kio3 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 lai5, tham3 i e5 oe7-i3. 58).
Chiu7 kio3 Li7-pek-ka lai5, mng7 i kong2, Li2 beh kap chit-lang5 khi3
mah? i kong2, Goa2 beh khi3. 59). In chiu7 chhe sio2-be7 Li7-pek-ka, kap
i e5 leng-bu2, kap A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 loo5-pok8, i2-kip8 te3 i e5 lang5
khi3. 60). In chiu7 ka7 Li7-pek-ka chiok-hok, tui3 i kong2, Goan2
sio2-be7 ah, goan7 li2 choe3 chheng-ban7 lang5 e5 lau7-bu2, goan7 li2 e5
hoo7-e3 tit-tioh8 tui3-tek8 e5 koan-ai3. 61). Li7-pek-ka kap i e5
lu2-pi7 khi2-lai5 khia5 lok8-to5, te3 hit e5 lang5; loo5-pok8 chiu7
chhoa7 Li7-pek-ka khi3.

62). I2-sat khia7-khi2 ti7 Lam5-toe7, hit-si5 tui3
Pi2-ji*2-lah8-hai2-lai5 e5 loo7 lai5. 63). Jit8 beh am3, I2-sat
chhut-lai5 ti7 chhan5--nih, cheng7-cheng7 teh siu*7, kiah8-bak8 chit8-e7
khoa*3, khoa*3-ki*3 lok8-to5 lai5. 64). Li7-pek-ka khoa*3-ki*3 I2-sat,
chiu7 tui3 lok8-to5 loh8-lai5. 65). Mng7 hit e5 loo5-pok8 kong2, Ti7
chhan5--nih kia*5-lai5 ngia5-chih lan2--e5 si7 chi7-chui7? Loo5-pok8
kong2, Si7 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5. Li7-pek-ka chiu7 theh8 phe3 ka-ki7 ta3.
66). Loo5-pok8 chiong soo2 choe3 it-chhe3 e5 su7, ka7 I2-sat kong2. 67).
I2-sat chiu7 khan Li7-pek-ka jip8 i e5 lau7-bu2 Sat-lah8 e5 poo3-pi*5,
chhoa7 i choe3 boo2; koh chin thia*3 i. I2-sat tui3 lau7-bu2 si2-au7,
kau3 chit-tiap8 chiah tit-tioh8 an-ui3.


[25] A-pek-lah8-han2 koh chhoa7 chit8 e5 boo2, mia5 kio3 Ki-thoo2-lah8.
2). Ki-thoo2-lah8 ka7 i si* Sim-lan5, Iok-san, Bi2-tan3, Bi2-tian5,
I-si-pa, Su-a. 3). Iok-san si* Si7-pa kap Ti2-tan3. Ti2-tan3 e5
kia*2-sun si7 A-su-li7 chok8, Li7-too-si7 chok8, kap Li7-oo-bi2 chok8.
4). Bi2-tian5 e5 kia*2 si7 I2-hoat, I2-hut, Hap-lok8, A-pi2-tai7,
I2-lek8-tai7; chiah-e5 long2 si7 Ki-thoo2-lah8 e5 kia*2. 5).
A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5 hoo7 I2-sat. 6).
A-pek-lah8-han2 chiong chai5-but2 pun hoo7 i chiah e5 soe2-i5 e5 kia*2;
than3 i pun2-sin iau2 oah8 e5 si5, chhe in li7-khui i e5 kia*2 I2-sat
khi3 tang--si3, kau3 tang-peng5 e5 toe7. 7). A-pek-lah8-han2 it-seng e5
ni5-jit8 si7 chit8-pah chhit-chap8 goo7 he3. 8). A-pek-lah8-han2 chiah8
tng5 he3-siu7, chia*5-choe3 lau7-lang5, ni5-he3 moa2-chiok, tng7-khui3
si2, to3-choo2. 9). I e5 kia*2 I2-sat, I2-sit8-ma2-li7, chiong i
bai5-chong3 ti7 Bek8-pi2-lah8 e5 hiat8; chit e5 hiat8 ti7 Ban7-li7 e5
thau5-cheng5, Hek-lang5 So2-hat e5 kia*2 I2-hut-lun5 e5 chhan5-tiong,
10). chiu7-si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3 Hek-lang5 soo2 boe2 hit khu chhan5.
A-pek-lah8-han2 kap i e5 boo2 Sat-lah8 long2 bai5-chong3 ti7-hia. 11).
A-pek-lah8-han2 si2 liau2-au7, Siong7-te3 su3-hok hoo7 i e5 kia*2
I2-sat; I2-sat oa2-kun7 Pi2-ji*2-lah8-hai2-lai5 khia7-khi2.

12). A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kia*2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 se3-he7, ki3 ti7
e7-toe2: I2-sit8-ma2-li7 chiu7-si7 Sat-lah8 e5 lu2-pi7 Ai-kip8 lang5
Ha7-kah tui3 A-pek-lah8-han2 soo2 si*--e5. 13). I2-sit8-ma2-li7 chiah e5
kia*2 e5 mia5, chiau3 i e5 mia5-ji7 se3-he7, chhin-chhiu*7 e7-toe2:
I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 toa7-kia*2 Ni5-pai5-iok; koh u7 Ki-tat8, A-tek-piat8,
Bi2-pi2-sam; 14). Bi2-si-ma2, Too7-ma2, Ma2-sat; 15). Hap-tai7,
The5-ma2, I-tut8, Na2-hui-si, Ki-ti2-ma2; 16). chiah-e5 chiu7-si7
I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 kia*2 e5 mia5; chiau3 in e5 hiu*-chhng ia*5-che7,
choe3 chap8-ji7 chok8 e5 chok8-tiu*2. 17). I2-sit8-ma2-li7 it-seng
he3-siu7, chit8-pah sa*-chap8 chhit; khui3-tng7 si2 chiu7 to3-choo2.
18). I e5 kia*2-sun toa3 ti7 Hap-hui-lah8 kau3 Ai-kip8 thau5-cheng5 e5
Su-ji*2, beh khi3 A-sut8 e5 loo7; khia7-khi2 ti7 i cheng3 hia*-ti7 e5
thau5-cheng5.

19). A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 kia*2 I2-sat e5 se3-he7, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2:
A-pek-lah8-han2 si* I2-sat; I2-sat chhoa7 Li7-pek-ka choe3 boo2 e5 si5,
tu2-a2 si3-chap8 he3. I si7 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 toe7 e5 A-lan5 lang5
Pi2-thoo2-li7 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2, A-lan5 lang5 Lah8-pan e5 sio2-be7. 21).
I2-sat in-ui7 i e5 boo2 bo5 si*-kia*2, thoe3 i ki5-kiu5 Ia5-ho5-hoa;
Ia5-ho5-hoa un2-chun2 i soo2 kiu5; i e5 boo2 Li7-pek-ka chiu7 hoai5-in7.
22). gin2-a2 ti7 i e5 pak-lai7 sa*-khoeh; i chiu7 kong2, Na7 si7
chit-khoan2, goa2 mih8-sai2 an2-ni? Chiu7 khi3 mng7 Ia5-ho5-hoa. 23).
Ia5-ho5-hoa ka7 i kong2, Nng7-kok ti7 li2 pak-lai7, nng7-chok8 beh tui3
li2 e5 sin-khu chhut; chit-chok8 beh khah-kiong5 hit-chok8; si7-toa7-e5
beh hok8-sai7 si7-soe3-e5. 24). Seng-san2 e5 jit8-ki5 kau3, ko2-jian5
pak-lai7 si7 siang-si*--e5. 25). Thau5-chit8-e5 chhut-lai5--e5, sin-the2
ang5-ang5, thong sin-khu chhin-chhiu*7 phe5-a2-sa*; chiu7 ka7 i ho7-mia5
choe3 I2-so3. 26). Te3-au7 i e5 sio2-ti7 koh chhut-lai5, i e5 chhiu2
khi*5 I2-so3 e5 kha-au7-ti*; chiu7 ka7 i ho7-mia5 kio3 Nga2-kok. Nng7 e5
kia*2 chhut-si3 e5 si5, I2-sat tu2-a2 lak8-chap8 he3.

27). Nng7 e5 gin2-a2 chiam7-chiam7 toa7; I2-so3 gau5 phah-lah8,
siong5-siong5 ti7 soa*-ia2; Nga2-kok choe3-lang5 thiam5-cheng7,
siong5-siong5 toa3 poo3-pi*5-lai7. 28). I2-sat thia*3 I2-so3, in-ui7
siong5-siong5 chiah8 i e5 ia2-bi7. Li7-pek-ka thia*3 Nga2-kok. 29). U7
chit8 jit8 Nga2-kok chu2-thng, I2-so3 tui3 soa*-ia2 to3-lai5, ia3-sian7
kau3-kek8. 30). I2-so3 tui3 Nga2-kok kong2, Goa2 chin ia3-sian7, kiu5
li2 eng7 chit e5 ang5 e5 thng hoo7 goa2 chiah8; in-ui7 an2-ni I2-so3
iah8 mia5 kio3 I2-tong. 31). Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 kin-a2-jit8 eng7
toa7-kia*2 e5 beng5-hun7 boe7 hoo7 goa2. 32). I2-so3 kong2, Goa2 to beh
si2 lah; chit e5 toa7-kia*2 e5 beng5-hun7, tui3 ti7 goa2 u7 sia*2
li7-ek? 33). Nga2-kok kong2, Kin-a2-jit8 li2 tioh8 tui3 goa2
chiu3-choa7. I chiu7 tui3 i chiu3-choa7, chiong toa7-kia*2 e5 beng5-hun7
boe7 hoo7 Nga2-kok. 34). Nga2-kok chiu7 chiong pia*2 kap ang5-tau7-thng
hoo7 I2-so3; i chiu7 lim-chiah8, khi2-lai5 choe3 i khi3; che chiu7-si7
I2-so3 khoa*3-khin toa7-kia*2 e5 beng5-hun7.


[26] A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 si5, thau5-chit8-pai2 ki-hng i2-au7, hit
soo2-chai7 koh u7 ki-hng. I2-sat chiu7 khi3 Ki-lah8-ji*2, kau3
Hui-li7-su7 e5 ong5 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 hia. 2). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 i
chhut-hian7 kong2, Li2 m7-thang loh8-khi3 Ai-kip8, tioh8 toa3 ti7 Goa2
soo2 chi2-si7 li2 e5 toe7. 3). Li2 kia3-ku ti7 chit e5 toe7, Goa2 beh
kap li2 ti7-teh, su3-hok li2; in-ui7 Goa2 beh chiong chiah e5 toe7 long2
hoo7 li2, kap li2 e5 hoo7-e3; Goa2 beh kian-koo3 Goa2 tui3 li2 e5 pe7
A-pek-lah8-han2 soo2 chiu3 e5 choa7. 4). Goa2 beh ke-thi* li2 e5
hoo7-e3, chhin-chhiu*7 thi*--nih e5 chhi* hiah-choe7; koh beh chiong
chiah e5 toe7 long2 hoo7 li2 e5 hoo7-e3; koh toe7-chiu*7 ban7-kok beh
in-ui7 li2 e5 hoo7-e3 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3. 5). Si7 in-ui7 A-pek-lah8-han2
thia* Goa2 e5 oe7, siu2 Goa2 e5 hoan-hu3, Goa2 e5 beng7-leng7, Goa2 e5
lut8-le7, goa2 e5 hoat-too7. 6). I2-sat khia7-khi2 Ki-lah8-ji*2 . 7).
Hit soo2-chai7 e5 lang5 mng7 kau3 i e5 boo2; i chiu7 kong2, I si7 goa2
e5 sio2-be7; m7-ka*2 kong2, Si7 goa2 e5 boo2; sim-lai7 siu*7, Kia*-liau2
hit soo2-chai7 e5 lang5 ui7-tioh8 Li7-pek-ka e5 ian5-koo3 thai5 goa2;
in-ui7 i bin7-mau7 chin sui2. 8). I ti7-hia i2-keng ku2, Hui-li7-su7
ong5, A-pi2-bi2-lek8, tui3 thang-a2 khoa*3, khoa*3-ki*3 I2-sat kap i e5
boo2 Li7-pek-ka teh kun2-chhio3. 9). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kio3 I2-sat lai5,
ka7 i kong2, I sit8-chai7 si7 li2 e5 boo2; li2 sia*2-su7 kong2, i si7
goa2 e5 sio2-be7? I2-sat kong2, Goa2 sim-lai7 siu*7, kia*-liau2 goa2
ui7-tioh8 i lai5 si2. 10). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kong2, Li2 tui3 goan2
soo2-choe3--e5 si7 sim2-mih8 su7? peh-si*3 e5 tiong-kan, hiam2-hiam2 u7
lang5 kap li2 e5 boo2 sa*-kap khun3; li2 chiu7 hoo7 goan2 ham7-loh8
choe7. 11). Tui3 hit-tiap8 A-pi2-bi2-lek8 chiu7 hoan-hu3 cheng3 peh-si*3
kong2, Hoan7-na7 khap8-tioh8 chit-lang5 kap i e5 boo2--e5, tia*7-tioh8
beh hoo7 i si2.

12). I2-sat ti7 hit soo2-chai7 cheng3-choh, hit-ni5 tit-tioh8 pah-pe7;
Ia5-ho5-hoa su3 i hok-khi3. 13). I chiu7 chia*5-choe3 toa7, na2-ku2
na2-toa7, kau3 chia*5-choe3 toa7 hu3-hoo7. 14). I u7 iu*5-kun5 gu5-kun5,
iah8 u7 choe7-choe7 loo5-pok8; Hui-li7-su7 lang5 chiu7 oan3-too3 i. 15).
Tng i e5 lau7-pe7 A-pek-lah8-han2 ti7-teh e5 jit8, i e5 lau7-pe7 e5
loo5-pok8 soo2 khui e5 chi*2, Hui-li7-su7 lang5 long2 ka7 i that--khi3,
eng7 thoo5 thun7-moa2. 16). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 ka7 I2-sat kong2, Li2 tioh8
li7-khui goan2 khi3, in-ui7 li2 pi2 goan2 cham2-jian5 khah kiong5-seng7.
17). I2-sat chiu7 li7-khui hia, ti7 Ki-lah8-ji*2 e5 soa*-kok tah
poo3-pi*5, tiam3 hia khia7-khi2. 18). Tng i e5 lau7-pe7 A-pek-lah8-han2
ti7-teh e5 jit8, soo2 khui hiah e5 chui2-chi*2, kau3 A-pek-lah8-han2
si2-au7, hoo7 Hui-li7-su7 lang5 thun7--khi3; I2-sat teng5-chai3 ka7 i
khui; iu5-gôan chiau3 in lau7-pe7 soo2 ho7 e5 mia5 lai5 mia5 hiah e5
chi*2. 19). I2-sat e5 loo5-pok8 ti7 soa*-kok teh kut8, tu2-tioh8 chit8
e5 oah8-chui2 e5 chi*2. 20). Ki-lah8-ji*2 e5 bok8-chia2 kap I2-sat e5
bok8-chia2 sa*-chi*, kong2 Chit e5 chui2 si7 goan2-e5. I2-sat chiu7 ho7
hit e5 chi*2 e5 mia5 kio3 Ai-sek; in-ui7 in kap i sa*-chi*. 21). In koh
khui chit8 e5 chi*2, ui7 chit e5 chi*2 koh sa*-chi*; chiu7 kio3 i e5
mia5 Se-the5-na2. 22). Li7-khui hia koh khui chit8 e5 chi*2; in bo5 ui7
chit e5 chi*2 koh sa*-chi*; chiu7 ka7 i ho7 mia5 Li7-ho5-pok; si7 kong2,
Ia5-ho5-hoa ta* hoo7 goan2 khui-khoah e5 toe7; goan2 beh ti7 chit e5
toe7 heng-ong7.

23). I2-sat tui3 hia chiu*7-khi3 Piat8-si7-pa. 24). Hit-mi5 Ia5-ho5-hoa
tui3 i chhut-hian7 kong2, Goa2 si7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5
Siong7-te3, m7-bian2 kia*; in-ui7 Goa2 kap li2 ti7-teh, beh su3-hok li2,
hoo7 li2 e5 hoo7-e3 heng-ong7, long2 si7 ui7-tioh8 Goa2 e5 loo5-pok8
A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 ian5-koo3. 25). I chiu7 ti7-hia khi2 chit8 cho7
toa*5, kiu5-kio3 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 mia5, ti7-hia tah i e5 poo3-pi*5. I2-sat
e5 loo5-pok8 chiu7 ti7-hia khui chit8 e5 chi*2.

26). A-pi2-bi2-lek8 kap i e5 peng5-iu2 A-hoo7-sat i2-kip8 i e5 kun-tiu*2
Hui-kok, tui3 Ki-lah8-ji*2 lai5 ki*3--i. 27). I2-sat tui3 in kong2, Lin2
ki3-jian5 oan3-hun7 goa2, kah goa2 li7-khui lin2; ta* sia*2-su7 lai5
goa2 chia? 28). In kong2, Goan2 beng5-beng5 khoa*3-ki*3 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap
li2 ti7-teh, m7-tat8--tioh8 lan2 tiong-kan li2 goan2 chiu3-choa7, hoo7
goan2 kap li2 lip8-iok; 29). li2 bo5 hai7 goan2, chhin-chhiu*7 goan2
be7-bat khap8-tioh8 li2, tok8-tok8 ho2 khoan2-thai7 li2, sang3 li2
an-jian5 to3-khi3; ta* li2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok--e5. 30). I2-sat
chiu7 ui7 in siat ian5-siah8, in chiu7 chiah8 chiu7 lim. 31). Thau3-cha2
khi2-lai5, tai7-ke chiu3-choa7; I2-sat sang3 in khi2-sin, in chiu7
an-jian5 li7-khui i khi3. 32). Siang5 hit-jit8, I2-sat e5 loo5-pok8
lai5, chiong in khui-chi*2 e5 su7 thong-ti i; kong2, Goan2 tit-tioh8
chui2 lah. 33). I chiu7 kio3 hit e5 chi*2 e5 mia5 kio3 Si7-pa; soo2-i2
kau3 kin-a2-jit8 hit e5 sia*5 e5 mia5 kio3-choe3 Piat8-si7-pa.

34). I2-so3 si3-chap8 he3 e5 si5, chhoa7 Hek-lang5 Pi2-li7 e5
cha-boo2-kia*2 Iu5-tek, kap Hek-lang5 I2-lun5 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2
Pa-sit8-boat choe3 boo2. Chi2 nng7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 siong5-siong5 hoo7
I2-sat kap Li7-pek-ka sim-lai7 toa7 iu-hun7.


[27] I2-sat ni5-lau7, bak8-chiu hoe boe7 khoa*3-ki*3, chiu7 kio3 i e5
toa7-kia*2 I2-so3 lai5, ka7 i kong2, Goa2 e5 kia*2 ah; i in3 kong2, Goa2
ti7-chia. 2). Kong2, Goa2 ta* lau7 lah, m7-chai tah-loh8 chit8-jit8 beh
si2. 3). Ta* kiah8 li2 e5 ke-si, chiu7-si7 chi*3-te7 kap keng, khi3
soa*--nih, ka7 goa2 phah-lah8, 4). chiau3 goa2 soo2 kah-i3 e5, chu2 hoo7
i ho2 chu-bi7, phang5-lai5 hoo7 goa2, goa2 thang chiah8; hoo7 goa2 ti7
be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng ka7 li2 chiok-hok. 5). I2-sat ka7 i e5 kia*2 I2-so3
kong2-oe7 e5 si5, Li7-pek-ka thia*-ki*3. I2-so3 khi3 soa*--nih beh
phah-lah8, thang toa3 to3--lai5. 6). Li7-pek-ka chiu7 tui3 i e5 kia*2
Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 khoa*3, goa2 thia*-ki*3 lin2 lau7-pe7 ka7 li2 e5
hia* I2-so3 kong2, Li2 chiong ia2-siu3 ka7 goa2 toa3--lai5, ka7 goa2
chu2 hoo7 i ho2 chu-bi7, hoo7 goa2 chiah8; goa2 beh ti7 be7 si2 e5
tai7-seng, ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5 bin7-cheng5 ka7 li2 chiok-hok. 8). Ta*
goa2 e5 kia*2, li2 tioh8 thia* goa2 e5 oe7, chiau3 goa2 soo2 hoan-hu3
li2--e5. 9). Li2 khi3 iu*5-kun5 hia, ka7 goa2 liah8 nng7 chiah pui5 e5
soa*-iu*5-a2 lai5; goa2 beh ka7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 chu2 ho2 e5 bi7-soo3,
chiau3 i soo2 kah-i3--e5. 10). Li2 phang--khi3 lin2 lau7-pe7 hia, hoo7 i
chiah8; hoo7 i ti7 be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng ka7 li2 chiok-hok. 11). Nga2-kok

u7 mng5, goa2 si7 kng-kut8. 12). Siat-su2 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 bong-tioh8
goa2, beh khoa*3 goa2 choe3 khi-phian3 lang5--e5, goa2 chiu7 chio

lau7-bu2; lau7-bu2 chiu7 chu2 ho2 e5 chu-bi7, chiau3 lau7-pe7 soo2

ke-lai7 e5 sui2-sa*, ka7 i e5 soe2-kia*2 Nga2-kok chheng7. 16). Koh eng7
soa*-iu*5-a2 phe5 pau Nga2-kok e5 chhiu2, kap i am7-kun2 kng-kut8 e5
ui7. 17). Chiu7 chiong soo2 chu2 e5 ho2 chu-bi7 kap pia*2, he7 ti7 i e5
kia*2 Nga2-kok e5 chhiu2. 18). Nga2-kok kau3 in lau7-pe7 hia, kong2,
Goa2 e5 pe7 ah; i kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia; goa2 e5 kia*2; li2 si7
chi7-chui7? 19). Nga2-kok tui3 i e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Goa2 si7 li2 e5
toa7-kia*2 I2-so3; goa2 i2-keng chiau3 li2 soo2 hoan-hu3 goa2--e5 khi3

kia*2, li2 chai*2-iu*7 chiah khoai3 tit-tioh8? I kong2, In-ui7 li2 e5

Nga2-kok chiu7 oa2-kun7 i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat; i chiu7 bong i kong2,
Sia*, si7 Nga2-kok e5 sia*; chhiu2, si7 I2-so3 e5 chhiu2. 23). I2-sat
hun-piat boe7 beng5, in-ui7 i e5 chhiu2 u7 mng5, chhin-chhiu*7 i e5 hia*
I2-so3 e5 chhiu2; chiu7 ka7 i chiok-hok. 24). Koh kong2, Li2 chin-chia*3
si7 goa2 e5 kia*2 I2-so3 mah? I kong2, Goa2 si7. 25). I2-sat kong2,
Phang5-lai5 hoo7 goa2, goa2 beh chiah8 goa2 e5 kia*2 soo2 tit-tioh8 e5
ia2-bi7, ho2 thang ka7 li2 chiok-hok. Chiu7 phang5 hoo7 i, i chiu7
chiah8; iah8 phang5 chiu2 hoo7 i, i chiu7 lim. 26). I e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat
tui3 i kong2, Goa2 e5 kia*2 chin3-cheng5 lai5 chim goa2. 27). I chiu7
chin3-cheng5, chim i e5 lau7-pe7; i e5 lau7-pe7 phi*7-tioh8 i e5 sa* e5
phang-bi7, chiu7 ka7 i chiok-hok kong2:

Goa2 e5 kia*2 e5 phang-bi7,

Chhin-chhiu*7 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok e5 chhan5 e5 phang-bi7;

28). Goan7 Siong7-te3 siu*2-su3 li2 thi*-teng2 e5 kam-loo7;

Se3-chiu*7 e5 pui5-toe7,

Goo7-kak kap sin e5 chiu2 chin-choe7;

29). Cheng3 peh-si*3 hok8-sai7 li2,

Liat8-kok kui7-pai3 li2,

Li2 choe3 li2 hia*-ti7 e5 chu2,

Li2 e5 lau7-bu2 e5 kia*2 kui7-pai3 li2;

Chiu3-choo2 li2--e5 siu7 chiu3-choo2,

Chiok-hok li2--e5 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3.

30). I2-sat ka7 Nga2-kok chiok-hok beng5-pek8, Nga2-kok tu2-tu2 tui3 i
e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat hia chhut-lai5, i e5 hia* I2-so3 phah-lah8 to3--lai5.
31). I iah8 chu2 ho2 e5 bi7-soo3, phang5-lai5 hoo7 i e5 lau7-pe7, kong2,
goa2 e5 pe7 ah, chhia*2 khi2-lai5 chiah8 kia*2 soo2 phah--tioh8-e5, ho2
thang ka7 goa2 chiok-hok. 32). I e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat ka7 i kong2, Li2 si7
chi7-chui7? I kong2, Goa2 si7 li2 e5 kia*2, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 toa7-kia*2,
I2-so3. 33). I2-sat toa7-kia*, ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, kong2, He si7
chi7-chui7, li2 be7 lai5 e5 tai7-seng, phang5 i soo2 phah--tioh8-e5 lai5
hoo7 goa2; goa2 chiah8 i, ka7 i chiok-hok? i tek-khak beh tit-tioh8
hok-khi3. 34). I2-so3 thia*-ki*3 lau7-pe7 e5 oe7, khui-sia* kio3-khoo2
toa7-khau3; tui3 i e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Goa2 e5 pe7 ah, goa2, li2 iah8
tioh8 ka7 goa2 chiok-hok. 35). I2-sat kong2, Li2 e5 sio2-ti7 eng7
khui2-ke3 lai5, chhiu*2 li2 e5 hok-hun7. 36). I2-so3 kong2, I mia5-choe3
Nga2-kok, kiam2 bo5 chin hap8 mah? i khi-phian3 goa2 nng7-pai2; cheng5
chhiu*2 goa2 toa7-kia*2 e5 beng5-hun7; li2 khoa*3, ta* i koh chhiu*2
goa2 e5 hok-hun7. Koh kong2, Kiam2 bo5 lau5 chit8-e5 thang ka7 goa2
chiok-hok mah? 37). I2-sat in3 I2-so3 kong2, Goa2 i2-keng lip8 i choe3
li2 e5 chu2, iah8 chiong i e5 cheng3 hia*-ti7 hoo7 i choe3 loo5-pok8;
iah8 eng7 goo7-kak sin-chiu2 iu*2-chhi7 i; goa2 e5 kia*2 ah, ta* goa2
iau2 oe7 ka7 li2 choe3 sim2-mih8? 38). I2-so3 ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 kong2,
Pe7 ah, li2 e5 chiok-hok kiam2 chi2-u7 chit8-pai2 mah? Goa2 e5 pe7 ah,
goa2, li2 iah8 tioh8 ka7 goa2 chiok-hok. 39). I2-so3 khui-sia*
thi5-khau3. I e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat in3 i, kong2:

Li2 soo2 khia7-khi2--e5, beh u7 se3-chiu*7 e5 pui5-toe7,

Iah8 u7 thi*-teng2 e5 kam-loo7;

40). Li2 beh oa2-kho3 to-kiam3 too7-oah8, koh beh hok8-sai7 li2 e5 sio2-ti7;

Kau3 li2 hun3-heng e5 si5,

Beh tui3 li2 e5 am7-kun2 kun3-khui i e5 gu5-ta*.

41). I2-so3 in-ui7 i e5 lau7-pe7 ka7 Nga2-kok chiok hok-khi3, chiu7
oan3-hun7 Nga2-kok; sim-lai7 kong2, Ui7 lau7-pe7 teng-iu e5 si5
kun7--lah; kau3 hit-si5, goa2 beh thai5-si2 goa2 e5 sio2-ti7 Nga2-kok.
42). U7 lang5 chiong i e5 toa7-kia*2 I2-so3 e5 oe7 ka7 Li7-pek-ka kong2;
i chiu7 chhe lang5 khi3 kio3 i e5 soe3-kia*2 Nga2-kok lai5, ka7 i kong2,
Li2 e5 hia* I2-so3 beh thai5 li2, lai5 siau i e5 hun7-khi3. 43). Ta*
goa2 e5 kia*2, li2 tioh8 thia* goa2 e5 oe7; khi2-lai5, chau2 khi3
Hap-lan5, goa2 e5 hia* Lah8-pan hia; 44). kap i tiam3 kui2-jit8,
theng3-hau7 li2 e5 hia* siu7-khi3 siau. 45). Kau3 li2 e5 hia* siu7-khi3
soah, boe7 ki3-tit li2 tui3 i soo2 choe3 e5 su7, hit-si5 goa2 chiu7 chhe
lang5 chhoa7 li2 tui3 hia to3--lai5. Goa2 sia*2-su3 chit8-jit8 sit-loh8
lin2 nng7-lang5?

46). Li2-pek-ka ka7 I2-sat kong2, Goa2 in-ui7 chiah e5 Hek-lang5 e5
cha-boo2-kia*2, lian5 si*3-mia7 to m7-ai3. Siat-su2 Nga2-kok ia7 chhoa7
chit soo2-chai7 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 choe3 boo2, chhin-chhiu*7 Hek-lang5 e5
cha-boo2-kia*2 hit-khoan2, goa2 oah8 u7 sia*2 loo7-eng7?


[28] I2-sat kio3 Nga2-kok lai5, ka7 i chiok-hok, iah8 hoan-hu3 i kong2,
Li2 m7-thang chhoa7 Ka-lam5 e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 choe3 boo2. 2). Li2
khi2-lai5, khi3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5, kau3 li2 e5 goa7-kong Pi2-thoo2-li7 e5
ke; ti7 li2 e5 bu2-ku7 Lah8-pan cha-boo2-kia*2 e5 tiong-kan, chhoa7
chit8-e5 choe3 boo2. 3). Goan7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3 su3-hok li2,
hoo7 li2 si*-thoa*3 chin-choe7, chia*5-choe3 choe7-choe7 chok8. 4). Koh
chiong soo2 eng3-un2 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 hok-khi3 hoo7 li2, kap li2 e5
hoo7-e3; hoo7 li2 seng5-chiap li2 soo2-kia3-ku e5 toe7, chiu7-si7
Siong7-te3 soo2 hoo7 A-pek-lah8-han2--e5. 5). I2-sat chhe Nga2-kok khi3;
i chiu7 khi3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5; kau3 A-lan5 lang5 Pi2-thoo2-li7 e5 kia*2
Lah8-pan hia; i si7 Nga2-kok I2-soo3 e5 bu2-ku7. 6). I2-so3 khoa*3-ki*3
I2-sat ka7 Nga2-kok chiok-hok, koh chhe i khi3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5, beh tui3
hia chhoa7-boo2; iah8 khoa*3-ki*3 chiok-hok i e5 si5, hoan-hu3 i kong2,
M7-thang chhoa7 Ka-lam5 e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 choe3 boo2; 7). koh
khoa*3-ki*3 Nga2-kok thia* pe7-bu2 e5 oe7, khi3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5; 8).
I2-so3 chiu7 chai Ka-lam5 e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2, i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat
m7-teng3-i3; 9). I2-so3 chiu7 khi3 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 hia, ti7 i hiah e5
boo2 i2-goa7, koh chhoa7 Ma2-hap-lah8 choe3-boo2; i si7 A-pek-lah8-han2
e5 kia*2 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2, Ni5-pai5-iok e5 sio2-be7.

10). Nga2-kok li7-khui Piat8-si7-pa, ng3 Hap-lan5 khi3. 11). Kau3 chit8
soo2-chai7, in-ui7 jit8 loh8, chiu7 ti7-hia hioh-mi5; tui3 hiah e5
chioh8-thau5 e5 tiong-kan, theh8 chit8-te3 choe3 chim2-thau5, ti7-hia
khun3. 12). Bang7-ki*3 u7 thui khia7 ti7 toe7--nih, thui-teng2 tu2-thi*;
u7 Siong7-te3 e5 su3-chia2 ti7 thui--nih teh chiu*7-loh8. 13).
Ia5-ho5-hoa khia7 ti7 thui-teng2, kong2, goa2 si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa li2 e5
choo2 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3, iah8 si7 I2-sat e5 Siong7-te3. Goa2
beh chiong li2 hian7-chai7 soo2 khun3 e5 toe7 siu*2-su3 li2, kap li2 e5
hoo7-e3. 14). Li2 e5 hoo7-e3 beh chhin-chhiu*7 toe7-chiu*7 e5 thoo5-soa;
li2 beh tui3 tang, sai, lam5, pak lai5 hoat-tian2; toe7-chiu*7
ban7-chok8 beh in-ui7 li2 kap li2 e5 hoo7-e3 tit-tioh8 hok-khi3. 15).
Goa2 iah8 kap li2 ti7-teh, li2 bo5-lun7 khi3 tah-loh8, Goa2 beh po2-hoo7
li2; iah8 beh chhoa7 li2 to3-lai5 chit soo2-chai7, long2 bo5 pang3-sak
li2, kau3 Goa2 chia*5 tui3 li2 soo2 kong2--e5. 16). Nga2-kok
khun3-chhi*2 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa chin-chia*3 ti7-chia, goa2 keng2-jian5
m7-chai. 17). Chiu7 kia* kong2, Chit soo2-chai7 kau3 chiah thang kia*!
m7-si7 pat8-hang7, che si7 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3, che si7 thi* e5 mng5.
18). Nga2-kok cha2-cha2 khi2--lai5, chiong i choe3 chim2-thau5 e5 chioh8
khia7 choe3 thiau7; to3 iu5 ti7 teng2-bin7. 19). Chiu7 mia5 hit
soo2-chai7 kio3 Pek-tek8-li7, chit e5 sia*5 pun2 mia5 Loo7-su. 20).
Nga2-kok he7-goan7 kong2, Siong7-te3 na7 kap goa2 ti7-teh, ti7 goa2 soo2
kia*5 e5 loo7 po2-hoo7 goa2, koh hoo7 goa2 u7 mih8 thang chiah8, u7 sa*
thang chheng7, 21). hoo7 goa2 an-jian5 to3-lai5 goa2 e5 pe7 e5 chhu3,
chiu7 Ia5-ho5-hoa tek-khak choe3 goa2 e5 Siong7-te3. 22). Goa2 soo2
khia7 choe3 thiau7 e5 chioh8 beh choe3 Siong7-te3 e5 chhu3; ki*3-na7 Li2
soo2 siu*2-su3 goa2 e5, goa2 beh chiong chap8-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7 hian3
hoo7 Li2.


[29] Nga2-kok khi2-sin, kau3 tang-hng e5 lang5 e5 toe7; khoa*3-ki*3
chhan5--nih u7 chit8 khau2 chi*2, u7 sa* tin7 iu*5 to2 ti7 chi*2-pi*,
in-ui7 lang5 hoo7 iu*5-kun5 lim, long2 si7 eng7 hit e5 chi*2 e5 chui2;
chi*2-chhui3 eng7 toa7 chioh8 kham3. 3). Peng5-si5 iu*5-kun5 chu7-chip8
ti7-hia, lang5 chiu7 chiong chioh8-thau5 soa2 li7 chi*2-chhui3, hoo7
iu*5 lim chui2; chiah koh chiong chioh8-thau5 soa2 kau3 gôan-ui7. 4).
Nga2-kok tui3 in kong2, Hia*-ti7 ah, tui3 tah-loh8 lai5? in kong2, Goan2
tui3 Hap-lan5 lai5. 5). Mng7 in kong2, Na2-hok8 e5 sun Lah7-pan, lin2
bat i mah? 6). kong2, Pat--i. Koh tui3 in kong2, I peng5-an mah? kong2,
Peng5-an. Li2 khoa*3, i e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 Lah8-kiat chhoa7 i e5
iu*5-kun5 teh lai5. 7). Kong2, Jit8 iau2 koai*5, cheng-si* chu7-chip8 e5
si5 be7 kau3, m7-tat8--tioh8 hoo7 iu*5 lim chui2, koh khi3 chhi7. 8). In
kong2, Goan2 boe7-oe7, tioh8 theng3-hau7 choe7-choe7 tin7 long2
chu7-chip8, lang5 soa2 chioh8 li7-khui chi*2-chhui3, chiah thang hoo7
iu*5 lim. 9). Nga2-kok teh kap in kong2-oe7 e5 si5, Lah8-kiat chhoa7 in
lau7-pe7 e5 iu*5 lai5; in-ui7 si7 i teh koo3. 10). Nga2-kok khoa*3-ki*3
bu2-ku7 Lah8-pan e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 Lah8-kiat, kap bu2-ku7 Lah8-pan e5
iu*5-kun5, chiu7 chin3-cheng5 chiong chioh8 soa2 li7 chi*2-chhui3, hoo7
in bu2-ku7 Lah8-pan e5 iu*5-kun5 lim. 11). Nga2-kok ka7 Lah8-kiat
chim-chhui3, khui-sia* khau3. 12). Nga2-kok koh ka7 Lah8-kiat kong2 i
si7 in lau7-pe7 e5 goe7-seng, si7 Li7-pek-ka e5 kia*2; Lah8-kiat chiu7
chau2-khi3 ka7 in lau7-pe7 kong2. 13). Lah8-pan thia*-ki*3 goe7-seng
Nga2-kok e5 siau-sit, chiu7 chau2-khi3 ngia5-chih--i, pho7--i, kap i
chim-chhui3; chhoa7 i kau3 in tau; Nga2-kok chiong it-chhe3 e5
su7-cheng5 ka7 Lah8-pan kong2. 14). Lah8-pan ka7 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2
sit8-chai7 si7 goa2 e5 kut-jiok8. I chiu7 kap i toa3 chit8-geh8-jit8.
15). Lah8-pan ka7 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 sui-jian5 si7 goa2 e5 chhin-chhek,
kiam2 thang peh8-peh8 choe3 goa2 e5 kang; chhia*2 ka7 goa2 kong2, li2
beh sim2-mih8 kang-chi*5. 16). Lah8-pan u7 nng7 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2,
toa7-e5 mia5-kio3 Li7-a, soe3--e5 mia5-kio3 Lah8-kiat. 17). Li7-a
bak8-chiu khah-su, Lah8-kiat si*-choe3 ho2-khoa*3. 18). Nga2-kok thia*3
Lah8-kiat, chiu7 kong2, Goa2 goan7 ui7-tioh8 li2 soe3 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2
Lah8-kiat, ka7 li2 choe3-kang chhit-ni5. 19). Lah8-pan kong2, Chiong i
ke3 hoo7 li2, khah-ho2 hoo7 pat8-lang5; li2 kap goa2 toa3. 20). Nga2-kok
chiu7 ui7-tioh8 Lah8-kiat ka7 i choe3 kang chhit-ni5; in-ui7
chhim-thia*3 i, khoa*3-choe3 kui2-na7 jit8. 21). Nga2-kok tui3 Lah8-pan
kong2, Jit8-ki5 i2-keng moa2, kiu5 li2 chiong goa2 e5 boo2 hoo7 goa2,
goa2 thang kap i tang5-pang5. 22). Lah8-pan chu7-chip8 hit soo2-chai7 e5
cheng3-lang5, pan7 ian5-siah8 chhia*2 in. 23). Kau3 jit8 am3, Lah8-pan
chiong i e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 Li7-a, sang3 lai5 hoo7 i; Nga2-kok chiu7 kap
i tang5-pang5. 24). Lah8-pan chiong i e5 lu2-pi7 Sek-pha*3 hoo7 i e5
cha-boo2-kia*2 Li7-a choe3 lu2-pi7. 25). Kau3 thi*-kng, chit8-e7
khoa*3-ki*3 si7 Li7-a, chiu7 tui3 Lah8-pan kong2, Li2 ka7 goa2
choe3--e5, si7 sim2-mih8? Goa2 ka7 li2 choe3-kang, kiam2-m7-si7
ui7-tioh8 Lah8-kiat mah? li2 sia*2-su7 phian3 goa2? 26). Lah8-pan kong2,
Be7 ke3 toa7--e5 tai7-seng ke3 soe3--e5, ti7 goan2 chia bo5 lang5 an2-ni
choe3. 27). Li2 kap chit-e5 tioh8 moa2 chhit-jit8; goan2 chiu7 chiong
hit-e5 iah8 ke3 hoo7 li2; li2 ui7-tioh8 i koh ka7 goa2 choe3 kang
chhit-ni5. 28). Nga2-kok chiu7 chiau3 an2-ni kia*5; kap chit-e5 moa2
chhit-jit8; i chiu7 chiong i e5 cha-boo2-kia*2, Lah8-kiat, hoo7 i
choe3-boo2. 29). Lah8-pan chiong i e5 lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8, hoo7 i e5
cha-boo2-kia*2 Lah8-kiat choe3 lu2-pi7. 30). Nga2-kok iah8 kap Lah8-kiat
tang5-pang5, koh thia*3 Lah8-kiat ia*5-ke3 Li7-a; chiu7 koh ka7 Lah8-pan
choe3-kang chhit-ni5.

31). Ia5-ho5-hoa khoa*3 Li7-a bo5 tek-thiong2, chiu7 hoo7 i hoai5-in7;
tok8-tok8 Lah8-kiat bo5. 32). Li7-a hoai5-in7 si*-kia*2, chiu7 ka7 i
ho7-mia5 Liu5-pian7; in-ui7 kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa khoa*3-ki*3 goa2 e5
khoo2-cheng5; ta* goa2 e5 tiong7-hu beh thia*3 goa2. 33). I koh
hoai5-in7 si* kia*2, kong2, Ia5-ho5-hoa thia*-ki*3 goa2 bo5 tek-thiong2,
soo2-i2 koh hoo7 goa2 chit e5 kia*2; chiu7 ka7 i ho7-mia5 Se-bian7. 34).
Koh hoai5-in7 si* kia*2, kong2, Goa2 ka7 tiong7-hu si* sa* e5 kia*2, i
beh kap goa2 kiat-lian5; mia5 kio3 Li7-bi7. 35). Koh hoai5-in7 si*
kia*2; kong2 Chit-e7 goa2 beh o-lo2 Ia5-ho5-hoa; soo2-i2 kio3 i e5 mia5
Iu5-tai7; chiu7 theng5 bo5 koh si*.


[30] Lah8-kiat khoa*3 pun2-sin bo5 ka7 Nga2-kok si* kia*2, chiu7
oan3-too3 i e5 toa7-chi2; tui3 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 tioh8 kia*2 hoo7
goa2; na7 bo5, goa2 beh si2. 2). Nga2-kok siu7-khi3 Lah8-kiat; kong2,
Hoo7 li2 bo5 si*--e5, si7 Siong7-te3; goa2 kiam2 si7 thoe3 I mah? 3).
Lah8-kiat kong2, Li2 khoa*3 goa2 e5 lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8 ti7-chia; li2 khi3
kap i tang5-pang5, hoo7 i si* kia*2 pho7 ti7 goa2 e5 kha-thau5-u; goa2
ia7 chiu7 thang tui3 i tit-tioh8 kia*2. 4). Lah8-kiat chiu7 chiong i e5
lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8 hoo7 i choe3-boo2; Nga2-kok chiu7 kap i tang5-pang5.
5). Phek-lah8 hoai5-in7, ka7 Nga2-kok si* chit8 e5 kia*2. 6). Lah8-kiat
kong2, Siong7-te3 ka7 goa2 phoa*3-toan3, iah8 thia* goa2 e5 sia*, hoo7
goa2 u7 kia*2; soo2-i2 kio3 i e5 mia5 choe3 Tan3. 7). Lah8-kiat e5
lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8 koh hoai5-in7, ka7 Nga2-kok si* te7-ji7 e5 kia*2; 8).
Lah8-kiat kong2, Goa2 kap goa2 e5 toa7-chi2 hui-siong5 e5 sa*-chi*, iah8
tit-tioh8 khah-ia*5; chiu7 kio3 i e5 mia5 choe3 Na2-hut-tha-li7. 9).
Li7-a khoa*3 pun2-sin theng5-hioh bo5 si*, chiu7 chiong i e5 lu2-pi7,
Sek-pha*3, hoo7 Nga2-kok choe3 boo2. 10). Li7-a e5 lu2-pi7 Sek-pha*3 ka7
Nga2-kok si* kia*2. 11). Li7-a kong2, Kai-chai3! chiu7 kio3 i e5 mia5
choe3 Ka-tek. 12). Li7-a e5 lu2-pi7, Sek-pha*3, koh ka7 Nga2-kok si*
te7-ji7 e5 kia*2. 13). Li7-a kong2, Goa2 u7 hok-khi3! chiah e5
cha-boo2-gin2-a2 long2 beh chheng goa2 u7 hok-khi3; chiu7 kio3 i e5 mia5
