choe3 A-siat. 14). Koah-beh8 e5 si5, Liu5-pian7 khi3 chhan5--nih,
tit-tioh8 hong-ka, theh8-lai5 hoo7 i e5 lau7-bu2 Li7-a. Lah8-kiat tui3
Li7-a kong2, Chhia*2 chiong li2 e5 kia*2 e5 hong-ka hoo7 goa2. 15).
Li7-a tui3 i kong2, Li2 chhiu*2-toat8 goa2 e5 tiong7-hu, kiam2-si7
sio2-khoa2 su7; li2 koh chhiu*2-toat8 goa2 e5 kia*2 e5 hong-ka mah?
Lah8-kiat kong2, Ui7-tioh8 li2 e5 kia*2 e5 hong-ka, soo2-i2 kin-mi5 i
thang kap li2 sa*-kap khun3. 16). Kau3 am3, Nga2-kok tui3 chhan5--nih
to3-lai5; Li7-a chhut-khi3 ngia5-chih i, kong2, Li2 tioh8 kap goa2
sa*-kap khun3; in-ui7 goa2 sit8-chai7 eng7 goa2 e5 kia*2 e5 hong-ka
chhia*3 li2. Hit-mi5 i chiu7 kap i sa*-kap khun3. Siong7-te3 un2-chun2
Li7-a, i chiu7 hoai5-in7, ka7 Nga2-kok si* te7-goo7 e5 kia*2. 18). Li7-a
kong2, Siong7-te3 hoo7 goa2 kang-chi*5, in-ui7 goa2 chiong lu2-pi7 hoo7
goa2 e5 tiong7-hu; tui3 an2-ni ka7 i ho7-mia5 I2-sat-ka. 19). Li2-a koh
hoai5-in7, ka7 Nga2-kok si* te7-lak8 e5 kia*2. 20). Li7-a kong2,
Siong7-te3 siu*2-su3 goa2 ho2 e5 siu*2-su3; goa2 e5 tiong7-hu beh kap
goa2 toa3, in-ui7 goa2 ka7 i si* lak8 e5 kia*2; tui3 an2-ni ka7 i
ho7-mia5 Se-poo3-lun5. 21). Au7-lai5 si* chit8 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2, ka7 i
ho7-mia5 kio3 Ti2-na2. 22). Siong7-te3 siau3-liam7 Lah8-kiat, Siong7-te3
un2-chun2 i, hoo7 i oe7 si* kia*2. 23). I chiu7 hoai5-in7 si* kia*2;
kong2, Siong7-te3 tu5--khi3 goa2 e5 kian3-siau3; 24). chiu7 ka7 i
ho7-mia5 Iok-sek, kong2, Goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa koh ke-thi* goa2 chit8 e5 kia*2.

25). Lah8-kiat si* Iok-sek liau2-au7, Nga2-kok tui3 Lah8-pan kong2,
Chhia*2 chhe goa2 khi3, hoo7 goa2 to3-khi3 goa2 e5 pun2 soo2-chai7,
pun2-toe7; 26). chhia*2 li2 chiong goa2 hok8-sai7 li2 soo2 tit-tioh8 e5
boo2-kia*2 hoo7 goa2, iong5-un2 goa2 khi3; goa2 chai*2-iu*7 hok8-sai7
li2, li2 long2 chai. 27). Lah8-pan ka7 i kong2, Goa2 na7 ti7 li2 e5
bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, chhia*2 li2 kap goa2 toa3; in-ui7 goa2
chhim-chai Ia5-ho5-hoa su3 goa2 hok-khi3, si7 ui7-tioh8 li2 e5
ian5-koo3. 28). Koh ka7 i kong2, Chhia*2 li2 tia*7-tioh8 li2 e5
kang-chi*5, goa2 chiu7 hoo7 li2. 29). Nga2-kok ka7 i kong2, Goa2
hok8-sai7 li2 chai*2-iu*7, li2 e5 cheng-si* ti7 goa2 e5 chhiu2-thau5
chai*2-iu*7, si7 li2 soo2 chai. 30). Goa2 be7 lai5 e5 tai7-seng, li2
soo2-u7--e5 chin-chio2, ta* chiu7 toa7 hoat-tat8; Ia5-ho5-hoa eng7
hok-khi3 te3 goa2 e5 kha lai5 hoo7 li2; ta* goa2 beh sim2-mih8 si5 ui7
goa2 e5 ke kian3-ti3 san2-giap8? Lah8-pan kong2, Goa2 tioh8 hoo7 li2
sim2-mih8? Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 iah8 m7-bian2 hoo7 goa2 sim2-mih8; u7
chit8-hang7 su7, li2 na7 eng3-seng5, chiu7 goa2 iu5-gôan chhi7 li2 e5
iu*5-kun5 lai5 koo3-siu2. 32). Kin-a2-jit8 goa2 beh pian3-sun5 li2 e5
iu*5-kun5, chiong mi5-iu*5-tiong ki*3-u7 tiam2--e5, u7 pan--e5, kap
oo-sek--e5, i2-kip8 soa*-iu*5-tiong ki*3-u7 pan--e5, u7 tiam2--e5, long2
poah-chhut; chiong-lai5 chit-khoan2--e5 choe3 goa2 e5 kang-chi*5. 33).
I2-au7 li2 lai5 khoa*3 goa2 e5 kang-chi*5, hit tiong-kan na7 soa*-iu*5
bo5 tiam2 bo5 pan--e5, mi5-iu*5 bo5 oo-sek--e5, chiu7 sng3 si7 goa2
thau--e5; eng7 an2-ni lai5 cheng3-beng5 goa2 e5 kong-to7. 34). Lah8-pan
kong2, Ho2, goa2 goan7 chiau3 li2 e5 oe7 kia*5. 35). Tng hit-jit8, chiu7
chiong u7 hun5 u7 pan e5 soa*-iu*5-kang2, u7 tiam2 u7 pan, kai*3 peh8 e5
soa*-iu*5-bu2, i2-kip8 oo-sek e5 mi5-iu*5, long2 poah-chhut lai5 kau
hoo7 i hiah e5 kia*2. 36). I hoo7 ka-ki7 kap Nga2-kok sa*-li7 u7
sa*-jit8 e5 loo7-cham7; Nga2-kok chiu7 koo3 Lah8-pan ki5-u5 e5 iu*5.
37). Nga2-kok theh8 chhi* e5 iong5-chhiu7, heng7-chhiu7, png-chhiu7,
nng2 e5 ki, chiong phe5 pak chia*5 peh8-hun5, hoo7 ki-lai7 peh8--e5
loo7-chhut. 38). Chiong pah-phe5 e5 ki, chhah ti7 iu*5 lim-chui2 e5
chui2-kau kap chui2-cho5, hoo7 i kap iu*5 sa*-tui3; iu*5 lai5 lim e5
si5, kang-bu2 kau-hap8; 39). iu*5 ti7 ki e5 tui3-bin7 kau-hap8, chiu*7
si* u7-hun5--e5, u7-tiam2--e5, u7-pan--e5. 40). Nga2-kok chiong iu*5-a2
poah-chhut, hoo7 Lah8-pan e5 iu*5 kap chiah e5 u7-hun5 kap oo-sek e5
iu*5 sa*-tui3; chiong ka-ki7 e5 iu*5 leng7-goa7 pang3 ti7 chit8
soo2-chai7, bo5 hoo7 i kap Lah8-pan e5 iu*5 chham-chhap. 41). Tu2-tioh8
iu*5-kun5-tiong iong2-chong3-e5 kau-hap8 e5 si5, Nga2-kok chiu7 eng7
chhiu7-ki chhah ti7 chui2-kau-lai7; hoo7 iu*5 ti7 chhiu7-ki e5 tui3-bin7
kau-hap8. 42). Tu2-tioh8 iu*5-kun e5 san2--e5, chiu7 bo5 chhah
chhiu7-ki; tui3 an2-ni san2--e5 kui Lah8-pan, iong2-chong3--e5 kui
Nga2-kok. 43). Tui3 an2-ni i toa7 hoat-tat8, tit-tioh8 choe7-choe7
iu*5-kun5, lu2-pi7, loo5-pok8, lok8-to5, kap lu5.


[31] Nga2-kok thia*-ki*3 Lah8-pan cheng3-kia*2 u7 oe7 kong2, Lan2
lau7-pe7 soo2-u7--e5, Nga2-kok long2 chhiu*2-khi3, koh tui3 lan2 e5
lau7-pe7 tit-tioh8 chit-e5 it-chhe3 e5 eng5-kng. 2). Nga2-kok
khoa*3-ki*3 Lah8-pan ki*3-tioh8 i, bo5 chhin-chhiu*7 chiong5-cheng5 e5
bin7-sek. 3). Ia5-ho5-hoa tui3 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 tioh8 to3--khi3 li2
e5 pe7-kong e5 toe7, kau3 li2 e5 chhin-chok8 hia; Goa2 beh kap li2
ti7-teh. 4). Nga2-kok chhe lang5 kio3 Lah8-kiat kap Li7-a kau3 soa*-ia2,
kau3 iu*5-kun5 hia; 5). tui3 in kong2, Goa2 khoa*3-ki*3 lin2 lau7-pe7
ki*3-tioh8 goa2, bo5 chhin-chhiu*7 chiong5-cheng5 e5 bin7-sek;
chong2-si7 goa2 e5 pe7 e5 Siong7-te3 si5-siong5 kap goa2 ti7-teh. 6).
Lin2 iah8 chai goa2 chin7 goa2 e5 lat8 choe3 lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 kang. 7).
Lin2 lau7-pe7 phian3 goa2, chap8-pai2 koe2-oa*7 goa2 e5 kang-chi*5;
chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 bo5 iong2-un2 i hai7 goa2. 8). I na7 kong2,
U7-tiam2--e5 kui li2 choe3 kang-chi*5, chiu7 iu*5-kun5 soo2 si*--e5
long2 u7-tiam2; i na7 kong2, U7-hun5--e5 kui li2 choe3 kang-chi*5, chiu7
iu*5-kun5 soo2 si*--e5 long2 u7-hun5. 9). An2-ni Siong7-te3 chiong lin2
lau7-pe7 e5 cheng-si* chhiu*2-lai5 hoo7 goa2. 10). Iu*5 kau-hap8 e5 si5,
goa2 bang7-tiong kiah8-bak8 chit8-e7 khoa*3, khoa*3-ki*3 phah iu*5-bu2
e5 iu*5-kang2, long2 si7 u7-hun5--e5, u7-tiam2--e5, u7 hoe-pan--e5; 11).
Siong7-te3 e5 su3-chia2 ti7 hit bang7-tiong kio3 goa2 kong2, Nga2-kok;
goa2 kong2, Goa2 ti7 chia. 12). I kong2, Li2 kiah8-bak8 khoa*3, phah
iu*5-bu2 e5 iu*5-kang2, long2 si7 u7-hun5--e5, u7-tiam2--e5, u7
hoe-pan--e5; hoan7-na7 Lah8-pan tui3 li2 soo2 choe3--e5, Goa2 long2
khoa*3-ki*3. 13). Goa2 si7 Pek-tek8-li7 e5 Siong7-te3, li2 ti7-hia bat
eng7 iu5 boah thiau7, tui3 Goa2 he7-goan7. Ta* li2 tioh8 khi2-lai5,
li2-khui chit soo2-chai7, to3-khi3 pun2-toe7. 14). Lah8-kiat kap Li7-a
in3 i kong2, Ti7 goan2 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, kiam2 iau2 u7 goan2 thang tit e5
ke-he2 kap san2-giap8 mah? 15). Goan2 kiam2-m7-si7 hoo7 i khoa*3-choe3
goa7-lang5 mah? in-ui7 i boe7 goan2, thun-chiah8 goan2 e5 ke3-chi*5;
16). Siong7-te3 tui3 goan2 lau7-pe7 chhiu*2-chhut it-chhe3 e5
chai5-but8, hiah-e5 chiu7-si7 goan2 kap goan2 kia*2 e5. Ta* ki*3-na7
Siong7-te3 soo2 tui3 li2 kong2--e5, choe3 li2 khi3 kia*5. 17). Nga2-kok
chiu7 khi2-lai5, hoo7 i e5 kia*2 kap boo2 long2 khia5 lok8-to5. 18). Koh
toa3 it-chhe3 e5 cheng-si*, kap soo2 chek-chu7 e5 chai5-but8, soo2
tit-tioh8 e5 cheng-si*, si7 ti7 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 soo2 tit-tioh8-e5; beh
khi3 Ka-lam5 toe7, khi3 i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat hia. 19). Hit-si5 Lah8-pan
khi3 chian2 iu*5-mng5; Lah8-kiat thau-theh8 in lau7-pe7 ke-lai7 e5
ngoo2-siong7. 20). Nga2-kok poe7 A-lan5 lang5 Lah8-pan, thau-chau2 khi3,
bo5 ka7 i kong2. 21). Chiu7 toa3 it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5 to5-chau2; i
khi2-sin ke3 hit e5 Ho5, ng3 Ki-liat8 soa* khi3.

22). Kau3 te7-sa* jit8, u7 lang5 ka7 Lah8-pan kong2, Nga2-kok chau2-khi3
lah. 23). I chiu7 chhoa7 i e5 hia*-ti7 sa*-kap khi3 tui-jip; lek8-ke3
chhit-jit8 e5 loo7-cham7, kau3 Ki-liat8 soa* chiah jip-tioh8. 24).
Mi5--si5 bin5-bang7-tiong, Siong7-te3 kau3 A-lan5 lang5, Lah8-pan hia;
ka7 i kong2, Li2 tioh8 sio2-sim, m7-thang kap Nga2-kok kong2-ho2
kong2-phai*2. 25). Lah8-pan tui-tioh8 Nga2-kok, Nga2-kok ti7 hit e5 soa*
i2-keng tah poo3-pi*5; Lah8-pan kap i e5 cheng3 hia*-ti7, iah8 ti7
Ki-liat8 soa* tah poo3-pi*5. 26). Lah8-pan ka7 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 soo2
choe3 si7 sim2-mih8 su7, li2 sia*2-su7 poe7 goa2, chiong goa2 chiah e5
cha-boo2-kia*2 chhoa7--khi3, chhin-chhiu*7 eng7 to-kiam3 chhiu*2-liah8
chit8-iu*7? 27). Li2 sia*2-su7 am3-chi*7 chau2, thau-chau2 iah8 bo5 ka7
goa2 kong2; hoo7 goa2 thang eng7 hoa*-hi2, chhiu*3-koa, phah-koo2,
toa*5-khim5, sang3 li2 to3-khi3? 28). Koh bo5 iong5-un2 goa2 kap
goa7-sun, cha-boo2-kia*2 chim-chhui3? li2 ta* soo2 kia*5 si7 chin gong7.
29). Goa2 e5 chhiu2 pun2 u7 lat8 thang hai7 lin2; tok8-tok8 lin2
lau7-pe7 e5 Siong7-te3 cha7-mi5 ka7 goa2 kong2, Li2 tioh8 sio2-sim,
m7-thang kap Nga2-kok kong2-ho2 kong2-phai*2. 30). Ta* li2 sui-jian5
loan5-boo7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke, put-tek-put tioh8 khi3, sia*2-su7
thau-theh8 goa2 e5 sin5-beng5? 31). Nga2-kok in3 Lah8-pan kong2, In-ui7
goa2 kia*, sim-lai7 siu*7, kong2, Kia*-liau2 li2 chiong li2 e5
cha-boo2-kia*2 tui3 goa2 chhiu*2--khi3. 32). Lun7-kau3 li2 e5
sin5-beng5, li2 tui3 sim2-mih8 lang5 chhiau-tioh8, i chiu7 tioh8 si2;
tng lan2 cheng3 hia*-ti7 e5 bin7-cheng5, li2 jin7-khoa*3, ti7 goa2 chia
u7 sim2-mih8 mih8 si7 li2-e5, thang theh8--khi3. In-ui7 Nga2-kok m7-chai
Lah8-kiat u7 thau-theh8--in. 33). Lah8-pan chiu7 jip8 Nga2-kok e5
poo3-pi*5, Li2-a e5 poo3-pi*5, kap nng7 e5 lu2-pi7 e5 poo3-pi*5, long2
chhiau-bo5; chiu7 tui3 Li7-a e5 poo3-pi*5 chhut-lai5, jip8 Lah8-kiat e5
poo3-pi*5. 34). Lah8-kiat i2-keng chiong ngoo2-siong7 khng3 ti7 lok8-to5
e5 oa*-e7, lai5 che7 ti7 hit teng2-bin7. Lah8-pan ti7 i e5
poo3-pi*5-lai7 si3-koe3 bong, long2 chhiau-bo5. 35). Lah8-kiat tui3 i e5
lau7-pe7 kong2, Keng-ki5 tu2-a2 kau3, boe7-oe7 khi2-lai5 ti7 li2 e5
bin7-cheng5; kiu5 goa2 e5 chu2 boh8-tit siu7-khi3. Lah8-pan si3-koe3
chhe7 ngoo2-siong7, chhiau long2 bo5. 36). Nga2-kok chiu7 siu7-khi3, kap
Lah8-pan ke3-kau3; tui3 Lah8-pan kong2, Goa2 u7 hoan7-tioh8 sim2-mih8
ke3-sit, u7 sim2-mih8 choe7-ok, li2 keng2-jian5 jip goa2 chiah-kin2?
37). Li2 pian3-bong goa2 it-chhe3 e5 ke-si, u7 chhiau-tioh8 lin2 tau
sim2-mih8 ke-si chhut lai5? thang he7 ti7 goa2 e5 hia*-ti7 e5
bin7-cheng5; ho7 in ti7 lan2 nng7-lang5 e5 tiong-kan phoa*3-toan3. 38).
Goa2 kap li2 toa3 chi2 ji7-chap8 ni5, li2 e5 mi5-iu*5-bu2, m7-bat u7
lau3-the; li2 iu*5-kun5-tiong e5 iu*5-kang2, goa2 be7-bat chiah8--i.
39). Hoo7 ia2-siu3 siong-hai7--e5, goa2 bo5 toa3-lai5 hoo7 li2; goa2
pun2-sin che7-giah8; bo5 lun7 jit8--si5 siu7-thau, mi5-si5 siu7-thau,
li2 long2 tui3 goa2 tho2-pe5. 40). Goa2 jit8--si5 hoo7 jit8 phak8,
mi5--si5 hoo7 sng tang3, long2 boe7-koo3-tit khun3, goa2 siong5-siong5
si7 an2-ni. 41). Goa2 chi2 ji7-chap8-ni5 ti7 li2 e5 ke, ui7-tioh8 li2
nng7 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2, ka7 li2 choe3-kang chap8-si3 ni5; ui7-tioh8 li2
e5 iu*5-kun5 lak8 ni5; li2 chap8-pai2 koe2-oa*7 goa2 e5 kang-chi*5. 42).
Na7 m7-si7 u7 goa2 e5 pe7 e5 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5
Siong7-te3, koh si7 I2-sat soo2 kia*-ui3--e5, kap goa2 ti7-teh; li2 ta*
un2-tang3 hoo7 goa2 khang-chhiu2 khi3. Siong7-te3 khoa*3-ki*3 goa2 e5
khoo2-cheng5, kap goa2 e5 lo5-lok8, chiah ti7 cha7-mi5 chek-pi7 li2.
43). Lah8-pan in3 Nga2-kok kong2, Chiah e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 si7 goa2 e5
cha-boo2-kia*2; chiah e5 gin2-a2 si7 goa2 e5 gin2-a2; chiah e5 iu*5-kun5
iah8 si7 goa2 e5 iu*5-kun5; hoan7-na7 li2 soo2 khoa*3-ki*3--e5, long2
si7 goa2 e5; goa2 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2, kap in soo2 si* e5 gin2-a2;
kin-a2-jit8 goa2 oe7 ka7 in choe3 sim2-mih8? 44). Ta* lai5, lan2
nng7-lang5 thang lai5 lip8-iok, ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan choe3 cheng3-ku3.

45). Nga2-kok chhu2 chioh8, khia7 choe3 thiau7. 46). Nga2-kok tui3 chiah
e5 hia*-ti7 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 khioh chioh8-thau5; in chiu7 chiong
chioh8-thau5 khioh lai5 thiap8 kui-tui; tai7-ke chiu7 ti7 hit tui e5
pi*-a2 chiah8. 47). Lah8-pan mia5 i kio3 I-ka-ni2-sat-khap-too7-tha;
Nga2-kok mia5 i kio3 Ka-lui7-tek. 48). Lah8-pan kong2, Kin-a2-jit8 chit
e5 chioh8-tui choe3 li2 goa2 tiong-kan e5 cheng3-ku3. In-ui7 an2-ni,
mia5 i kio3 Ka-lui7-tek; 49). ia7 kio3-choe3 Bi2-su-pa; chiu7-si7 kong2,
Lan2 tai7-ke li7-piat8 i2-au7, goan7 Ia5-ho5-hoa ti7 li2 goa2 e5
tiong-kan kam3-chhat. 50). Li2 na7 khoo2-chhoo2 goa2 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2,
koh ti7 goa2 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 i2-goa7 leng7-goa7 chhoa7-boo2, sui-jian5
bo5 lang5 kap lan2 ti7-teh, u7 Siong7-te3 ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan
choe3 kan-cheng3. 51). Lah8-pan koh tui3 Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 khoa*3 chit
tui chioh8, li2 khoa*3 chit ki thiau7; chiu7-si7 goa2 soo2 he7 ti7 li2
goa2 e5 tiong-kan--e5. 52). Chit tui chioh8 choe3 kan-cheng3, chit ki
thiau7 choe3 kan-cheng3; goa2 bo5 beh ke3 chit tui chioh8 khi3 hai7 li2,
li2 ia7 m7-thang ke3 chit tui chioh8 kap thiau7, lai5 hai7 goa2. 53).
Goan7 A-pek-lah8-han2 e5 Siong7-te3, Na2-hok8 e5 Siong7-te3, in lau7-pe7
e5 Siong7-te3, ti7 li2 goa2 e5 tiong-kan phoa*3-toan3. Nga2-kok chiu7
ki2 in lau7-pe7 I2-sat soo2 kia*-ui3 e5 Siong7-te3 lai5 chiu3-choa7.
54). Nga2-kok ti7 soa*--nih hian3-che3, chhia*2 i hiah e5 hia*-ti7 lai5
chiah8; in chiah8-liau2, chiu7 ti7 soa*--nih hioh-mi5. 55). Lah8-pan
thau3-cha2 khi2-lai5, kap i e5 goa7-sun, kap i e5 cha-boo2-kia*2
chim-chhui3, ka7 in chiok-hok; chiu7 khi2-sin to3--khi3 ka-ki7 e5
soo2-chai7.


[32] Nga2-kok koh kia*5 i e5 loo7, Siong7-te3 e5 su3-chia2 tu2-tioh8 i.
2). Nga2-kok khoa*3-ki*3 in, chiu7 kong2, Che si7 Siong7-te3 e5
kun-tui7; soo2-i2 mia5 hit soo2-chai7 kio3 Ma2-khap-liam7.

3). Nga2-kok chhe lang5 tai7-seng khi3 Se-ji*2 e5 toe7, I2-tong e5
chhan5 ki*3 i e5 hia* I2-so3. 4). Hoan-hu3 in kong2, Lin2 ka7 goa2 e5
chu2 I2-so3 kong2, Li2 e5 loo5-pok8 Nga2-kok an2-ni kong2, Goa2 ti7
Lah8-pan hia kia3-ku, toa3 kau3 kin-a2-jit8. 5). goa2 u7 gu5, lu5,
iu*5-kun5, loo5-pok8, lu2-pi7; ta* chhe lang5 lai5 po3 goa2 e5 chu2, ai3
tit ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2. 6). Soo2 chhe e5 lang5
to3--lai5 Nga2-kok hia kong2, Goan2 kau3 li2 e5 hia* I2-so3 hia, i
tu2-tu2 teh lai5 beh ngia5-chih li2; koh u7 si3-pah lang5 kap i lai5.
7). Nga2-kok toa7 kia* koh peh-pak; chiong hiah-e5 kap i sa*-kap ti7-teh
e5 lang5, kap iu*5-kun5, gu5-kun5, lok8-to5, pun choe3 nng7 tui7; 8).
kong2, I2-so3 na7 lai5 kong-kek chit-tui7, chhun-e5 hit-tui7 iau2 thang
to5-chau2. 9). Nga2-kok koh kong2, Goa2 e5 choo2, A-pek-lah8-han2 e5
Siong7-te3, goa2 e5 pe7 I2-sat e5 Siong7-te3, Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, Li2 bat
tui3 goa2 kong2, To3-khi3 li2 e5 pun2-toe7 pun2-chok8, Goa2 beh ho2
khoan2-thai7 li2. 10). Li2 tui3 li2 e5 loo5-pok8 soo2 si it-chhe3 e5
chu5-ai3 kap it-chhe3 e5 seng5-sit8, chiu7 chi3-bi5-soe3 e5, goa2 ia7
boe7 kham-tit tit-tioh8; goa2 cheng5 kiah8 goa2 e5 koai*2-a2, ke3 chit
e5 Iok-tan3 ho5; ta* goa2 i2-keng chia*5-choe3 nng7-tui7. 11). Kiu5 Li2
kiu3 goa2 thoat-li7 goa2 e5 hia* I2-so3 e5 chhiu2; in-ui7 goa2 kia* i,
kia*-liau2 i lai5 thai5-si2 goa2 kap in bu2-kia*2. 12). Li2 ia7 bat
kong2, Goa2 tek-khak beh ho2 khoan2-thai7 li2; hoo7 li2 e5 hoo7-e3
chhin-chhiu*7 hai2-pi* e5 soa, choe7 kau3 boe7-sng3-tit. 13). Hit-mi5
Nga2-kok hioh ti7-hia; chiu7 ti7 i soo2 u7 e5 mih8 e5 lai7-bin7,
keng2-chhut le2-mih8, beh sang3 i e5 hia* I2-so3; 14). soa*-iu*5-bu2
nng7-pah chiah, soa*-iu*5-kang ji7-chap8 chiah, mi5-iu*5-bu2 nng7-pah
chiah, mi5-iu*5-kang ji7-chap8 chiah; 15). lok8-to5-bu2 kap chiah8-ni e5
kia*2 sa*-chap8 chiah, gu5-bu2 si3-chap8 chiah, gu5-kang2 chap8 chiah,
lu5-bu2 ji7-chap8 chiah, lu5-kia*2 chap8-chiah. 16). Kok-iu*7 leng7-goa7
chit8-kun5, kau-tai3 loo5-pok8; ka7 loo5-pok8 kong2, Lin2 tai7-seng goa2
khi3, hoo7 tak8-kun5 u7 sa*-li7. 17). Koh hoan-hu3 choe3-thau5--e5,
kong2, Goa2 e5 hia* I2-so3 tu2-tioh8 li2 e5 si5, na7 mng7 li2 kong2, Li2
si7 sim2-mih8 lang5 e5? beh khi3 tah-loh8? li2 thau5-cheng5 hiah-e5
chi7-chui7 e5? 18). li2 tioh8 kong2, Si7 li2 e5 loo5-pok8 Nga2-kok e5;
si7 beh sang3 goa2 e5 chu2 I2-so3 e5 le2-mih8; hian7-chai7 i pun2-sin
iah8 ti7 goan2 e5 au7-bin7. 19). Koh hoan-hu3 te7-ji7 te7-sa*, kap
it-chhe3 koa*2 kui-kun5 cheng-si* e5 lang5, kong2, Lin2 tu2-tioh8 I2-so3
e5 si5, iah8 tioh8 chiau3 an2-ni ka7 i kong2. 20). Koh lin2 iah8 tioh8
kong2, Li2 e5 loo5-pok8 Nga2-kok ti7 goan2 e5 au7-bin7. In-ui7 Nga2-kok
ka-ki7 phah-sng3 kong2, Goa2 eng7 ti7 goa2 thau5-cheng5 khi3 e5 le2-mih8
lai5 koe2 i e5 hun7; jian5-au7 goa2 ki*3-tioh8 i e5 bin7, kiam2-chhai2 i
chiap-lap8 goa2. 21). Tui3 an2-ni, le2-mih8 seng kia*5; hit-mi5 Nga2-kok
hioh ti7 tui7-tiong.

22). I mi5--si5 khi2-lai5, chhoa7 i nng7 e5 boo2, nng7 e5 lu2-pi7, kap
chap8-it e5 kia*2, long2 ke3 Nga2-pok8 e5 too7-thau5. 23). Tai7-seng
hoo7 in ke3-khoe; hoan7 soo2-u7--e5 iah8 hoo7 in ke3. 24). Chi2-u7 chhun
Nga2-kok ka-ki7 ti7-teh; u7 chit8-lang5 lai5 kap i sa*-ian2, kau3 ti7
thi*-phu2-kng. 25). Hit-lang5 khoa*3 boe7 ia*5--i; chiu7 sian3 Nga2-kok
e5 toa7-thui2-khu7; sa*-ian2 e5 si5, Nga2-kok e5 toa7-thui2-khu7
choah8-tioh8. 26). Hit-lang5 kong2, Thi* beh kng lah, tioh8 pang3 goa2
khi3. Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 na7 bo5 ka7 goa2 chiok-hok, m7 pang3 li2 khi3.
27). Hit-lang5 kong2, Li2 mia5 choe3 sim2-mih8? i kong2, Goa2 mia5 choe3
Nga2-kok. 28). Hit-lang5 kong2, Li2 e5 mia5 bo5 beh koh kio3 Nga2-kok,
beh kio3-choe3 I2-sek-liat8; in-ui7 li2 kap Siong7-te3 kap lang5 tau3
su-ia*5, long2 tit-tioh8 khah-ia*5. 29). Nga2-kok mng7 i kong2, Chhia*2
chiong li2 e5 mia5 ka7 goa2 kong2. hit lang5 in3 kong2, Mih-sai2 mng7
goa2 e5 mia5? chiu7 ti7-hia ka7 i chiok-hok. 30). Nga2-kok mia5 Hit
soo2-chai7 kio3 Pian7-i2-li7, in-ui7 kong2, Goa2 tng-thau5 tui3-bin7
ki*3-tioh8 Siong7-te3, goa2 e5 si*3-mia7 iau2 tit-tioh8 po2-choan5. 31).
Jit8 tu2-a2 chhut, Nga2-kok keng-ke3 Pian7-i2-li7; i e5 toa7-thui2
i2-keng pai2. 32). Soo2-i2 chiah e5 I2-sek-liat8 lang5 bo5 chiah8
toa7-thui2-thau5 e5 kun, kau3 ti7 kin-a2-jit8; in-ui7 hit-lang5 sian3
Nga2-kok thui2-khu7 e5 toa7-kun.


[33] Nga2-kok kiah8-bak8 khoa*3; khoa*3-ki*3 I2-so3 lai5; koh u7 si3-pah
lang5 kap i lai5. I chiu7 chiong hiah e5 gin2-a2 pun-khui, kau hoo7
Li7-a, kau hoo7 Lah8-kiat, kau hoo7 nng7 e5 lu2-pi7. 2). Chiong lu2-pi7
kap in e5 kia*2 pai5 ti7 thau5-cheng5, Li2-a kap i e5 kia*2 pai5 ti7
au7-bin7, Lah8-kiat kap Iok-sek pai5 ti7 loo7-be2. 3). I pun2-sin ti7 in
e5 thau5-cheng5 ke3--khi3, lian5-lian5 chhit-pai2 phak ti7 toe7--nih,
chiah oa2-kun7 i e5 hia*. 4). I2-so3 chau2-lai5 ngia5-chih i, chiong i
pho7--teh, koh lam2 i e5 am7-kun2, chim i; nng7-lang5 chiu7 thi5-khau3.
5). I2-so3 kiah8-bak8 khoa*3-ki*3 hu7-jin5-lang5 kap gin2-a2, chiu7
kong2, Chiah-e5 kap li2 tang5-kia*5--e5 si7 chi7-chui7? Nga2-kok kong2,
Chiah e5 gin2-a2 si7 Siong7-te3 si-un hoo7 li2 e5 loo5-pok8--e5. 6).
Tui3 hit-tiap8 nng7 e5 lu2-pi7, kap in e5 gin2-a2, chin3-cheng5 lai5
pai3. 7). Li7-a kap i e5 gin2-a2 iah8 chin3-cheng5 lai5 pai3; loo7-be2
Iok-sek kap Lah8-kiat iah8 chin3-cheng5 lai5 pai3. 8). I2-so3 kong2,
Goa2 soo2 tu2-tioh8 kui-kun5 e5 cheng-si*, li2 si7 sim2-mih8 i3-su3?
Nga2-kok kong2, Si7 beh ti7 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8
un-tian2. 9). I2-so3 kong2, Sio2-ti7 ah, goa2-e5 i2-keng kau3-giah8,
li2-e5 iu5-gôan kui li2. 10). Nga2-kok kong2, Boh8 an2-ni, goa2 na7 ti7
li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, kiu5 li2 tui3 goa2 e5 chhiu2 siu
goa2 e5 le2-mih8; in-ui7 goa2 ki*3-tioh8 li2 e5 bin7, chhin-chhiu*7
ki*3-tioh8 Siong7-te3 e5 bin7, li2 iah8 chiap-lap8 goa2; 11). kiu5 li2
siu goa2 toa3--lai5 hoo7 li2 e5 le2-mih8; in-ui7 Siong7-te3 un-tian2
goa2, hoo7 goa2 chhiong-chiok; pek--i, jian5-au7 siu. 12). I2-so3 kong2,
Lan2 khi2-sin lai5 khi3, goa2 choe3-thau5 kia*5. 13). Nga2-kok tui3 i
kong2, goa2 e5 chu2 chai chiah e5 gin2-a2 nng2-chia*2, gu5-iu*5 iah8
tu2-a2 si*; na7 choe3 chit8-jit8 koa*2, kui-kun5 long2 beh si2. 14).
Kiu5 goa2 e5 chu2 ti7 loo5-pok8 e5 thau5-cheng5 kia*5, goa2 beh chiau3
ti7 goa2 bin7-cheng5 kui-kun5 cheng-si* e5 lek8-liong7, iah8 chiau3
gin2-a2 e5 lek8-liong7, ban7-ban7 chin3-cheng5, kia*5 kau3 Se-ji*2, kau3
goa2 e5 chu2 hia. 15). I2-so3 kong2, Iong5-un2 goa2 chiong te3 goa2 e5
lang5 lau5 kui2-e5 kap li2 choe3-tin7. Nga2-kok kong2, Mih-sai2 an2-ni?
ti7 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2 chiu7 ho2. 16).
Hit-jit8 I2-so3 khi2-sin, chiau3 gôan-loo7 to3--khi3 Se-ji*2. 17).
Nga2-kok kia*5 kau3 Soo3-kat, ti7-hia ui7 pun2-sin khi2-chhu3, ui7
cheng-si* tah chhau2-liau5; soo2-i2 mia5 hit soo2-chai7 choe3 Soo3-kat.

18). Nga2-kok tui3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 to3--lai5 e5 si5, peng5-an kau3
Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 Si7-kiam3 sia*5; ti7 sia*5 e5 bin7-cheng5 tah poo3-pi*5.
19). Eng7 chit8-pah te3 gun5, tui3 Si7-kiam3 e5 lau7-pe7 Hap-boat e5
kia*2-sun, boe2 i tah poo3-pi*5 hit te3 toe7; 20). ti7-hia khi2 chit8
cho7 toa*5, ka7 i ho7 mia5 kio3 I-li7 I-lo5-i I2-sek-liat8.


[34] Li7-a ka7 Nga2-kok soo2 si* e5 cha-boo2-kia*2, Ti2-na2, chhut-khi3
beh ki*3 hit soo2-chai7 e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2. 2). Hit soo2-chai7 e5
bok8-pek Hi-bi7 lang5 Hap-boat e5 kia*2 Si7-kiam3 khoa*3-ki*3 i; chiu7
khiu2--i, kap i sa*-kap khun3, leng5-jiok8 i. 3). I e5 sim loan5-boo7
Nga2-kok e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 Ti2-na2; thia*3 chit e5 cha-boo2-kia*2, eng7
ho2-oe7 an-ui3 i. 4). Si7-kiam3 ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 Hap-boat, kong2, Kiu5
li2 ka7 goa2 pheng3 chit e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 choe3-boo2. 5). Nga2-kok
thia*-ki*3 i phah la5-sam5 i e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 Ti2-na2; hit-si5 i hiah
e5 kia*2 kap i e5 cheng-si* ti7 soa*--nih; Nga2-kok cheng7-cheng7 bo5
choe3 sia*, theng3-hau7 in to3-lai5. 6). Si7-kiam3 e5 lau7-pe7,
Hap-boat, chhut-lai5 ki*3 Nga2-kok, beh kap i kong2-oe7. 7). Nga2-kok
hiah e5 kia*2 thia*-ki*3 chit e5 tai7-chi3, chiu7 tui3 soa*-nih
to3--lai5, tak8-e5 m7 kam-goan7, chap8-hun siu7-khi3; in-ui7 Si7-kiam3
ti7 I2-sek-liat8 choe3 chhut kian3-siau3 e5 tai7-chi3, kap Nga2-kok e5
cha-boo2-kia*2 sa*-kap khun3; che pun2 si7 m7 eng-kai choe3 e5 su7. 8).
Hap-boat kap in chham-siong5 kong2, Goa2 e5 kia*2 Si7-kiam3 e5 sim
him-boo7 lin2 e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2; kiu5 lin2 chiong i hoo7 goa2 e5 kia*2
choe3-boo2. 9). Lin2 kap goan2 tai7-ke kiat-chhin; lin2 thang chiong
lin2 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 hoo7 goan2, lin2 iah8 thang chhoa7 goan2 e5
cha-boo2-kia*2. 10). Lin2 kap goan2 sa*-kap khia7-khi3; toe7 ti7 lin2 e5
bin7-cheng5, lin2 toa3 chia khia7, choe3 seng-li2, kian3-ti3 san2-giap8.
11). Si7-kiam3 tui3 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 e5 lau7-pe7 kap i e5 hia*-ti7
kong2, Goan7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2; lin2 soo2 tui3
goa2 kong2--e5 goa2 beh hoo7 lin2. 12). Chhut-chai7 lin2 beh tui3 goa2
tho2 joa7-choe7 pheng3-kim, kap le2-mih8, goa2 tek-khak chiau3 lin2 soo2
kong2--e5 hoo7 lin2; chi2-u7 ai3 lin2 eng7 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 hoo7 goa2
choe3-boo2. 13). Nga2-kok hiah e5 kia*2, in-ui7 Si7-kiam3 phah la5-sam5
in e5 sio2-be7 Ti2-na2, chiu7 eng7 kan-cha3 e5 oe7 lai5 in3 Si7-kiam3,
kap i e5 lau7-pe7, Hap-boat, tui3 in kong2, 14). Chiong goan2 e5
sio2-be7 hoo7 bo5 siu7 kat-le2 e5 lang5 choe3-boo2, che e5 tai7-chi3
goan2 boe7-choe3-tit; in-ui7 he si7 goan2 e5 kian3-siau3. 15). Lin2 soo2
u7 e5 ta-poo-lang5, na7 long2 siu7 kat-le2 chhin-chhiu*7 goan2
chit8-iu*7, u7 chi2 chit8-hang7 chiah thang eng3-un2 lin2; 16). goan2
chiu7 chiong goan2 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 hoo7 lin2, goan2 iah8 chhoa7 lin2
e5 cha-boo2-kia*2; goan2 chiu7 kap lin2 sa*-kap toa3, chia*5-choe3 chit8
e5 peh-si*3. 17). Siat-su2 lin2 m7-thia* goan2 e5 oe7 lai5 siu7 kat-le2,
goan2 chiu7 toa3 goan2 e5 sio2-be7 lai5 khi3. 18). Hap-boat kap i e5
kia*2 Si7-kiam3, hoa*-hi2 in e5 oe7. 19). Hit e5 siau3-lian5 lang5 choe3
chit e5 tai7-chi3, long2 bo5 ian5-chhian5; in-ui7 i thia*3 Nga2-kok e5
cha-boo2-kia*2; koh i ti7 in lau7-pe7 e5 ke te7-it chun-kui3. 20).
Hap-boat, kap i e5 kia*2 Si7-kiam3, lai5 kau3 pun2-sia*5 e5 mng5-khau2,
ka7 pun2-sia*5 e5 lang5 kong2, Chiah e5 lang5 kap lan2 ho5-ho2;
m7-tat8--tioh8 chun2 in ti7 chit e5 toe7 khia7-khi2, choe3 seng-li2; koh
chit e5 toe7 iah8 khui-khoah, oe7 iong5-un2--tit in; lan2 thang chhoa7
in e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 choe3-boo2, iah8 thang chiong lan2 e5
cha-boo2-kia*2 ke3 hoo7 in. 22). Tok8-tok8 tioh8 u7 chit8-hang7, hiah-e5
chiah beh un2 lan2, kap lan2 khia7-khi2, chia*5-choe3 chit8 e5 peh-si*3;
chiu7-si7 lan2 tiong-kan soo2 u7 e5 ta-poo-lang5 long2 tioh8 siu7
kat-le2, chhin-chhiu*7 in siu7 kat-le2 chit8-iu*7. 23). I e5 gu5,
chai5-san2, kap it-chhe3 e5 cheng-si*, kiam2 bo5 long2 kui ti7 lan2 mah?
chi2-u7 tioh8 un2--in, in chiu7 beh kap lan2 toa3. 24). Ki*3-na7 tui3
sia*5-mng5 chhut-lai5 e5 lang5 long2 thia*-than3 Hap-boat kap i e5 kia*2
Si7-kiam3 e5 oe7; tui3 an2-ni ki*3-na7 tui3 sia*5-mng5 chhut-lai5 e5
ta-poo-lang5 long2 siu7 kat-le2. 25). Kau3 te7-sa* jit8, cheng3-lang5
tng teh thang3-thia*3 e5 si5, Nga2-kok nng7 e5 kia*2, chiu7-si7 Ti2-na2
e5 hia* Se-bian7 kap Li7-bi7, long2 kiah8-to, than3 lang5 bo5 tiu*-ti5,
lai5 kau3 sia*5-lai7, thai5-si2 long2-chong2 e5 ta-poo-lang5. 26). Ia7
eng7 to thai5-si2 Hap-boat kap i e5 kia*2 Si7-kiam3; chhoa7 Ti2-na2 tui3
Si7-kiam3 e5 chhu3 chhut-lai5, chiu7 khi3. 27). Nga2-kok hiah e5 kia*2,
ui7-tioh8 in sio2-be7 siu7 phah la5-sam5, chiu7 lai5 kau3 siu7-thai5 e5
lang5 hia, chhiu*2-kiap in e5 sia*5. 28). Chhiu*2 in e5 iu*5-kun5,
gu5-kun5, kap lu5; i2-kip8 sia*5-lai7 kap chhan5--nih soo2 u7 e5. 29).
Koh chiong in it-chhe3 e5 he3-mih8 chi*5-chai5, it-chhe3 e5 gin2-a2 kap
hu7-jin5-lang5, i2-kip8 tak8 te3 chhu3 soo2-u7--e5, long2 chhiu*2, liah8
chiu7 khi3. 30). Nga2-kok ka7 Se-bian7 kap Li7-bi7 kong2, Lin2
lian5-lui7 goa2, hoo7 goa2 ti7 chit soo2-chai7 khia7-khi2 e5 peh-si*3 e5
tiong-kan, chiu7-si7 ti7 Ka-lam5 lang5 kap Pi2-li7-se2 lang5 e5
tiong-kan u7 chhau3-mia5. Koh goa2 e5 lang5-giah8 chio2; in tek-khak
chu7-chip8 lai5 kong-kek goa2, phah goa2; goa2 kap choan5-ke e5 lang5
long2 oe7 biat8-bo5. 31). In kong2, I kiam2 thang khoan2-thai7 goan2
sio2-be7 chhin-chhiu*7 chhiong-ki mah?


[35] Siong7-te3 ka7 Nga2-kok kong2, Khi2--ah, chiu*7-khi3 Pek-tek8-li7,
toa3 ti7-hia. Koh tioh8 ti7-hia ka7 Siong7-te3 khi2 chit8 cho7 toa*5,
chiu7-si7 li2 siam2-pi7 li2 e5 hia* I2-so3 e5 bin7 e5 si5, tui3 li2
chhut-hian7--e5, hit-e5. 2). Nga2-kok chiu7 ka7 choan5-ke i2-kip8
it-chhe3 kap i ti7-teh e5 lang5 kong2, Lin2 tioh8 tu5-khi3 lin2
tiong-kan goa7-pang e5 siong7-te3; iah8 tioh8 ka-ki7 chheng-khi3, oa*7
lin2 e5 i-chiu*5. 3). Lan2 tioh8 khi2-lai5, chiu*7-khi3 Pek-tek8-li7;
ti7-hia goa2 beh ka7 Siong7-te3 khi2 chit8 cho7 toa*5; chiu7-si7 ti7
goa2 tu2-tioh8 hoan7-lan7 e5 jit8, un2-chun2 goa2 e5 ki5-to2, ti7 goa2
soo2 kia*5 e5 loo7 kap goa2 ti7-teh, hit-e5. 4). In chiu7 chiong in
chhiu2-lai7 soo2 u7 i*7-pang e5 sin5-beng5, kap in e5 hi7-kau, long2
hoo7 Nga2-kok; Nga2-kok chiong hiah-e5 tai5 ti7 Si7-kiam3 hit-ui7 e5
siong7-chhiu7-kha. 5). In chiu7 khi2-sin, Siong7-te3 hoo7 si3-chiu-ui5
e5 sia*5 e5 lang5 long2 chin kia*; in chiu7 bo5 tui-jip Nga2-kok e5
cheng3-kia*2. 6). Nga2-kok, i2-kip8 it-chhe3 kap i choe3-tin7 e5 lang5,
kau3 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 Loo7-su, chiu7-si7 Pek-tek8-li7. 7). I ti7-hia khi2
chit8 cho7 toa*5, chiu7 ka7 hit soo2-chai7 ho7-mia5, kio3
I-lek8-pek-tek8-li7; in-ui7 i siam2-pi7 i e5 hia* e5 si5, Siong7-te3
ti7-hia tui3 i chhut-hian7. 8). Li7-pek-ka e5 ni-bu2 Ti2-pho3-lat si2;
chiu7 bai5-chong3 ti7 Pek-tek8-li7 e5 e7-bin7, siong7-chhiu7-kha;
soo2-i2 kio3 i e5 mia5 A-lun5-pa-koo2.

9). Nga2-kok tui3 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 to3--lai5, Siong7-te3 koh tui3 i
chhut-hian7, su3-hok hoo7 i. 10). Siong7-te3 koh ka7 i kong2, Li2 mia5
si7 Nga2-kok; ta* i2-au7 li2 e5 mia5 bo5 koh kio3 Nga2-kok, beh mia5
kio3 I2-sek-liat8; chiu7 kio3 i e5 mia5 I2-sek-liat8. 11). Siong7-te3
koh ka7 i kong2, Goa2 si7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3; li2 tioh8
si*-thoa*3 choe7-choe7; chiong-lai5 u7 chit8-kok, koh u7 choe7-choe7
kok, tui3 li2 lai5 si*, koh u7 kun-ong5 tui3 li2 si*-chhut. 12). goa2
soo2 hoo7 A-pek-lah8-han2 kap I2-sat e5 toe7, Goa2 beh hoo7 li2, iah8
beh chiong chit e5 toe7 hoo7 li2 e5 hoo7-e3. 13). Siong7-te3 chiu7 tui3
kap i kong2-oe7 e5 soo2-chai7 chiu*7-khi3. 14). Nga2-kok chiu7 ti7
Siong7-te3 kap i kong2-oe7 e5 soo2-chai7, khia7 chit8 ki thiau7,
chiu7-si7 chioh8-thiau7; ti7 hit teng2-bin7 koan3-tian3 to3-iu5. 15).
Nga2-kok chiu7 chheng Siong7-te3 kap i kong2-oe7 e5 soo2-chai7, mia5
choe3 Pek-tek8-li7. 16). In tui3 Pek-tek8-li7 khi2-sin; li7-khui
I2-hoat-tha iau2 u7 chit8 cham7 e5 loo7; Lah8-kiat tit-beh si* lim5-san2
kan-lan5. 17). Tng i kan-khoo2 si* e5 si5, khioh-chia2 tui3 i kong2,
M7-bian2 kia*, li2 ta* beh koh tit-tioh8 chit8 e5 kia*2. 18). I khui3
beh tng7, lim5-chiong e5 si5, chiu7 kio3 i e5 kia*2 e5 mia5
Pian7-go5-ni5; i e5 lau7-pe7 ka7 i ho7-mia5 Pian7-nga2-bin2. 19).
Lah8-kiat si2, bai5-chong3 ti7 khi3 I2-hoat-tha e5 loo7; I2-hoat-tha
chiu7-si7 Pek-li7-heng5. 20). Nga2-kok khia7 thiau7 ti7 i e5
bong7-teng2; chit e5 thiau7 chiu7-si7 Lah8-kiat e5 bong7-pai5; kau3
kin-a2-jit8 iau2 ti7-teh. 21). I2-sek-liat8 koh khi2-sin khi3, ti7
I2-tek-tai5 tah poo3-pi*5. 22). I2-sek-liat8 toa3 ti7 hit soo2-chai7 e5
si5, Liu5-pian7 khi3 kap i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 soe3-i5, Phek-lah8, sa*-kap
khun3; I2-sek-liat8 iah8 thia*.

23). Nga2-kok kiong7 u7 chap8-ji7 e5 kia*2, Li7-a e5 kia*2, chiu7-si7
Nga2-kok e5 toa7-kia*2 Liu5-pian7, i2-kip8 Se-bian7, Li7-bi7, Iu5-tai7,
I2-sat-ka, Se-poo3-lun5; 24). Lah8-kiat e5 kia*2, chiu7-si7 Iok-sek,
Pian7-nga2-bin2; 25). Lah8-kiat e5 lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8 soo2 si* e5 kia*2,
chiu7-si7 Tan3 kap Na2-hut-tha-li7; 26). Li7-a e5 lu2-pi7 Sek-pha*3 soo2
si* e5 kia*2 Ka-tek, A-siat; che si7 Nga2-kok ti7 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 soo2
si* e5 kia*2. 27). Nga2-kok lai5 ki*3 i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat ti7 Ban7-li7,
kau3 Ki-liat8-a-pa, chiu7-si7 Hi-pek-lun5, A-pek-lah8-han2 kap I2-sat
bat kia3-ku e5 soo2-chai7.

28). I2-sat hiong2-siu7 chit8-pah poeh-chap8 he3; 29). I2-sat ni5-he3
lau7, jit8-chi2 moa2-chiok, khui3 tng7 lai5 si2, to3--khi3 i e5
liat8-choo2 hia; i nng7 e5 kia*2 I2-so3, Nga2-kok, ka7 i bai5-chong3.


[36] I2-so3 chiu7-si7 I2-tong, i e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2. I2-so3
chhoa7 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 cha-boo2-gin2-a2 choe3-boo2; chiu7-si7 Hek-lang5
I2-lun5 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 A-tai7, kap Hi-bi7 lang5 che3-pian7 e5
cha-boo2-sun, A-na2 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2, A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2. 3). Koh chhoa7
I2-sit8-ma2-li7 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2, Ni5-pai5-iok e5 chi2-be7,
Pa-sit8-boat. 4). A-tai7 ka7 I2-so3 si* I2-li7-hoat; Pa-sit8-boat si*
Liu5-ji*2; 5). A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2 si* Ia5-oo-si, Nga2-lan5, Kho2-lah8; che
long2 si7 I2-so3 e5 kia*2, ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 si*--e5. 6). I2-so3 toa3 i
e5 boo2, kia*2, cha-boo2-kia*2, kap ke-lai7 long2-chong2 e5 lang5,
i2-kip8 gu5, iu*5, kap it-chhe3 e5 cheng-si*, it-chhe3 e5 chai5-but8,
chiu7-si7 i ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 soo2 tit-tioh8--e5, khi3 pat8 soo2-chai7,
li7-khui i e5 sio2-ti7 Nga2-kok. 7). In-ui7 nng7-lang5 soo2-u7--e5
chin-choe7, boe7 thang sa*-kap khia7; koh in-ui7 in e5 gu5, iu*5 choe7,
soo2 kia3-kha e5 soo2-chai7 boe7 iong5-un2--tit. 8). Tui3 an2-ni I2-so3
toa3 ti7 Se-ji*2 soa*. I2-so3 chiu7-si7 I2-tong.

9). I2-so3 e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2: I2-so3 chiu7-si7 Se-ji*2 soa*
I2-tong lang5 e5 choo2; 10). I2-so3 chiah e5 kia*2 e5 mia5 ki3 ti7
e7-toe2, I2-so3 e5 boo2 A-tai7 e5 kia*2 I2-li7-hoat, I2-so3 e5 boo2
Pa-sit8-boat e5 kia*2 Liu5-ji*2. 11). I2-li7-hoat e5 kia*2; The5-ban7,
O-boat, Se2-pho, Ka-than2, Ki-lap8-su; 12). Teng5-lap8 si7 I2-so3 e5
kia*2 I2-li7-hoat e5 soe2-i5, i ka7 I2-li7-hoat si* A-ma2-lek8; che si7
I2-so3 e5 boo2 A-tai7 e5 kia*2-sun. 13). Liu5-ji*2 e5 kia*2 Na2-hap,
Sia7-lah8, Sa-ma2, Bi2-sat; chiah-e5 si7 I2-so3 e5 boo2 Pa-sit8-boat e5
kia*2-sun. 14). I2-so3 e5 boo2 A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2 si7 Che3-pian7 e5
cha-boo2-sun, A-na2 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2; i ka7 I2-so3 si* Ia5-oo-si,
Nga2-lan5, Kho2-lah8.

15). I2-so3 e5 kia*2 soo2 si* choe3 chok8-tiu*2--e5, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2;
I2-so3 e5 toa7-kia*2 I2-li7-hoat e5 kia*2, u7 The5-ban7 chok8-tiu*2,
O-boat chok8-tiu*2, Se2-pho chok8-tiu*2, Ki-lap8-su chok8-tiu*2, 16).
Kho2-lah8 chok8-tiu*2, Ka-than2 chok8-tiu*2, A-ma2-lek8 chok8-tiu*2;
chiah-e5 si7 ti7 I2-tong toe7, I2-li7-hoat soo2 si* e5 chok8-tiu*2, si7
A-tai7 e5 kia*2-sun. 17). I2-so3 e5 kia*2-sun Liu5-ji*2 e5 kia*2, u7
Na2-hap chok8-tiu*2, Sia7-lah8 chok8-tiu*2, Sa-ma2 chok8-tiu*2, Bi2-sat
chok8-tiu*2; che si7 ti7 I2-tong toe7, tui3 Liu5-ji*2 soo2 chhut e5
chok8-tiu*2, long2 si7 I2-so3 e5 boo2 Pa-sit8-boat e5 kia*2-sun. 18).
I2-so3 e5 boo2 A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2 e5 kia*2, u7 Ia5-oo-si chok8-tiu*2,
Nga2-lan5 chok8-tiu*2, Kho2-lah8 chok8-tiu*2; che si7 tui3 I2-so3 e5
boo2, A-na2 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2, soo2 chhut e5
chok8-tiu*2. 19). Chiah-e5 si7 I2-so3 e5 kia*2-sun, koh chiah-e5 si7 in
e5 chok8-tiu*2; I2-so3 chiu7-si7 I2-tong.

20). Hit soo2-chai7 e5 pun2-toe7 lang5, chiu7-si7 Ho5-li7 lang5 Se-ji*2
e5 kia*2-sun, ki3 e7-toe2; chiu7-si7 Lo5-tan, Sok-pa, Che3-pian7, A-na2,
Ti2-sun7, I2-chhat, Ti2-san; 21). chiah-e5 si7 tui3 I2-tong toe7 e5
Ho5-li7 lang5, Se-ji*2 kia*2-sun-tiong soo2 chhut e5 chok8-tiu*2. 22).
Lo5-tan e5 kia*2 si7 Ho5-li7, Hi-ban7; Lo5-tan e5 chi2-be7 si7
Teng5-lap8. 23). Sok-pa e5 kia*2 si7 A-lek8-bun5, Ma2-na2-hat,
I2-pa-liok8, Si7-pho, O-lam5. 24). Che3-pian7 e5 kia*2; A-nga2, A-na2;
tng-si5 teh chhi7 in lau7-pe7 Che3-pian7 e5 lu5, ti7 khong3-ia2
chhe7-tioh8 un-choa*5--e5, chiu7-si7 chit e5 A-na2. 25). A-na2 e5 kia*2
si7 Ti2-sun7; A-na2 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 si7 A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2. 26).
Ti2-sun7 e5 kia*2 si7 Him-tan3, I-si7-pan, Ek-lan5, Ki-lan5. 27).
I2-chhat e5 kia*2 si7 Phek-han2, Sat-hoan, A-kan. 28). Ti2-san e5 kia*2
si7 OO-su, A-lan5. 29). Tui3 Ho5-li7 lang5 soo2 chhut e5 chok8-tiu*2,
ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; chiu7-si7 Lo5-tan chok8-tiu*2, Sok-pa chok8-tiu*2,
Che3-pian7 chok8-tiu*2, A-na2 chok8-tiu*2, 30). Ti2-sun7 chok8-tiu*2,
I2-chhat chok8-tiu*2, Ti2-san chok8-tiu*2. Chiah-e5 si7 tui3 Ho5-li7
lang5 soo2 chhut e5 chok8-tiu*2, long2 ti7 Se-ji*2 toe7 choe3 chok8-tiu*2.

31). Tng I2-sek-liat8 lang5 be7 u7 kun-ong5 ti7-li2 e5 tai7-seng, ti7
I2-tong toe7 choe3 ong5 lai5 ti7-li2--e5 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2. 32). Pi2-ji*2
e5 kia*2, Pi2-lah8, ti7 I2-tong choe3 ong5; i e5 kia*-sia*5 mia5 kio3
Teng5-hap-pa. 33). Pi2-lah8 si2-liau2, Pho-su-lah8 lang5 Sia7-lah8 e5
kia*2, Iok-pa, soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5. 34). Iok-pa si2, The5-ban7 toe7
e5 lang5 Hoo7-san soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5. 35). Hoo7-san si2, Pi2-tat8
e5 kia*2 Hap-tat8, soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5; i chiu7-si7 ti7 Moo5-ap toe7
thai5-ia*5 Bi2-tian5 lang5--e5. I e5 kia*-sia*5 mia5 kio3 A-bi7-tek.
36). Hap-tat8 si2, Ma2-su7-li7-ka lang5 Song-lah8 soa3-chiap i choe3
ong5. 37). Song-lah8 si2-liau2, Ho5-pi* e5 Li7-ho5-pek lang5 So3-lo5
soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5. 38). So3-lo5 si2, A-kek-pho e5 kia*2,
Pa-lek8-hap-lam5, soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5. 39). A-kek-pho e5 kia*2
Pa-lek8-hap-lam5 si2, Hap-tat8 soa3-chiap i choe3 ong5; i e5 kia*-sia*5
mia5-kio3 Pa-oo; i e5 boo2 mia5-kio3 Bi2-hi-tha-piat, si7 Bi2-sat-hap8
e5 cha-boo2-sun, Ma2-tek-liat8 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2.

40). Tui3 I2-so3 soo2 chhut e5 chok8-tiu*2, chiau3 in e5 chong-chok8,
soo2-chai7, mia5-ji7, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; chiu7-si7 Teng5-lap8 chok8-tiu*2,
A-lek8-oa2 chok8-tiu*2, Ia5-thiap chok8-tiu*2; 41). A-ho5-li7-pa-ma2
chok8-tiu*2, I2-lah8 chok8-tiu*2, Pi2-lun3 chok8-tiu*2; 42). Ki-lap8-su
chok8-tiu*2, The5-ban7 chok8-tiu*2, Bi2-pi2-sat chok8-tiu*2; 43).
Ma2-ki-tiap8 chok8-tiu*2, I2-lan5 chok8-tiu*2; chiah-e5 si7 I2-tong e5
chok8-tiu*2, chiau3 in khia7-khi2 e5 soo2-chai7, ti7 soo2 tit-tioh8
choe3-giap8 e5 toe7. Chit-e5 si7 I2-tong lang5 e5 choo2, chiu7-si7 I2-so3.


[37] Nga2-kok khia7-khi2 Ka-lam5 toe7, chiu7-si7 i e5 lau7-pe7 kia3-kha
e5 soo2-chai7. 2). Nga2-kok e5 se3-he7 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2. Iok-sek
chap8-chhit he3 kap i hiah e5 hia* sa*-kap koo3 iu*5; i si7 chit8 e5
gin2-a2 kap i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 soe3-i5 Phek-lah8 e5 kia*2, Sek-pha*3 e5
kia*2, siong5-siong5 choe3-tin7; Iok-sek chiong i hiah e5 hia* e5 phai*2
phin2-heng7 ka7 in lau7-pe7 kong2. 3). Ta* I2-sek-liat8 thia*3 Iok-sek
khah ia*5-ke3 ti7 thia*3 i e5 cheng3-kia*2, in-ui7 Iok-sek si7 i
ni5-lau7 si*--e5; i ka7 i choe3 chit8 nia2 chhai2-sek e5 sa*. 4).
Iok-sek hiah e5 hia* khoa*3-ki*3 lau7-pe7 thia*3 Iok-sek, ke3-thau5 ti7
thia*3 in; chiu7 oan3-hun7 Iok-sek, boe7-oe7 kap i kong2 ho5-bok8 e5 oe7.

5). Iok-sek bang7-ki*3 chit8 e5 bang7, ka7 i hiah e5 hia* kong2; in
chiu7 koh-khah oan3-hun7 i. 6). Iok-sek tui3 in kong2, Chhia*2 lin2
thia* goa2 soo2 bang7-ki*3 e5 bang7. 7). Lan2 ti7 hng5--nih ha5
goo7-kak; goa2 soo2-ha5--e5 khi2-lai5 khia7, lin2 soo2-ha5--e5 ui5-lui5
lai5 pai3 goa2 soo2 ha5--e5. 8). I e5 hia* in3 kong2, Chong2-bo5 li2
chin-chia*3 beh choe3 goan2 e5 ong5 mah? chin-chia*3 beh koan2-hat goan2
mah? In chiu7 ui7-tioh8 i e5 bang7, kap i e5 oe7, koh-khah oan3-hun7 i.
9). Au7-lai5 i koh bang7-ki*3 chit8 e5 bang7, iah8 ka7 i e5 hia* kong2,
Li2 khoa*3, goa2 iu7-koh bang7-ki*3 chit8 e5 bang7; u7 jit8, geh8, kap
chap8-it liap8 chhi* teh pai3 goa2. 10). Iok-sek ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 kap i
e5 hia* kong2; in lau7-pe7 chiu7 chek-pi7 i, kong2, Li2 soo2 bang7-ki*3
chit e5 bang7 si7 chai*2-iu*7? chong2-bo5 goa2 kap lin2 lau7-bu2 lin2
hia*-ti7, long2 beh phak-teh pai3 li2 mah? 11). I e5 hia* long2
oan3-too3 i; i e5 lau7-pe7 eng7 chiah e5 oe7 ki3 ti7 sim-lai7.

12). Iok-sek e5 hia* khi3 Si7-kiam3, chhi7 lau7-pe7 e5 iu*5. 13).
I2-sek-liat8 tui3 Iok-sek kong2, Lin2 hia* kiam2 m7-si7 ti7 Si7-kiam3
chhi7 iu*5 mah? Li2 lai5, goa2 beh chhe li2 khi3 in hia. 14). I in3
kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia. I ka7 i kong2, Li2 khi3 khoa*3 lin2 hia* u7
peng5-an a2-bo5, iu*5-kun5 u7 peng5-an a2-bo5; to3--lai5 ka7 goa2 kong2.
Chiu7 chhe i chhut Hi-pek-lun5 e5 soa*-kok; i chiu7 khi3 kau3 Si7-kiam3.
15). U7 lang5 tng7--tioh8 i ti7 soa*--nih be5-loo7; chiu7 mng7 i kong2,
Li2 teh chhe7 sim2-mih8? 16). I kong2, Goa2 teh chhe7 goa2 e5 hia*;
chhia*2 ka7 goa2 kong2, in ti7 tah-loh8 teh chhi7 iu*5. 17). Hit-lang5
kong2, In i2-keng li7-khui chia; in-ui7 goa2 thia*-ki*3 in teh kong2,
Lan2 lai5-khi3 To-tan. Iok-sek chiu7 khi3 jip i e5 hia*, tu2-tioh8 in
ti7 To-tan. 18). In hng7-hng7 khoa*3-ki*3 i, i iau2-be7 kia*5 kau3 in
hia, in chiu7 sa*-kap ke3-boo5 beh hai7-si2 i. 19). Tai7-ke sa*-kap
kong2, Li2 khoa*3, choe3-bang7--e5 lai5--lah. 20). Hoo3--lai5, ta* lan2
ka7 i thai5-si2, hiat ti7 chit8 e5 ta-chi*2; chiah lai5 kong2 u7
phai*2-siu3 chiah8--i; lan2 chiah khoa*3 i e5 bang7 chiong-lai5
chai*2-iu*7. 21). Liu5-pian7 thia*-ki*3, chiu7 kiu3 i thoat-li7 in e5
chhiu2; kong2, Lan2 m7-thang hai7 i e5 si*3-mia7. 22). Liu5-pian7 koh
tui3 in kong2, M7-thang hoo7 i lau5-huih; thang ka7 i hiat ti7 chit e5
khong3-ia2 e5 ta-chi*2, m7-thang he7 chhiu2 hai7 i; i3-su3 si7 beh kiu3
i thoat-li7 in e5 chhiu2, hoo7 i to3--khi3 i e5 lau7-pe7 hia. 23).
Iok-sek kau3 i e5 hia* hia, hit-tiap8 in chiu7 thng3 Iok-sek e5
goa7-sa*, chiu7-si7 i seng-khu hit-nia2 chhai2-sek e5 sa*; chiu7 liah8
i, hiat-loh8 chi*2, hit e5 chi*2 si7 ta--e5, lai7-bin7 bo5 chui2.

25). In che7-teh chiah8-pia*2; kiah8-bak8 khoa*3, khoa*3-ki*3 chit8-tin7
I2-sit8-ma2-li7 lang5 tui3 Ki-liat8 lai5; eng7 lok8-to5 pe7 hiu*-liau7,
ju2-hiu*, but8-ioh8, beh toa3 loh8--khi3 Ai-kip8. 26). Iu5-tai7 tui3
chiah e5 hia*-ti7 kong2, Lan2 thai5-si2 lan2 e5 sio2-ti7, khng3-bat8 i
e5 huih, u7 sim2-mih8 li7-ek? 27). Lan2 lai5 ka7 i boe7 hoo7
I2-sit8-ma2-li7 lang5; m7-thang he7-chhiu2 hai7 i; in-ui7 i si7 lan2 e5
sio2-ti7, lan2 e5 kut-jiok8. Hia*-ti7 thia*--i. 28). U7 hiah e5
Bi2-tian5 e5 seng-li2 lang5 tui3 hia ke3, i e5 hia* chiu7 ka7 Iok-sek
tui3 chi*2-lai7 puih8--khi2-lai5, chiong i boe7 hoo7 I2-sit8-ma2-li7
lang5, tit-tioh8 ji7-chap8 e5 gun5. Hiah e5 lang5 chiu7 toa3 Iok-sek
khi3 Ai-kip8. 29). Liu5-pian7 to3-tng2--lai5 chi*2-pi*, khoa*3-ki*3
Iok-sek bo5 ti7 chi*2-lai7, chiu7 thiah-lih8 ka-ki7 e5 sa*. 30).
To3--khi3 sio2-ti7 hia, kong2, Gin2-a2 bo5--khi3 lah; ia7 goa2 nih, goa2
beh tah-loh8 khi3? 31). In chiu7 thai5 chit8 chiah soa*-iu*5-kang2,
chiong Iok-sek hit nia2 sa* un3-huih; chiu7 chhe lang5 theh8 hit nia2
chhai2-sek e5 sa* khi3 in lau7-pe7 hia, kong2, Goan2 chhe7-tioh8
chit-nia2, chhia*2 li2 jin7-khoa*3 si7 li2 e5 kia*2 e5 goa7-sa* a2
m7-si7. 33). I jin7-tit, chiu7 kong2, Che si7 goa2 e5 kia*2 e5 goa7-sa*,
u7 phai*2-siu3 ka7-chiah8--i; Iok-sek tek-khak hoo7 i thiah-chhui3. 34).
Nga2-kok chiu7 thiah-lih8 sa*, io ha5 moa5-poo3, ui7 i e5 kia*2 ai-siong
choe7-choe7 jit8. 35). I e5 kia*2 kap i e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 long2
khi2-lai5 an-ui3 i; i m7-kheng2 siu7 an-ui3; kong2, Goa2 tek-khak
ai-siong loh8 im-hu2, kau3 goa2 e5 kia*2 hia. I e5 lau7-pe7 ui7-tioh8 i
thi5-khau3. 36). Bi2-tian5 lang5 toa3 Iok-sek kau3 Ai-kip8, chiong i
boe7 hoo7 Hoat-lo2 e5 jin5-sin5, si7-oe7-tiu*2, Pho-the5-hoat.


[38] Hit-si5 Iu5-tai7 li7-khui i e5 hia*-ti7, loh8--khi3 kau3 chit8 e5
A-too7-lan5 lang5, mia5 choe3 Hi-lah8 e5 ke; 2). Iu5-tai7 ti7-hia
khoa*3-ki*3 chit8 e5 Ka-lam5 lang5, mia5-kio3 Su-a e5 cha-boo2-kia*2;
chiu7 chhoa7 i, kap i tang5-pang5. 3). I chiu7 hoai5-in7 si*-kia*2;
Iu5-tai7 chiu7 ka7 i ho7 mia5 choe3 Ji*2. 4). I koh hoai5-in7 si*-kia*2;
lau7-bu2 ka7 i ho7 mia5 Go5-lam5. 5). I iu7-koh si*-kia*2, ka7 i
ho7-mia5 Si7-lah8; i si* Si7-lah8 e5 si5, Iu5-tai7 tu2-a2 ti7 Ki-sek.
6). Iu5-tai7 ka7 i e5 toa7-kia*2 Ji*2 chhoa7-boo2, mia5-kio3 Tha-ma2.
7). Iu5-tai7 e5 toa7-kia*2 Ji*2 kia*5-phai*2 ti7 Ia5-ho5-hoa e5
bin7-cheng5; Ia5-ho5-hoa chiu7 hoo7 i si2. 8). Iu5-tai7 ka7 Go5-lam5
kong2, Li2 tioh8 kap li2 e5 hia*-so2 tang5-pang5, tui3 i lai5 chin7 li2
choe3 sio2-ti7 e5 pun2-hun7, ka7 li2 e5 hia* lip8 hoo7-su5. 9). Go5-lam5
chai soo2 si* e5 kia*2 bo5 kui ti7 i ka-ki7; soo2-i2 tang5-pang5 e5 si5,
ui5-siat ti7 toe7--nih, bian2-tit hoo7 i e5 hia* u7 hoo7-su5. 10). I e5
soo2-choe3, Ia5-ho5-hoa khoa*3 choe3 phai*2; hoo7 i ia7 si2. 11).
Iu5-tai7 sim-lai7 kong2, Kia*-liau2 Si7-lah8 iah8 si2, chhin-chhiu*7 i
nng7 e5 hia* chit8-iu*7; chiu7 tui3 i e5 sim-pu7 Tha-ma2 kong2, Li2 khi3
toa3 lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 ke chiu2-koa*2, theng3-hau7 goa2 e5 kia*2 Si7-lah8
tiong2-seng5. Tha-ma2 chiu7 to3--khi3, toa3 ti7 in lau7-pe7 e5 ke.

12). Ke3 ku2-ku2, Iu5-tai7 e5 boo2 Su-a e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 si2; Iu5-tai7
siu7 an-ui3; chiu7 kap i e5 peng5-iu2 A-too7-lan5 lang5 Hi-lah8
chiu*7-khi3 Teng5-na2, kau3 i chian2 iu*5-mng5 e5 lang5 hia. 13). U7
lang5 ka7 Tha-ma2 kong2, Lin2 ta-koa* chiu*7-khi3 Teng5-na2, chian2 i e5
iu*5 e5 mng5. 14). Tha-ma2 khoa*3-ki*3 Si7-lah8 i2-keng tiong2-seng5,
iau2 bo5 chhoa7 i choe3-boo2; chiu7 thng3 i chiu2-koa*2 e5 sa*, eng7
phe3 ta3-bin7, koh moa sin-the2; che7 ti7 Teng5-na2 e5 loo7, I-na2-in3
mng5-khau2. 15). Iu5-tai7 khoa*3-ki*3 i, liah8-choe3 si7 chhiong-ki,
in-ui7 i u7 ta3-bin7. 16). Chiu7 oat-khi3 loo7-pi* chiu7-kun7 i; kong2,
Lai5, hoo7 goa2 kap li2 sa*-kap khun3; in-ui7 m7-chai si7 i e5 sim-pu7;
in3 kong2, Li2 beh kap goa2 khun3, beh eng7 sim2-mih8 hoo7 goa2? 17).
Iu5-tai7 kong2, Goa2 tui3 iu*5-kun5-lai7 liah8 chit8 chiah soa*-iu*5-a2,
kia3--lai5 hoo7 li2. Kong2, Li2 beh eng7 mih8 hoo7 goa2 choe3
chun2-tng3, theng3-hau7 li2 kia3-lai5 mah? 18). Iu5-tai7 kong2, Goa2
tioh8 sim2-mih8 hoo7 li2 choe3 chun2-tng3? I chiu7 kong2, Li2 e5 in3,
li2 e5 toa3, kap li2 chhiu2--nih e5 koai*2-a2; chiu7 hoo7 i, kap i
khun3; i chiu7 tui3 Iu5-tai7 hoai5-in7. 19). Tha-ma2 khi2-lai5 khi3;
thng3 i e5 phe3, iu5-gôan chheng7 i chiu2-koa*2 e5 sa*. 20). Iu5-tai7
thok i e5 peng5-iu2 A-too7-lan5 lang5 sang3 chit8 chiah soa*-iu*5-a2,
beh tui3 hit e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 chhiu2 theh8 chun2-tng3; chhe7 i boe7
tioh8. 21). Chiu7 mng7 hit soo2-chai7 e5 lang5 kong2, I-na2-in3 loo7-pi*
e5 chhiong-ki ti7 tah-loh8? in kong2, chit-ui7 bo5 chhiong-ki. 22). I
to3--khi3 ki*3 Iu5-tai7 kong2, Goa2 chhe7 i bo5; hit-ui7 e5 lang5 iah8
kong2, Chit-ui7 bo5 chhiong-ki. 23). Iu5-tai7 kong2, Ku3-chai7 i
theh8-khi3, bian2-tit lan2 kian3-siau3; li2 khoa*3, goa2 i2-keng chiong
chit chiah soa*-iu*5-a2 sang3 i, li2 keng2-jian5 chhe7 i bo5. 24).
Iok-liok8 ke3 sa*-geh8-jit8, u7 lang5 ka7 Iu5-tai7 kong2, Li2 e5 sim-pu7
Tha-ma2 choe3 chhiong-ki; koh in-ui7 kia*5-im5, soa3 u7 sin-in7.
Iu5-tai7 kong2, Ka7 i thoa--chhut-lai5 sio. 25). Tha-ma2 hoo7 lang5
thoa--chhut-lai5 e5 si5, chiu7 chhe lang5 khi3 ki*3 i e5 ta-koa* kong2,
Chiah e5 mih8 si7 chi7-chui7 e5, goa2 chiu7-si7 tui3 i lai5 hoai5-in7.
26). Koh kong2, Chhia*2 li2 jin7, khoa*3 chit e5 in3 kap toa3 kap
koai*2-a2 si7 chi7-chui7 e5. Iu5-tai7 jin7-tit, chiu7 kong2, I pi2 goa2
khah u7-gi7; in-ui7 goa2 bo5 chiong i ke3 hoo7 goa2 e5 kia*2 Si7-lah8;
tui3 hit-tiap8 Iu5-tai7 bo5 koh chhin-kun7 i. 27). Tha-ma2 tit-beh si*
e5 si5, chai i pak-too2-lai7 si7 siang-e5. 28). Teh si* e5 si5, chit8 e5
gin2-a2 chhun chit8 ki chhiu2 chhut-lai5; khioh-chia2 theh8 ang5-soa*3
pak8 ti7 i e5 chhiu2 kong2, Chit-e5 si7 tai7-seng chhut-e5. 29).
Au7-lai5 i e5 chhiu2 kiu--jip8-khi3; te7-ji7--e5 chhut-si3; khioh-chia2
kong2, Li2 sia*2-su7 chong5--chhut-lai5? chit e5 piak-phoa3 si7
ui7-tioh8 li2; soo2-i2 ka7 i ho7-mia5 choe3 Hoat-lek8-su. 30). Au7-lai5
hit-e5, chhiu2 pak8 ang5-soa*3--e5, iah8 si*--chhut-lai5; chiu7 ho7 i e5
mia5 choe3 Sia7-lah8.


[39] Iok-sek hoo7 lang5 toa3 loh8-khi3 Ai-kip8; u7 chit8 e5 Ai-kip8
lang5, si7 Hoat-lo2 e5 jin5-sin5 si7-oe7-tiu*2 Pho-the5-hoat, tui3
hiah-e5 toa3 i lai5 e5 I2-sit8-ma2-li7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 boe2--khi3. 2).
Ia5-ho5-hoa kap i sa*-kap ti7-teh, hoo7 i tak8-hang7 heng-thong; toa3
ti7 i e5 chu2-lang5 Ai-kip8 lang5 e5 ke. 3). I e5 chu2-lang5 khoa*3-ki*3
Ia5-ho5-hoa kap i sa*-kap ti7-teh; koh Ia5-ho5-hoa hoo7 i e5 chhiu2 soo2
choe3--e5 long2 heng-thong. 4). Iok-sek chiu7 ti7 chu2-lang5 e5
bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, lai5 hok8-sai7 i; chu2-lang5 siat-lip8 i
koan2-li2 i e5 ke, chiong it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5 kau i e5 chhiu2. 5). Tui3
chu2-lang5 siat-lip8 i koan2-li2 ke-su7, kap i it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5,
Ia5-ho5-hoa ui7-tioh8 Iok-sek e5 ian5-koo3, su3-hok ti7 hit e5 Ai-kip8
lang5 e5 ke; ki*3-na7 ke-lai7 kap chhan5--nih it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5,
long2 tit-tioh8 Ia5-ho5-hoa su3-hok. 6). I chiong it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5,
long2 kau Iok-sek e5 chhiu2; tu5-khi3 i soo2 chiah8 e5 mih8 i2-goa7,
pat8-hang7 soo2-u7--e5, long2 m7-chai. Iok-sek sui2 koh ho2-si*-choe3.

7). Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 i2-au7, Iok-sek e5 chu2-bu2 chu3-sin5 khoa*3--i,
kong2, Lai5 kap goa2 khun3. 8). Iok-sek m7-than3, tui3 i e5 chu2-bu2
kong2, Li2 khoa*3, ke-lai7 u7 sim2-mih8 ti7 goa2 e5 chhiu2, goa2 e5
chu2-lang5 long2 m7-chai; i i2-keng chiong soo2-u7--e5 kau ti7 goa2 e5
chhiu2; ti7 chi2 ke-lai7 bo5 chit8-e5 pi2 goa2 khah-toa7; 9). li2
i2-goa7, i bo5 chit8-hang7 bo5 kau goa2, in-ui7 li2 si7 i e5 boo2; goa2
chai*2-iu*7 thang kia*5 chit e5 toa7-phai*2, lai5 tek-choe7 Siong7-te3?
10). Au7-lai5 i tak8-jit8 kap Iok-sek kong2-oe7; Iok-sek bo5 thia* i e5
oe7; bo5 kap i khun3, iah8 bo5 kap i choe3-tui. 11). U7 chit8-jit8,
Iok-sek jip8 chhu3 pan7 i e5 tai7-chi3; ke-lai7 e5 lang5 bo5 chit8-e5
ti7 chhu3-lai7. 12). Hu7-jin5-lang5 chiu7 khiu2 i e5 sa* kong2, Li2 lai5
kap goa2 khun3; Iok-sek chiong sa* pang3 ti7 i e5 chhiu2, chau2
chhut-khi3 goa7-bin7. 13). Hu7-jin5-lang5 khoa*3-ki*3 Iok-sek chiong sa*
pang3 ti7 i chhiu2--nih, koh chau2-chhut goa7-bin7; 14). chiu7 kio3
ke-lai7 e5 lang5 lai5, tui3 in kong2, Lin2 khoa*3--teh, i toa3 chit8 e5
Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 jip8-lai5 lan2 e5 ke beh hi3-lang7 lan2; i lai5 goa2
chia, beh kap goa2 khun3, goa2 chiu7 toa7-sia* hoah; 15). i thia*-ki*3
goa2 chhut-sia* hoah, chiu7 chiong i e5 sa* pang3 ti7 goa2 chia,
chau2-chhut goa7-bin7. 16). Hu7-jin5-lang5 chiong Iok-sek e5 sa* siu ti7
i hia, theng3-hau7 i e5 chu2-lang5 to3--lai5. 17). Chiu7 tui3 i
kong2-khi2 chiah e5 su7; kong2, Li2 soo2 toa3-lai5 lan2 chia, hit e5
Hi-pek-lai5 e5 loo5-pok8, kau3 goa2 chia, beh hi3-lang7 goa2; goa2
chhut-sia* hoah, i chiong i e5 sa* pang3 ti7 goa2 chia, chau2-chhut
goa7-bin7. 19). Chu2-lang5 thia*-ki*3 i e5 boo2 tui3 i soo2 kong2 e5
oe7, kong2, Li2 e5 loo5-pok8 chhin-chhiu*7 an2-ni khoan2-thai7 goa2, i
chiu7 siu7-khi3. 20). Iok-sek e5 chu2-lang5 chiong i koai*-loh8 ka*,
chiu7-si7 ong5 e5 choe7-hoan7 siu7 koai* e5 soo2-chai7; tui3 an2-ni
Iok-sek ti7 hit e5 ka*-lai7.

21). Chong2-si7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap Iok-sek ti7-teh, si-un hoo7 i; hoo7 i
ti7 koan2-ka* e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2. 22).
Koan2-ka*--e5 chiu7 chiong ka*-lai7 soo2 u7 e5 hoan7-lang5 long2 kau
Iok-sek e5 chhiu2; in ti7-hia soo2 choe3 e5 tai7-chi3, long2 si7 i teh
choe3. 23). Ki*3-na7 Iok-sek chhiu2-e7 e5 tai7-chi3, koan2-ka*--e5
it-khai3 bo5 chhap; in-ui7 Ia5-ho5-hoa kap Iok-sek ti7-teh, koh i soo2
choe3--e5, Ia5-ho5-hoa long2 hoo7 i heng-thong.


[40] Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 i2-au7 Ai-kip8 ong5 e5 chiu2-cheng3 kap
tu5-pang5 tek-choe7 in e5 chu2 Ai-kip8 ong5. 2). Hoat-lo2 siu7-khi3 i
nng7 e5 jin5-sin5, chiu7-si7 chiu2-cheng3-tiu*2 kap tu5-pang5-tiu*2, 3).
chiong in koai* ti7 si7-oe7-tiu*2 hu2-lai7 e5 ka*, chiu7-si7 Iok-sek
siu7 koai* e5 soo2-chai7. 4). Si7 -oe7-tiu*2 chiong in kau-tai3 Iok-sek,
i chiu7 su-hau7 in; in chiu7 ti7 ka*-lai7 u7 hiah-ku2. 5). Siu7-koai*
ti7 ka*--e5, Ai-kip8 ong5 e5 chiu2-cheng3 kap tu5-pang5, nng7-lang5
tang5 chit8-mi5 kok bang7-ki*3 chit8 e5 bang7, long2 chiau3 tak8 e5
bang7 e5 i3-gi7 lai5 bang7. 6). Kau3 thi*-kng, Iok-sek jip8--khi3 in
hia, khoa*3-ki*3 in u7 iu-bun7 e5 khoan2-sit. 7). I chiu7 mng7 Hoat-lo2
nng7 e5 jin5-sin5, chiu7-si7 kap i pi*5-pi*5 koai* ti7 chu2-lang5
hu2-lai7--e5, kong2, Kin-a2-jit8 lin2 sia*2-su7 bin7 tai3-iu-iong5? 8).
In ka7 i kong2, Goan2 tak8-lang5 bang7-ki*3 chit8 e5 bang7, bo5 lang5
thang oan5. Iok-sek ka7 in kong2, Oan5-bang7 kiam2-m7-si7 chai7 ti7
Siong7-te3 mah? chhia*2 lin2 ka7 goa2 kong2. 9). Chiu2-cheng3 chiu7 tui3
Iok-sek pai5-liat8 i e5 bang7, kong2, Goa2 bang7-tiong khoa*3-ki*3 u7
chit8 chang5 phu5-to5-chhiu7 ti7 goa2 e5 bin7-cheng5; 10). chhiu7-teng2
u7 sa*-ki, chhin-chhiu*7 u7 hoat-ge5 khui-hoe; i e5 pha kiat-chia*5 sek8
e5 phu5-to5. 11). Hoat-lo2 e5 poe ti7 goa2 e5 chhiu2-lai7, goa2 chiu7
theh8 phu5-to5, nih8 i ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 poe-lai7, chiong poe phang5 kau
Hoat-lo2 e5 chhiu2. 12). Iok-sek ka7 i kong2, Li2 e5 bang7 si7 an2-ni
oan5; sa*-ki chiu7-si7 sa*-jit8; 13). koh sa*-jit8, Hoat-lo2 beh
ku2-khi2 li2 e5 thau5, hok8-to3 li2 e5 koa*-chit; Hoat-lo2 e5 chiu2-poe
beh iu5-gôan he7 ti7 li2 e5 chhiu2, chhin-chhiu*7 cheng5 choe3 i e5
chiu2-cheng3 chit8-iu*7. 14). Li2 na7 tek-chi3 e5 si5, tioh8 ki3-liam7
goa2, si-un hoo7 goa2; ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 thoe3 goa2 kong2
chit8 sia*; kiu3 goa2 chhut chit e5 ka*. 15). Goa2 sit8-chai7 si7 tui3
Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 e5 toe7 siu7-boe7--lai5-e5; goa2 ti7-chia iah8 bo5
choe3-chhut sim2-mih8, hoo7 in ka7 goa2 koai*-loh8 ka*. 16). Tu5-pang5
khoa*3-ki*3 bang7 oan5-liau2 ho2, chiu7 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 iah8 ti7
goa2 e5 bang7-tiong khoa*3, ti7 goa2 e5 thau5-khak-teng2 u7 sa*-kheng
pek e5 pia*2; 17). teng2-bin7 hit-kheng u7 toe2 Hoat-lo2 soo2 chiah8
tak8-ho7 pek e5 mih8; u7 chiau2 lai5 teh goa2 thau5-khak-teng2
kheng-lai7 e5 mih8. 18). Iok-sek in3 i kong2, Li2 e5 bang7 si7 an2-ni
oan5; sa* khia kheng si7 sa*-jit8; 19). koh sa*-jit8, Hoat-lo2 beh
ku2-khi2 li2 e5 thau5-khak li7-khui li2, tiau3 li2 ti7 chha5--nih; beh
u7 pe-chiau2 lai5 teh li2 sin-khu e5 bah. 20). Kau3 te7-sa* jit8, si7
Hoat-lo2 e5 si*-jit8, i ui7 cheng3 jin5-sin5 pai5-siat ian5-siah8; ti7
chiah e5 jin5-sin5 e5 tiong-kan, thai-ku2 chiu2-cheng3, kap tu5-pang5;
21). hoo7 chiu2-cheng3-tiu*2 hok8-to3 koa*-chit; i iu5-gôan phang5-poe
ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5 chhiu2; 22). chong2-si7 chiong tu5-pang5-thau5
tiau3--khi2-lai5; tu2-tu2 chiau3 Iok-sek soo2 ka7 in oan5--e5. 23).
Na7-si7 chiu2-cheng3-tiu*2 bo5 liam7-tioh8 Iok-sek, keng2-jian5
boe7-ki3-tit i.


[41] Ke3 nng7-ni5 ka-nng5, Hoat-lo2 bin5-bang7; bang7-ki*3 i khia7 ti7
ho5-pi*, 2). khoa*3-ki*3 chhit chiah gu5-bu2 tui3 ho5--nih khi2-lai5,
sui2 koh pui5; ti7 loo5-tek-a2-lai7 teh chiah8. 3). Te3-au7 koh u7 chhit
chiah gu5-bu2 tui3 ho5--nih khi2--lai5, khiap-si3 koh san2; kap cheng5
hiah e5 gu5 tang5-khia7 ti7 ho5-pi*. 4). Chiah e5 khiap-si3 koh san2 e5
gu5-bu2 it-chin7 chiah8 hi2 chhit-chiah sui2 koh pui5 e5 gu5. Hoat-lo2
chiu7 chhi*2. 5). I koh khun3, te7-ji7 pai2 bin5-bang7; bang7-ki*3 chit8
chang5 beh8 chhut chhit-sui7, phauh koh ho2. 6). Au7-lai7 khoa*3-ki*3
koh chhut chhit-sui7, pha*3-pha*3, koh hoo7 tang-hong sau3-phai*2. 7).
Chiah e5 pha*3 e5 sui7 thun hi2 chhit-sui7 phauh koh pa2-moa2--e5.
Hoat-lo2 chhi*2, chiah chai si7 bang7--ki*3. 8). Kau3 thi*-kng, Hoat-lo2
sim bo5 peng5-an; chiu7 chhe lang5 tiau3 Ai-kip8 soo2 u7 e5 sut8-su7,
phok-su7 lai5; Hoat-lo2 chiu7 chiong i soo2 bang7-ki*3--e5 ka7 in kong2;
in bo5 lang5 oe7 ka7 Hoat-lo2 oan5.

9). Hit-si5 chiu2-cheng3-tiu*2 ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Goa2 kin-a2-jit8
ki3-tit goa2 e5 choe7. 10). Cheng5 Hoat-lo2 siu7-khi3 jin5-sin5, chiong
goa2 kap tu5-pang5-thau5 koai* ti7 si7-oe7-tiu*2 hu2-lai7 e5 ka*. 11).
Goa2 kap i, nng7-lang5 siang5 hit-mi5 u7 bang7-ki*3, kok chiau3 i e5
bang7 e5 i3-gi7 lai5 bang7. 12). Ti7-hia, kap goan2 ti7-teh, u7 chit e5
Hi-pek-lai5 e5 siau3-lian5 lang5, si7 si7-oe7-tiu*2 e5 loo5-pok8, goan2
ka7 i kong2, i chiu7 ka7 goan2 oan5 goan2 e5 bang7; si7 chiau3 goan2
tak8-lang5 e5 bang7 lai5 oan5. 13). Au7-lai7 tu2-tu2 chiau3 i soo2 ka7
goan2 oan5--e5 lai5 chia*5; i hoo7 goa2 hok8-chit, hit-lang5 siu7 tiau3
lai5 si2.

14). Hoat-lo2 chiu7 chhe lang5 khi3 tiau3 Iok-sek, in chiu7 kin2-kin2
chhoa7 i chhut-ka*; i chiu7 chian2-hoat, oa*7 i e5 sa*, lai5 ki*3
Hoat-lo2. 15). Hoat-lo2 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 bang7-ki*3 chit8 e5
bang7, bo5 lang5 oe7 oan5--i; goa2 thia*-ki*3 lang5 kong2 kau3 li2
thia*-ki*3 bang7 chiu7 oe7 oan5. 16). Iok-sek in3 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Che
m7-si7 chai7-ti7 goa2; Siong7-te3 beh chiong peng5-an chi2-si7 Hoat-lo2.
17). Hoat-lo2 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, 18). Goa2 bang7-ki*3 goa2 khia7 ti7
ho5-pi*, u7 chhit chiah gu5-bu2 tui3 ho5--nih khi2--lai5, pui5 koh sui2;
ti7 loo5-tek-a2-lai7 teh chiah8; 19). te3-au7 koh u7 chhit chiah gu5-bu2
khi2--lai5, nng7-chia*2, chin khiap-si3, koh chin san2; pian3 Ai-kip8
toe7, goa2 m7-bat khoa*3-ki*3 kau3 chiah phai*2. 20). Chiah e5 san2 koh
khiap-si3 e5 gu5-bu2 it-chin7 chiah8 tai7-seng hi2 chhit chiah pui5 e5
gu5-bu2; 21). thun loh8 pak, iau2-boe7 khoa*3-chhut u7 thun--loh8 khi3;
hit e5 khiap-si3 e5 khoan2 iu5-gôan kap tai7-seng bo5 koh-iu*7; goa2
chiu7 chhi*2. 22). Goa2 ti7 bang7-tiong koh khoa*3-ki*3 chit8 chang5
beh8, chhut chhit-sui7, pa2-moa2 koh ho2; 23). au7-lai7 koh chhut
chhit-sui7, koo-ta5, pha*3-pha*3, koh hoo7 tang-hong sau3-phai*2; 24).
chiah e5 pha*3-pha*3 e5 sui7 thun hi2 chhit sui7 ho2--e5. Goa2 kong2
hoo7 sut8-su7 thia*, ia7 bo5 lang5 oe7 ka7 goa2 koe2-beng5.

25). Iok-sek ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Hoat-lo2 e5 bang7 chiu7-si7 chit8-e5;
Siong7-te3 soo2 beh kia*5 e5 su7, u7 chi2-si7 Hoat-lo2. 26). chhit-chiah
ho2 e5 gu5-bu2 si7 chhit-ni5; chhit-sui7 ho2--e5, iah8 si7 chhit-ni5;
bang7 si7 chit8-e5. 27). Hiah e5 te3-au7 khi2--lai5 e5 chhit chiah san2
koh khiap-si3 e5 gu5-bu2, si7 chhit-ni5; hiah e5 chhit sui7 khang-pha*3,
koh hoo7 tang-hong sau3-phai*2--e5, iah8 si7 chhit ni5; beh choe3 chhit
ni5 e5 ki-hng. 28). Siong7-te3 soo2 beh choe3 e5 su7, u7 hian2-beng5 ti7
Hoat-lo2; che si7 goa2 tui3 Hoat-lo2 soo2 kong2--e5. 29). Li2 khoa*3
Ai-kip8 pian3-toe7 beh tu2-tioh8 toa7 ho2-ni5-tang chhit-ni5; 30).
te3-au7, koh beh tu2-tioh8 ki-hng chhit-ni5; sim7-chi3 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7
long2 boe7 ki3-tit i2-cheng5 e5 ho2-siu; choan5-toe7 beh hoo7 ki-hng
soo2 biat8; 31). in-ui7 i2-au7 e5 ki-hng thai3 siong-tiong7, chiu7
m7-chai i2-cheng5 toe7-hng e5 ho2-siu. 32). Lun7-kau3 Hoat-lo2 nng7 pai2
e5 bin5-bang7, si7 in-ui7 Siong7-te3 chu3-tia*7 chit e5 tai7-chi3, koh
Siong7-te3 beh kin2-kin2 chia*5-i. 33). Soo2-i2 Hoat-lo2 tioh8 keng2
chit8 e5 u7 chhang-mia5, u7 ti3-hui7 e5 lang5, phai3 i ti7-li2 Ai-kip8
toe7. 34). Hoat-lo2 tioh8 an2-ni kia*5, koh lip8 koa*-oan5 koan2-li2
chit e5 toe7; tng chhit-ni5 ho2-ni5-tang e5 si5, Ai-kip8 toe7
soo2-siu--e5, goo7-hun7 thiu chit8-hun7; 35). hoo7 in ti7 chiong-lai5 e5
ho2-ni5-tang, chek-chu7 it-chhe3 e5 bi2-niu5; chu7-chip8 ngoo2-kok,
siu-khng3 chiau3-koo3; ti7 tak8 e5 sia*5 choe3 chiah8-mih8, kui ti7
Hoat-lo2 e5 chhiu2-thau5. 36). Soo2 chek-chu7 e5 bi2-niu5, thang choe3
Ai-kip8 toe7 chiong-lai5 chhit-ni5 ki-hng e5 loo7-eng7; bian2-tit chit
e5 toe7 hoo7 ki-hng soo2 biat8.

37). Hoat-lo2 kap i it-chhe3 e5 jin5-sin5 long2 liah8 chit e5 tai7-chi3
choe3-ho2. 38). Hoat-lo2 tui3 i e5 jin5-sin5 kong2, Lan2 kiam2 oe7
chhe7-tioh8 chit8-e5 chhin-chhiu*7 i chit e5 lang5, u7 Siong7-te3 e5
sin5 ti7 i e5 lai7-bin7 mah? 39). Hoat-lo2 tui3 Iok-sek kong2,
Siong7-te3 i2-keng chiong chit e5 tai7-chi3 long2 chi2-si7 li2,
kho2-kian3 bo5 lang5 chhin-chhiu*7 li2 u7 chit-ho7 e5 chhang-mia5
ti3-hui7. 40). Li2 thang koan2-li2 goa2 e5 ke; goa2 e5 peh-si*3 long2
tioh8 thia* li2 e5 oe7, hoo7 li2 koan2-li2; tok8-tok8 ti7 po2-cho7, goa2
pi2 li2 khah toa7. 41). Hoat-lo2 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 ku2-khi2 li2
koan2-hat Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7. 42). Hoat-lo2 chiu7 pak i chhiu2--nih
choe3 in3 e5 chhiu2-chi2, koa3 ti7 Iok-sek e5 chng2-thau5-a2, ka7 i
chheng7 iu3-toe7-sa*; chiong kim-lian7 koa3 ti7 i e5 am7-kun2. 43). Koh
hoo7 Iok-sek che7 i e5 te7-ji7 pan7 chhia; khui-to7--e5 kio3 kong2,
Kui7; an2-ni Hoat-lo2 siat-lip8 i ti7-li2 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7. 44).
Hoat-lo2 tui3 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 si7 Hoat-lo2, na7 bo5 li2 u7 sia*, ti7
Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7, m7-chun2 lang5 tang7 kha-chhiu2. 45). Hoat-lo2
khim-su3 Iok-sek e5 mia5 kio3 Sat-hoat-na2-thek Pa-loe7-a; koh chiong
An-sia*5 e5 che3-si Pho-the5-hui-lah8 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 A-se-lap8 hoo7 i
choe3-boo2. Iok-sek chiu7 chhut-sun5 Ai-kip8 toe7.

46). Iok-sek ki*3 Ai-kip8 ong5 Hoat-lo2 e5 si5, hit-ni5 sa*-chap8 he3.
Iok-sek tui3 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5 chhut-khi3, pian3 kia*5 Ai-kip8
choan5-toe7. 47). Chhit-e5 ho2 ni5-tang e5 lai7-bin7, toe7 e5 chhut-san2
kek8-ki5 hong-seng7. 48). Iok-sek chu7-chip8 Ai-kip8 toe7 chhit e5 ho2
ni5-tang it-chhe3 e5 bi2-niu5; chiong bi2-niu5 chek-chu7 ti7 tak8 e5
sia*5; chiu-ui5 chhan5-toe7 e5 bi2-niu5, long2 chek-chu7 ti7 i e5
pun2-sia*5. 49). Iok-sek chek-chu7 goo7-kak kek8-choe7, chhin-chhiu*7
hai2-pi* e5 soa, kau3 i theng5-chi2 bo5 sng3; in-ui7 sng3-boe7-liau2.
50). Ki-hng e5 ni5 be7-kau3 i2-cheng5, An-sia*5 e5 che3-si
Pho-the5-hui-lah8 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 A-se-lap8 ka7 Iok-sek si* nng7 e5
kia*2. 51). Iok-sek ka7 toa7 kia*2 ho7 mia5 kio3 Ma2-na2-se; in-ui7 i
kong2, Siong7-te3 hoo7 goa2 boe7-ki3-tit goa2 it-chhe3 e5 khun3-khoo2,
kap goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 choan5-ke. 52). I ka7 te7-ji7 kia*2 ho7 mia5
I2-hoat-lian5; in-ui7 i kong2, Siong7-te3 hoo7 goa2 ti7 goa2 siu7-khoo2
e5 toe7-hng heng-ong7. 53). Ai-kip8 toe7 chhit-ni5 ho2 ni5-tang i2-keng
oan5, 54). chhit-ni5 ki-hng chiu7 lai5, tu2-tu2 chiau3 Iok-sek soo2
kong2--e5; tak8-kok long2 u7 ki-hng; tok8-tok8 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7 u7
bi2-niu5.

55). Kau3 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7 u7 ki-hng, cheng3 peh-si*3 tui3 Hoat-lo2
ai-kiu5 bi2-niu5; Hoat-lo2 tui3 Ai-kip8 e5 cheng3-lang5 kong2, Lin2 khi3
chhe7 Iok-sek, hoan7-na7 i soo2 kong2--e5, lin2 long2 tioh8 choe3. 56).
Tng-si5 ki-hng pian3-moa2 thi*-e7; Iok-sek khui tak8 soo2-chai7 e5
chhek-chhng, thio3 bi2-niu5 hoo7 Ai-kip8 lang5; ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 ki-hng
chin siong-tiong7. 57). Tak8-kok e5 lang5 long2 khi3 Ai-kip8, kau3
Iok-sek hia tiah8 ni2-niu5; in-ui7 thi*-e7 ki-hng chin siong-tiong7.


[42] Nga2-kok khoa*3-ki*3 Ai-kip8 u7 goo7-kak, Nga2-kok chiu7 ka7 i hiah
e5 kia*2 kong2, Lin2 sia*2-su7 teh sa*-khoa*3. 2). Koh kong2, Goa2
thia*-ki*3 Ai-kip8 u7 goo7-kak, lin2 thang loh8-khi3 hia, ui7 lan2 tiah8
tam7-poh8, hoo7 lan2 thang too7-oah8, bian2 si2. 3). Tui3 an2-ni Iok-sek
chap8 e5 hia* long2 loh8 Ai-kip8, khi3 tiah8 bi2-niu5. 4). Chong2-si7
Iok-sek e5 sio2-ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2, Nga2-kok bo5 chhe i kap in hia*
sa*-kap khi3; in-ui7 i kong2, Kia*-liau2 i tu2-tioh8 hai7. 5). Lai5
tiah8 bi2-niu5 e5 lang5 e5 tiong-kan, I2-sek-liat8 hiah e5 kia*2 iah8 u7
lai5, in-ui7 Ka-lam5 toe7 iah8 u7 ki-hng. 6). Tng-si5 ti7-li2 Ai-kip8
toe7 e5 si7 Iok-sek; thio3 bi2-niu5 hoo7 hit soo2-chai7 e5 cheng3
peh-si*3--e5, iah8 si7 i; Iok-sek hiah e5 hia* lai5, phak-loh8 toe7 pai3
i. 7). Iok-sek khoa*3-ki*3 i hiah e5 hia*, oe7 jin7--tit, ke2-choe3
si*-hun7-lang5, tui3 in kong2 khah-giam5 e5 oe7, mng7 in kong2, Lin2
tui3 tah-loh8 lai5? in kong2, Tui3 Ka-lam5 toe7 lai5 tiah8 bi2-niu5. 8).
Iok-sek oe7 jin7-tit in hia*, in boe7 jin7--tit i. 9). Iok-sek ki3-tit
cheng5 soo2 bang7 lun7-kau3 in-e5 hiah e5 bang7, chiu7 tui3 in kong2,
Lin2 si7 cheng-tham3, lai5 tham3-thia* chit soo2-chai7 e5 hu-sit8. 10).
In tui3 i kong2, goan2 e5 chu2 ah, m7-si7, li2 e5 loo5-pok8 lai5 beh
tiah8 bi2-niu5. 11). Goan2 long2 si7 chit8-lang5 e5 kia*2, goan2 si7
lau2-sit8 lang5, li2 e5 loo5-pok8 m7-si7 cheng-tham3. 12). Iok-sek ka7
in kong2, M7-si7 an2-ni, lin2 lai5 si7 beh tham3-thia* chit soo2-chai7
e5 hu-sit8. 13). In kong2, Li2 e5 loo5-pok8 chap8-ji7 e5 hia*-ti7, si7
Ka-lam5 toe7 chit8 e5 lang5 e5 kia*2; te7-it-soe3--e5, hian7-kim ti7
goan2 lau7-pe7 hia; u7 chit8-e5 bo5--khi3 lah. 14). Iok-sek ka7 in
kong2, Goa2 tu2-a2 kong2 lin2 si7 cheng-tham3, chit e5 oe7 sit8-chai7
bo5 chho3. 15). Goa2 ki2 Hoat-lo2 e5 si*3-mia7 lai5 chiu3-choa7, na7
lin2 soah-be2 e5 sio2-ti7 bo5 kau3 chia, lin2 boe7-tit-thang chhut chit
soo2-chai7; eng7 an2-ni lai5 chhi3-giam7 lin2 e5 hu-sit8. 16). Tioh8
chhe lin2 tiong-kan chit8-lang5 khi3 chhoa7 lin2 e5 sio2-ti7 lai5, lin2
chiah-e5 long2 tioh8 koai* ti7-chia, cheng3-beng5 lin2 e5 oe7, chai lin2
seng5-sit8 a2-bo5; na7 bo5, goa2 ki2 Hoat-lo2 e5 si*3-mia7 lai5
chiu3-choa7, lin2 it-teng7 si7 cheng-tham3. 17). Tui3 an2-ni Iok-sek
chiong in long2 koai* ti7 Ka*--nih sa*-jit8.

18). Kau3 te7-sa* jit8 Iok-sek tui3 in kong2, Goa2 keng3-ui3 Siong7-te3;
lin2 chiau3 goa2 e5 oe7 kia*5, chiu7 oe7 oah8. 19). Lin2 na7 ko2-jian5
si7 lau2-sit8 lang5, lin2 hia*-ti7-tiong thang lau5 chit8-e5 pak8 ti7
lin2 hi2 ka*-lai7; chong2-si7 lin2 thang toa3 bi2-niu5 to3--khi3, kiu3
lin2 ke-lai7 e5 ki-hng, 20). chiong lin2 soah-be2 sio2-ti7 chhoa7 lai5
goa2 chia; an2-ni lin2 e5 oe7 chiu7 u7 pin5-ku3, lin2 ia7 m7-bian2 si2.
In chiu7 chiau3 an2-ni kia*5. 21). In sa*-kap kong2, Lan2 tui3 ti7 lan2
e5 sio2-ti7 sit8-chai7 u7 choe7, i ai-kiu5 lan2 e5 si5, lan2 khoa*3-ki*3
i sim-lai7 e5 kan-khoo2, ia7 m7-kheng2 thia* i; soo2-i2 chit-tiu*5 e5
khoo2-lan7 kau3 ti7 lan2. 22). Liu5-pian7 in3 in kong2, Goa2 kiam2
m7-si7 tui3 lin2 kong2, m7-thang hai7 hit e5 gin2-a2 lai5 chhu2-choe7,
tok8-tok8 lin2 m7-thia*? soo2-i2 lau5 i e5 huih e5 choe7, tui3 lan2
chiah-e5 tho2. 23). In m7-chai Iok-sek thia* oe7 hiau2--tit; in-ui7 ti7
in tiong-kan u7 eng7 hoan-ek8-koa*. 24). Iok-sek oat8-tng2-sin lau5
bak8-sai2; koh oat8-lai5 kap in kong2-oe7; chiu7 ti7 in tiong-kan chhu2
Se-bian7 chhut--lai5, ti7 in e5 bin7-cheng5 ka7 i pak8--teh. 25).
Iok-sek hoan-hu3 lang5 chiong goo7-kak jip8 ti7 in e5 khi3-ku7 kau3
moa2-moa2, ia7 chiong in tak8-lang5 e5 gun5 he7 ti7 in e5 poo3-te7-lai7,
lai5 heng5 in, koh eng7 loo7--nih e5 chiah8-mih8 hoo7 in; lang5 chiu7
chiau3 an2-ni lai5 ka7 in choe3.

26). In chiu7 chiong goo7-kak hoo7 in e5 lu5 chai3, chiu7 li7-khui hia
khi3. 27). Kau3 hioh-mi5 e5 soo2-chai7, in tiong-kan u7 chit8-lang5
thau2-khui i e5 poo3-te7, beh theh8 hoo7 lu5 chiah8, chiah khoa*3-ki*3 i
e5 gun5 iu5-gôan ti7--teh, he7 ti7 poo3-te7-khau2. 28). Chiu7 ka7 i e5
hia*-ti7 kong2, Goa2 e5 gun5 heng5 to3-tng2, li2 khoa*3, iu5-gôan ti7
goa2 e5 poo3-te7-lai7; in chiu7 kia* kau3 bo5 sim-koa*,
ngiauh8-ngiauh8-chhoah, sa*-kap kong2, Siong7-te3 an2-ni khoan2-thai7
lan2 si7 sim2-mih8? 29). In kau3 Ka-lam5 toe7, kau3 in lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok
hia, chiong soo2 tu2-tioh8 e5 su7 long2 ka7 i kong2, kong2, Hit-lang5,
chiu7-si7 hit soo2-chai7 e5 chu2, tui3 goan2 kong2 chin giam5 e5 oe7,
liah8 goan2 choe3 hit soo2-chai7 e5 cheng-tham3. 31). Goan2 ka7 i kong2,
Goan2 si7 lau2-sit8 lang5, goan2 m7-si7 cheng-tham3, 32). goan2 si7
chap8-ji7 e5 hia*-ti7, si7 goan2 lau7-pe7 e5 kia*2; u7 chit8-e5
bo5--khi3, te7-it-soe2-e5 hian7-kim kap goan2 lau7-pe7 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7.
33). Hit-lang5 chiu7-si7 hit soo2-chai7 e5 chu2, ka7 goan2 kong2, Na7
ai3 ho7 goa2 chai lin2 si7 lau2-sit8 lang5, lin2 hia*-ti7-tiong thang
lau5 chit8-e5 ti7 goa2 chia, lin2 chiah-e5 thang toa3 goo7-kak
to3--khi3, kiu3 lin2 ke-lai7 e5 ki-hng; 34). chhoa7 lin2 soah-be2 e5
sio2-ti7 lai5 goa2 chia, goa2 chiu7 chai lin2 m7-si7 cheng-tham3, si7
lau2-sit8 lang5; an2-ni goa2 chiu7 chiong lin2 e5 hia*-ti7 kau hoo7
lin2, lin2 ia7 thang ti7 chit soo2-chai7 boe2-boe7.

35). Au7-lai5 in pia*3 in e5 poo3-te7, bo5 phah-sng3, in tak8-lang5 e5
gun5-pau long2 ti7 in e5 poo3-te7-lai7; in kap in lau7-pe7 khoa*3-ki*3
gun5-pau chiu7 long2 kia*-hia*5. 36). In e5 lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok ka7 in
kong2, Lin2 hoo7 goa2 sit-loh8 goa2 e5 kia*2; Iok-sek bo5--khi3,
Se-bian7 ia7 bo5--khi3, lin2 koh beh chhoa7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 khi3; chiah
e5 tai7-chi3 long2 si7 hai7-tioh8 goa2. 37). Liu5-pian7 ka7 i e5
lau7-pe7 kong2, Goa2 na7 bo5 chhoa7 i to3-lai5 kau li2, li2 thang thai5
goa2 nng7 e5 kia*2; choe3 li2 thang chiong i kau-tai3 goa2, goa2
tek-khak chhoa7 i to3--lai5 kau li2. 38). Nga2-kok kong2, goa2 e5 kia*2
goa2 bo5 beh hoo7 i kap lin2 khi3; i e5 hia* i2-keng si2, chi2-u7 chhun
i; i na7 ti7 lin2 soo2 kia*5 e5 loo7 tu2-tioh8 ham7-hai7, he! chiu7-si7
lin2 hoo7 goa2 peh8-thau5-mng5 chhi*-chham2 loh8 im-hu2.


[43] Hit soo2-chai7 ki-hng chin-toa7. In tui3 Ai-kip8 toa3-lai5 e5
goo7-kak i2-keng chiah8-liau2, in lau7-pe7 ka7 in kong2, Lin2 tioh8 khi3
ka7 lan2 tiah8 tam7-poh8 bi2-niu5 lai5. 3). Iu5-tai7 in3 i kong2,
Hit-lang5 chhiat-chhiat hoan-hu3 goan2 kong2, Lin2 sio2-ti7 na7 bo5 kap
lin2 sa*-kap lai5, lin2 chiu7 boe7 tit-tioh8 ki*3 goa2 e5 bin7. 4). Lin2
na7 chhe goan2 sio2-ti7 kap goan2 sa*-kap khi3, goan2 chiu7 loh8--khi3,
ka7 li2 tiah8 bi2-niu5. 5). Li2 na7 m7 chhe i khi3, goan2 chiu7 m7
loh8--khi3; in-ui7 hit-lang5 ka7 goan2 kong2, Lin2 sio2-ti7 na7 bo5 kap
lin2 sa*-kap lai5, lin2 chiu7 boe7 tit-tioh8 ki*3 goa2 e5 bin7. 6).
I2-sek-liat8 kong2, Lin2 sia*2-su7 an2-ni hai7 goa2, ka7 hit-lang5 kong2
lin2 iau2 u7 sio2-ti7 ah? 7). In in3 kong2, Hit-lang5 ti3-i3 mng7 goan2
kap goan2 chhin-chok8 e5 tai7-chi3 kong2, Lin2 lau7-pe7 iau2 ti7-teh
bo5? lin2 iau2 u7 hia*-ti7 bo5? goan2 chiau3 i soo2 mng7--e5 ka7 i
kong2; goan2 thai2-tho2 oe7 chai i beh kong2, Tioh8 toa3 lin2 sio2-ti7
loh8--lai5? 8). Iu5-tai7 koh ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sek-liat8 kong2, Li2
chhe gin2-a2 kap goa2 khi3, goan2 chiu7 khi2-sin khi3, thang hoo7 goan2
kap li2, i2-kip8 goan2 e5 gin2-a2, tit-tioh8 oah8, bian2 si2. 9). Goa2
ka7 i po2, li2 thang tui3 goa2 tho2; goa2 na7 bo5 chhoa7 i to3-lai5,
khia7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5, goa2 goan7 it-seng tam-tng choe7. 10).
Lan2 na7 m7-si7 u7 ian5-chhian5, i2-keng te7-ji7-pai2 to3--lai5 lah.
11). In lau7-pe7 I2-sek-liat8 tui3 in kong2, Na7 si7 an2-ni, lin2 chiu7
tioh8 an2-ni choe3; thang chhu2 chit soo2-chai7 te7-it ho2 e5
thoo2-san2, ju2-hiu* tam7-poh8, phang-bit8 tam7-poh8, i2-kip8
hiu*-liau7, but8-ioh8, hui2-chi2, heng7-jin5 , long2 siu ti7 khi2-ku7
lai7; toa3--khi3 sang3 hit-lang5. 12). Koh tioh8 toa3 gun5 teng5-pe7,
iah8 tioh8 chiong lin2 poo3-te7-khau2, i heng5 lin2 e5 gun5, toa3
to3-tng2 khi3 hoo7--i; hit-e5 kiam2-chhai2 si7 sit-chho3; 13). iah8
chhoa7 lin2 sio2-ti7 khi2-sin, khi3 koh ki*3 hit-lang5. 14). Tok8-tok8
goan7 choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3 hoo7 lin2 ti7 hit-lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5
tit-tioh8 lin5-bin2; chiong lin2 hit e5 hia*-ti7 kap Pian7-nga2-bin2 kau
lin2; goa2 na7 sit-loh8 goa2 e5 kia*2, iah8 tioh8 hoo7 i sit-loh8
chiu7-si7. 15). Tui3 hit-tiap8 in toa3 hiah e5 le2-mih8, iah8 toa3 gun5
teng5-pe7, koh chhoa7 Pian7-nga2-bin2, khi2-sin loh8--khi3 Ai-kip8;
khia7 ti7 Iok-sek e5 bin7-cheng5.

16). Iok-sek khoa*3-ki*3 Pian7-nga2-bin2 kap in sa*-kap lai5, chiu7 tui3
koan2-ke--e5 kong2, Chhoa7 chiah e5 lang5 khi3 chhu3-lai7, thai5
cheng-si*, pi7-pan7 ian5-siah8; in-ui7 jit8-tau3, chiah e5 lang5 beh kap
goa2 sa*-kap chiah8. 17). Hit-lang5 chiu7 chiau3 Iok-sek e5 oe7 khi3
kia*5; chhoa7 in hiah e5 lang5 jip8 Iok-sek e5 chhu3. 18). Hiah e5
lang5, in-ui7 hoo7 i chhoa7 kau3 Iok-sek e5 chhu3, chiu7 kia*-hia*5;
kong2, Chhoa7 lan2 kau3 chia, tek-khak si7 in-ui7 thau5-chit8-pai2 heng5
lan2 ti7 poo3-te7-lai7 e5 gun5, beh chhe7 lan2 e5 khang-phang7, he7
chhiu2 hai7 lan2, kiong5-kiong5 liah8 lan2 choe3 loo5-pok8, chhiu*2 lan2
e5 lu5. 19). In chiu7 oa2-kun7 Iok-sek e5 koan2-ke--e5, ti7
chhu3-mng5-khau2 kap i kong2-oe7, 20). kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2 ah, goan2
thau5-pai2 loh8-lai5, sit8-chai7 si7 beh tiah8 bi2-niu5; 21). au7-lai5
kau3 hioh-mi5 e5 soo2-chai7, khui goan2 e5 poo3-te7, bo5 phah-sng3,
goan2 tak8-lang5 e5 gun5 chiok-soo3 iu5-gôan ti7 tak8-lang5 e5
poo3-te7-khau2; ta* goan2 u7 koh toa3--lai5; goan2 leng7-goa7 u7 koh
toa3 gun5 beh lai5 tiah8 bi2-niu5; 22). goan2 m7-chai chi7-chui7 chiong
goan2 e5 gun5 he7 ti7 goan2 e5 poo3-te7-lai7. 23). Koan2-ke--e5 kong2,
Choe3 lin2 an-sim, bian2 kia*; si7 lin2 e5 Siong7-te3, kap lin2 lau7-pe7
e5 Siong7-te3, siu*2-su3 lin2 chai5-po2 ti7 lin2 e5 poo3-te7-lai7; lin2
e5 gun5 goa2 i2-keng siu-liau2. Chiu7 chhoa7 Se-bian7 chhut-lai5 hoo7
in. 24). Hit-lang5 chiu7 chhoa7 hiah e5 lang5 jip8 Iok-sek e5 chhu3,
phang5 chui2 hoo7 in, in chiu7 soe2 kha; koh theh8 chhau2-liau7 chhi7 in
e5 lu5. 25). In chiu7 pi7-pan7 hiah e5 le2-mih8, theng3-hau7 Iok-sek
jit8-tau3 to3--lai5; in-ui7 in thia*-ki*3 beh ti7-hia chiah8.

26). Iok-sek to3--lai5 kau3 chhu3, in chiu7 chiong soo2 toa3--lai5 e5
le2-mih8 theh8 jip8 chhu3 sang3--i; koh phak ti7 toe7--nih pai3 i. 27).
Iok-sek mng7 in peng5-an; koh kong2, Lin2 e5 lau7-pe7, chiu7-si7 lin2
soo2 kong2 hit e5 lau7-lang5, peng5-an mah? i iau2 ti7--teh mah? 28). In
in3 kong2, Li2 e5 loo5-pok8, goan2 e5 lau7-pe7 peng5-an, i iau2 ti7-teh;
in chiu7 a*3-thau5 pai3 i. 29). Iok-sek kiah8-bak8 khoa*3-ki*3 i
tang5-bu2 e5 sio2-ti7, Pian7-nga2-bin2; chiu7 kong2, Li2 soo2 ka7 goa2
kong2 soah-be2 sio2-ti7, si7 chit-e5 mah? Koh kong2, Soe3-kia*2, goan7
Siong7-te3 si-un hoo7 li2. 30). Iok-sek thia*3 sio2-ti7 e5 cheng5 toa7
siu7 kek-tong7; chiu7 koa*2-kin2 chhe7 chit8-ui7 thang thi5-khau3; jip8
i e5 pang5-keng thi5-khau3; 31). au7-lai5 soe2-bin7 chhut-lai5,
bian2-kiong2 lun2--teh; hoan-hu3 khui-toh. 32). In chiu7 ui7 Iok-sek
leng7-goa7 pai5 chit8 te3 toh, ui7 hiah e5 lang5 koh pai5 chit8 te3,
iah8 ui7 kap Iok-sek sa*-kap chiah8 e5 Ai-kip8 lang5 leng7-goa7 pai5
chit8-te3; in-ui7 Ai-kip8 lang5 boe7 thang kap Hi-pek-lai5 lang5 sa*-kap
chiah8, che si7 Ai-kip8 lang5 soo2 iam3-oo*3. 33). Hiah e5 lang5 che7
ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5, toa7-soe3 chiau3 in ni5-he3 e5 chhu3-su7; hiah e5
lang5 tai7-ke gong5-ngiah8. 34). Iok-sek chiong i bin7-cheng5 e5
chiah8-mih8, pun hoo7 in; tok8-tok8 Pian7-nga2-bin2 soo2 tit-tioh8--e5,
pi2 pat8-lang5 goo7-pe7 choe7; in chiu7 lim chiu2, kap Iok-sek sa*-kap
ian3-lok8.


[44] Iok-sek hoan-hu3 koan2-ke--e5 kong2, chiong bi2-niu5 jip8 moa2
chiah e5 lang5 e5 poo3-te7, chin7 in soo2 oe7 toa3--e5; koh chiong
tak8-lang5 e5 gun5 lok ti7 i e5 poo3-te7-khau2. 2). Iah8 chiong goa2 e5
poe, chiu7-si7 hit te3 gun5-poe, he7 ti7 siau3-lian5--e5 e5
poo3-te7-khau2; i tiah8 goo7-kak e5 gun5 iah8 soa3 he7--teh.
Koan2-ke--e5 chiu7 chiau3 Iok-sek soo2 kong2 e5 oe7 khi3 kia*5. 3). Thi*
chit8-e7 kng, chiu7 chhe hiah e5 lang5 kap in e5 lu5 khi3. 4). In chhut
sia*5 kia*5 bo5 joa7-hng7, Iok-sek ka7 koan2-ke--e5 kong2, Khi2--lai5,
khi3 tui-jip hiah e5 lang5, tui-tioh8, chiu7 ka7 in kong2, Lin2
sia*2-su7 eng7 phai*2 po3 ho2 ah? 5). Che kiam2 m7-si7 goa2 e5
chu2-lang5 lim-chiu2 e5 poe mah? Kiam2 m7-si7 i chiam-pok teh eng7--e5
mah? lin2 an2-ni choe3 si7 phai*2. 6). Koan2-ke--e5 tui-tioh8 in, chiong
chiah e5 oe7 ka7 in kong2. 7). In in3 kong2, goa2 e5 chu2 sia*2-su7
kong2 chit ho7 oe7? li2 e5 loo5-pok8 toan3-toan3 bo5 choe3 chit-ho7 su7.
8). Li2 khoa*3, goan2 cheng5 ti7 poo3-te7-khau2 soo2 khoa*3-ki*3 e5
gun5, siong7-chhia*2 tui3 Ka-lam5 toe7 toa3--lai5 heng5 li2; goan2
thai2-tho2 oe7 tui3 li2 chu2-lang5 e5 ke thau-theh8 kim-gun5 ah? 9). Li2
e5 loo5-pok8 e5 tiong-kan, bo5-lun7 ti7 sim2-mih8 lang5 hia
chhiau--tioh8, chiu7 hoo7 i si2, goan2 iah8 beh choe3 goa2 e5 chu2-lang5
e5 loo5-pok8. 10). Koan2-ke--e5 kong2, Ta* chiu7 chiau3 lin2 e5 oe7
kia*5; ti7 sim2-mih8 lang5 hia chhiau--tioh8, hit-lang5 chiu7 choe3 goa2
e5 loo5-pok8; ki5-u5--e5 long2 bo5 choe7. 11). Tui3 hit-tiap8 in
tak8-lang5 koa*2-kin2 chiong poo3-te7 sia3 ti7 thoo5-kha, tak8-lang5
thau2-khui in e5 poo3-te7. 12). Koan2-ke--e5 chiu7 chhiau, tui3 toa7--e5
khi2, kau3 soe3--e5 chi2; hit e5 poe keng2-jian5 ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5
poo3-te7-lai7 chhiau--tioh. 13). In chiu7 thiah-lih8 in e5 sa*,
tak8-lang5 chiong in e5 mih8 hoo7 lu5 chai3, to3--khi3 sia*5-lai7. 14).
Iu5-tai7 kap i e5 hia*-ti7 kau3 Iok-sek e5 chhu3, Iok-sek iau2 ti7-hia,
in chiu7 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5 phak-loh8 toe7. 15). Iok-sek ka7 in kong2,
Lin2 soo2-choe3--e5 si7 sim2-mih8 su7? lin2 kiam2 m7-chai, chhin-chhiu*7
goa2 chit-ho7 e5 lang5 oe7 chiam-pok mah? 16). Iu5-tai7 kong2, Goan2
tui3 goa2 e5 chu2 beh kong2 sim2-mih8? iau2 u7 sia*2 oe7 thang kong2?
goan2 thai2 oe7 ka-ki7 soo3-beng5 ah? Siong7-te3 i2-keng cha-chhut li2
e5 loo5-pok8 e5 choe7-koa3, goan2 kap hit-e5 ti7 i e5 chhiu2 chhiau
tioh8 poe--e5, long2 si7 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 loo5-pok8. 17). Iok-sek kong2,
Goa2 toan3-toan3 bo5 beh an2-ni choe3; Ti7 sim2-mih8 lang5 e5 chhiu2
chhiau tioh8 poe, hit-lang5 chiu7 tioh8 choe3 goa2 e5 loo5-pok8; lin2
chiah-e5 thang peng5-an chiu*7 khi3 lin2 lau7-pe7 hia.

18). Iu5-tai7 oa2-kun7 i kong2, Goa2 e5 chu2 ah, kiu5 li2 iong5-un2 li2
e5 loo5-pok8 kong2 chit8-ku3-oe7 hoo7 goa2 e5 chu2 thia*, boh8-tit
siu7-khi3 li2 e5 loo5-pok8; in-ui7 li2 kap Hoat-lo2 chit8-iu*7. 19).
Goa2 e5 chu2 bat mng7 li2 chiah e5 loo5-pok8 kong2, Lin2 u7 lau7-pe7, u7
hia*-ti7 bo5? 20). Goan2 ka7 goa2 e5 chu2 kong2, Goan2 u7 lau7-pe7,
i2-keng ni5-lau7; iau2 u7 i ni5-lau7 soo2 si* chit8 e5 soah-be2 kia*2; i
e5 hia* i2-keng si2, i e5 lau7-bu2 kan-ta pang3 i chit8-e5, koh i e5
lau7-pe7 chin thia*3--i. 21). Li2 ka7 li2 e5 loo5-pok8 kong2, Chhoa7 i
loh8--lai5 goa2 chia, hoo7 goa2 chhin-bak8 khoa*3-ki*3 i. 22). Goan2 ka7
goa2 e5 chu2 kong2, Gin2-a2 boe7-oe7 li7-khui i e5 lau7-pe7; na7
li7-khui i e5 lau7-pe7, lau7-pe7 tek-khak si2. 23). Li2 ka7 li2 e5
loo5-pok8 kong2, Lin2 e5 soah-be2 sio2-ti7 na7 bo5 kap lin2 sa*-kap
loh8--lai5, lin2 chiu7 boe7-tit koh ki*3 goa2 e5 bin7. 24). Goan2 chiu*7
kau3 li2 e5 loo5-pok8, goan2 lau7-pe7 hia, chiu7 chiong goa2 e5 chu2 e5
oe7 ka7 i kong2. 25). Goan2 e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Lin2 koh khi3 ka7 lan2
tiah8 tam7-poh8 bi2-niu5 lai5. 26). Goan2 chiu7 kong2, Goan2 boe7-oe7
loh8-khi3; goan2 e5 soah-be2 sio2-ti7 na7 kap goan2 sa*-kap khi3, goan2
chiu7 beh loh8--khi3; in-ui7 soah-be2 sio2-ti7 na7 bo5 kap goan2 sa*-kap
khi3, goan2 tek-khak boe7-tit ki*3 hit-lang5 e5 bin7. 27). Li2 e5
loo5-pok8, goa2 e5 lau7-pe7, ka7 goan2 kong2, Lin2 chai goa2 e5 boo2 ka7
goa2 si* nng7 e5 kia*2; 28). chit8-e5 li7-khui goa2 chhut-khi3, goa2
kong2 i tek-khak si7 hoo7 ia2-siu3 thiah-chhui3; kau3-ta* goa2 iau2
m7-bat khoa*3-ki*3; 29). ta* lin2 koh chiong chit-e5 chhoa7-khi3,
li7-khui goa2; na7 i tu2-tioh8 ham7-hai7, chiu7-si7 lin2 hoo7 goa2
peh8-thau5-mng5 chhi*-chham2 loh8 im-hu2. 30). Goan2 lau7-pe7 e5
si*3-mia7 kap chit e5 gin2-a2 e5 si*3-mia7 si* sa*-lian5; ta* goa2
to3--khi3 li2 e5 loo5-pok8 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 hia; na7 gin2-a2 bo5 kap
goan2 sa*-kap ti7-teh, goan2 e5 lau7-pe7 khoa*3 bo5 gin2-a2, i chiu7
tek-khak si2. 31). che chiu7-si7 goan2 hoo7 li2 e5 loo5-pok8, goan2 e5
lau7-pe7, peh8-thau5-mng5 chhi*-chham2 loh8 im-hu2. 32). In-ui7 li2 e5
loo5-pok8 bat tui3 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 po2 chit e5 gin2-a2, kong2, Goa2 na7
bo5 chhoa7 i to3--lai5 kau li2, goa2 goan7 ti7 lau7-pe7 e5 bin7-cheng5
it-seng tam-tng choe7. 33). Ta* kiu5 li2 iong5-un2 li2 e5 loo5-pok8
tiam3--teh, thoe3 chit e5 gin2-a2 choe3 goa2 e5 chu2 e5 loo5-pok8; hoo7
gin2-a2 kap i hiah e5 hia* sa*-kap chiu*7--khi3. 34). Na7 gin2-a2 bo5
kap goa2 sa*-kap khi3, goa2 thai2-tho2 oe7 chiu*7-khi3 ki*3 goa2 e5
lau7-pe7 ah? kia*-liau2 goa2 khoa*3-ki*3 goan2 lau7-pe7 soo2 tu2-tioh8
e5 chai-e7.


[45] Iok-sek ti7 hiah-e5 khia7 i sin-pi* e5 lang5 e5 bin7-cheng5
lun2-boe7-tiau5; chiu7 hoah kong2, Cheng3-lang5 tioh8 li7-khui goa2
chhut-khi3. Iok-sek chiong i pun2-sin hoo7 hia*-ti7 jin7-tit e5 si5, bo5
chit8-lang5 khia7 ti7 i e5 bin7-cheng5. 2). I chiu7 chhut-sia*
toa7-khau3; Ai-kip8 lang5 thia*-ki*3, Hoat-lo2 e5 ke iah8 thia*-ki*3.
3). Iok-sek ka7 i e5 hia*-ti7 kong2, Goa2 si7 Iok-sek, goa2 e5 lau7-pe7
iau2 ti7-teh mah? I e5 hia*-ti7 boe7-oe7 in3, in-ui7 ti7 i e5
bin7-cheng5 long2 kia*-hia*5. 4). Iok-sek koh ka7 i e5 hia*-ti7 kong2,
Chhia*2 kia*5-oa2--lai5. In chiu7 oa2--lai5. I kong2, Goa2 si7 lin2 e5
sio2-ti7 Iok-sek, chiu7-si7 lin2 soo2 boe7 kau3 Ai-kip8--e5. 5). Ta*
m7-bian2 in-ui7 boe7 goa2 kau3 chia lai5 iu-bun7, lai5 ka-ki7 oan3-hun7;
che si7 Siong7-te3 chhe goa2 tai7-seng lin2 lai5, in-ui7 beh po2-choan5
si*3-mia7. 6). Ta* ti7 chit soo2-chai7 e5 ki-hng i2-keng nng7-ni5, iau2
u7 goo7-ni5, bo5 thang cheng3-choh, bo5 thang siu-seng5. 7). Siong7-te3
chhe goa2 tai7-seng lin2 lai5, ui7-tioh8 beh ka7 lin2 lau5 chhun e5
cheng2-chok8 ti7 se3-chiu*7; koh beh kia*5 I toa7 e5 chin2-kiu3,
po2-choan5 lin2 e5 oah8-mia7. 8). An2-ni khoa*3--khi2-lai5, chhe goa2
kau3 chia e5, m7-si7 lin2, chiu7-si7 Siong7-te3; I koh hoo7 goa2
chhin-chhiu*7 Hoat-lo2 e5 pe7, choe3 i choan5-ke e5 chu2, kap koan2-li2
Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7. 9). Lin2 tioh8 koa*2-kin2 chiu*7-khi3 goa2 e5
lau7-pe7 hia, ka7 i kong2, Li2 e5 kia*2 Iok-sek an2-ni kong2, Siong7-te3
hoo7 goa2 choe3 choan5 Ai-kip8 e5 chu2, chhia*2 loh8--lai5 goa2 chia,
m7-thang ian5-chhian5. 10). Li2 kap li2 e5 kia*2 li2 e5 sun, kap
gu5-kun5 iu*5-kun5, i2-kip8 it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5, long2 thang lai5 tiam3
ti7 Ko-san e5 toe7, kap goa2 sa*-kun7. 11). Goa2 beh ti7-hia hong7-seng5
li2; in-ui7 iau2 u7 goo7 ni5 e5 ki-hng, bian2-tit li2, kap li2 e5
ke-koan3, kap it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5 loh8-poh8. 12). Ho5-hong3 lin2 e5
bak8-chiu kap goa2 e5 sio2-ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 bak8-chiu long2
khoa*3-ki*3 goa2 kap lin2 chhin-chhui3 tui3 lin2 kong2-oe7. 13). Lin2
ia7 tioh8 chiong goa2 ti7 Ai-kip8 it-chhe3 e5 eng5-kng kap lin2 soo2
khoa*3-ki*3 e5 su7, long2 ka7 goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 kong2; koh tioh8
koa*2-kin2 chiong goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 poa*--lai5 goa2 chia. 14). Tui3
an2-ni Iok-sek phak ti7 i e5 sio2-ti7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 am7-kun2
thi5-khau5; Pian7-nga2-bin2 ia7 ti7 i e5 am7-kun2 thi5-khau3. 15). I koh
kap cheng3 hia*-ti7 chim-chhui3, pho7--in thi5-khau3; au7-lai5 i e5
hia*-ti7 chiu7 kap i kong2-oe7.

16). Chit e5 hong-sia* thoan5 kau3 Hoat-lo2 e5 keng-lai7, kong2, Iok-sek
e5 hia*-ti7 lai5 lah. Hoat-lo2 kap i e5 jin5-sin5 long2 hoa*-hi2. 17).
Hoat-lo2 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Li2 tioh8 ka7 li2 e5 hia*-ti7 kong2, Lin2
tioh8 an2-ni kia*5; chiong mih8 hoo7 cheng-si* chai3; khi2-sin khi3
Ka-lam5 toe7; 18). chiong lin2 e5 lau7-pe7, kap lin2 e5 ke-koan3, long2
poa*--lai5 goa2 chia; goa2 beh chiong Ai-kip8 toe7 e5 ho2-mih8 hoo7
lin2, lin2 iah8 thang chiah8 chit soo2-chai7 e5 san-tin hai2-bi7. 19).
Ta* goa2 beng7-leng7 li2, lin2 tioh8 an2-ni choe3; tui3 Ai-kip8 toe7
toa3 chhia khi3, chiong lin2 e5 gin2-a2, kap boo2, kap lin2 e5 lau7-pe7,
long2 poa*--lai5. 20). M7-thang khoa*3-tang7 lin2 ke-lai7 e5 mih8,
in-ui7 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7 e5 ho2-mih8, long2 si7 lin2 e5.

21). I2-sek-liat8 e5 cheng3-kia*2 chiu7 an2-ni kia*5. Iok-sek chiau3
Hoat-lo2 e5 beng7-leng7 hoo7 in chhia, kap loo7-tiong tioh8 eng7 e5
chiah8-mih8; 22). koh hoo7 in chit8-lang5 chit8-tho3 i-hok8; tok8-tok8
hoo7 Pian7-nga2-bin2 gun5 sa*-pah, i-hok8 goo7-tho3. 23). Sang3 in
lau7-pe7 e5 mih8, ki3 ti7 e7-toe2; lu5-kang2 chap8-chiah, chai3 Ai-kip8
e5 ho2-mih8; lu5-bu2 chap8-chiah, chai3 goo7-kak kap pia*2 kap chhai3,
hoo7 in lau7-pe7 loo7--nih thang eng7. 24). Iok-sek chiu7 chhe i e5
hia*-ti7 to3--khi3, in chiu7 khi2-sin; koh ka7 in kong2, Lin2 m7-thang
ti7 loo7--nih oan-ke. 25). In tui3 Ai-kip8 chiu*7--khi3, lai5 kau3
Ka-lam5 toe7, in lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok hia. 26). Ka7 i kong2, Iok-sek iau2
ti7-teh, koh koan2-li2 Ai-kip8 choan5-toe7. Nga2-kok sim hun7--khi3,
in-ui7 m7 sin3 in e5 oe7. 27). In chiu7 chiong Iok-sek tui3 in soo2
kong2 e5 oe7, long2 ka7 i kong2; i koh khoa*3-ki*3 Iok-sek soo2
chhe--lai5 beh chai3 i e5 chhia, in lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok e5 sim
oah8--khi2-lai5. 28). I2-sek-liat8 kong2, Ho2 lah; goa2 e5 kia*2 Iok-sek
iau2 ti7-teh, than3 goa2 iau2-be7 si2, goa2 beh khi3 khoa*3--i.


[46] I2-sek-liat8 toa3 it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5, khi2-sin lai5 kau3
Piat8-si7-pa; chiu7 hian3-che3 hoo7 i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sat e5 Siong7-te3.
2). Mi5-si5 Siong7-te3 ti7 i*7-siong7 e5 tiong-kan ka7 I2-sek-liat8
kong2, Nga2-kok ah, Nga2-kok ah. I kong2, Goa2 ti7-chia. 3). Siong7-te3
