kong2, Goa2 si7 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 Siong7-te3; li2
loh8--khi3 Ai-kip8 m7-sai2 kia*; in-ui7 Goa2 beh hoo7 li2 ti7-hia
chia*5-choe3 toa7-kok. 4). Goa2 beh kap li2 sa*-kap loh8--khi3 Ai-kip8,
Goa2 iah8 tek-khak chhoa7 li2 khi2-lai5; Iok-sek beh chhiu2 hoa*7 li2 e5
bak8-chiu, hoo7 li2 khoeh. 5). Nga2-kok chiu7 tui3 Piat8-si7-pa
khi2-sin; I2-sek-liat8 hiah e5 kia*2, hoo7 in e5 lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok, kap
in e5 kia*2-ji5, in e5 boo2, long2 che7 ti7 Hoat-lo2 soo2 chhe--lai5 beh
chai3 i e5 chhia. 6). Nga2-kok kap i it-chhe3 e5 kia*2-sun, toa3 in e5
cheng-si*, i2-kip8 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 soo2 tit-tioh8 e5 he3-chai5, long2
kau3 Ai-kip8. 7). Nga2-kok toa3 i e5 kia*2, sun, cha-boo2-kia*2,
cha-boo2-sun, kap i it-chhe3 e5 hoo7-e3, long2 kau3 Ai-kip8.

8). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 kau3 Ai-kip8--e5, Nga2-kok kap i e5 kia*2, in e5
mia5 ki3 ti7 e7-toe2. 9). Nga2-kok e5 toa7-kia*2 Liu5-pian7. 9).
Liu5-pian7 e5 kia*2; Hap-lok8, Hoat-loo7, Hi-su-lun5, Ka-bi2. 10).
Se-bian7 e5 kia*2; Ia5-boo2-li2, Nga2-bin2, O-hat, Nga2-kun, So2-hat;
iau2 u7 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 hu7-jin5-lang5 e5 kia*2 So3-lo5. 11). Li7-bi7 e5
kia*2; Kek-sun7, Kho-hat, Bi2-lah8-li7. 12). Iu5-tai7 e5 kia*2; Ji*2,
Go5-lam5, Si7-lah8, Hoat-lek8-su, Sia7-lah8; tok8-tok8 Ji*2 kap Go5-lam5
si2 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7. Hoat-lek8-su e5 kia*2; Hi-su-lun5, Hap-boo2-lek8.
13). I2-sat-ka e5 kia*2; To5-lah8, Phoo2-oa2, Iok-pek, Sin-lun5. 14).
Se-poo3-lun5 e5 kia*2; Se-liat8, I2-lun5, Nga2-li7. 15). Chiah-e5 si7
Li7-a ti7 Pa-tan3-a-lan5 ka7 Nga2-kok soo2 si* e5 kia*2; koh u7 i e5
cha-boo2-kia*2 Ti2-na2; kia*2-sun lam5-lu2 kiong7 sa*-chap8-sa* lang5.
16). Ka-tek e5 kia*2; Se2-hui-un5, Hap-ki, Su-ni5, I2-su-pun2, I2-li7,
A-lo5-ti2, A-liat8-li7. 17). A-siat e5 kia*2; Im-na2, Ek-si-oa2,
Ek-si-ui2, Pi2-li7-a; koh in e5 sio2-be7 Se-lah8. Pi2-li7-a e5 kia*2;
Hi-piat, Ma2-kiat. 18). Che si7 Lah8-pan hoo7 i e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 Li7-a
e5 lu2-pi7 Sek-pha*3 soo2 si* e5 kia*2-sun; chiu7-si7 i ka7 Nga2-kok
si*--e5; kiong7 chap8-lak8 lang5. 19). Nga2-kok e5 boo2 Lah8-kiat e5
kia*2; Iok-sek kap Pian7-nga2-bin2. 20). Iok-sek ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 si*
Ma2-na2-se kap I2-hoat-lian5; chiu7-si7 An-sia*5 e5 che3-si,
Pho-the5-hui-lah8 e5 cha-boo2-kia*2, A-se-lap8, ka7 Iok-sek si*--e5.
21). Pian7-nga2-bin2 e5 kia*2; Pi2-lah8, Pi2-kiat, A-sit8-piat8,
Ki-lah8, Nai2-ban7, I2-hi, Lo5-sit8, Boo2-peng5, Hoo7-peng5, A-lek8;
22). che si7 Lah8-kiat ka7 Nga2-kok soo2 si* e5 kia*2-sun, kiong7
chap8-si3 lang5. 23). Tan3 e5 kia*2, Hoo7-sin. 24). Na2-hut-tha-li7 e5
kia*2; Nga2-siat, Koo-ni5, Ia5-sek, Si7-leng2; 25). che si7 Lah8-pan
hoo7 i e5 cha-boo2-kia*2 Lah8-kiat e5 lu2-pi7 Phek-lah8 soo2 si* e5
kia*2-sun, chiu7-si7 i ka7 Nga2-kok soo2 si*--e5; kiong7 chhit-lang5.
26). Hiah-e5 kap Nga2-kok sa*-kap kau3 Ai-kip8--e5, tu5 i e5 sim-pu7
i2-goa7, ki*3-na7 tui3 i sin-khu soo2 chhut--e5, kiong7 lak8-chap8-lak8
lang5. 27). Koh u7 Iok-sek ti7 Ai-kip8 soo2 si* e5 kia*2, nng7-e5;
Nga2-kok e5 ke lai5 kau3 Ai-kip8--e5 kiong7 chhit-chap8 lang5.

28). Nga2-kok chhe Iu5-tai7 choe3-thau5 khi3 ki*3 Iok-sek, thang chhoa7
in khi3 Ko-san; in chiu7 kau3 Ko-san e5 toe7. 29). Iok-sek pi7-pan7 i e5
chhia; khi3 Ko-san, ngia5-chih i e5 lau7-pe7 I2-sek-liat8; kau3
ki*3--tioh8 bin7, chiu7 phak ti7 lau7-pe7 e5 am7-kun2, ti7 am7-kun2--nih
khau3 ku2-ku2. 30). I2-sek-liat8 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 ki*3--tioh8 li2
e5 bin7, chai li2 iau2 oah8--teh, goa2 ta* si2 iah8 kam-sim. 31).
Iok-sek ka7 i e5 hia*-ti7 kap lau7-pe7 e5 ke kong2, Goa2 beh chiu*7-khi3
thong-ti Hoat-lo2, ka7 i kong2, Goa2 e5 hia*-ti7 kap goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5
ke, cheng5 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7--e5, ta* long2 lai5 kau3 goa2 chia. 32). In
si7 bok8-chia2, in-ui7 in si7 chhi7 cheng-si* e5 lang5; in chiong
iu*5-kun5, gu5-kun5, kap it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5 long2 toa3--lai5. 33).
Hoat-lo2 tiau3 lin2 e5 si5, na7 mng7 lin2 kong2, Lin2 choe3 sim2-mih8
thau5-loo7? 34). lin2 tioh8 kong2, Li2 e5 loo5-pok8, tui3 siau3-lian5
kau3-ta*, goan2 lian5 goan2 e5 choo2-kong long2 si7 teh chhi7 cheng-si*;
an2-ni lin2 thang lai5 khia7 ti7 Ko-san e5 toe7; in-ui7 ki*3-na7 chhi7
cheng-si*--e5, long2 si7 Ai-kip8 lang5 soo2 iam3-chian7.


[47] Iok-sek jip8--khi3 ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Goa2 e5 lau7-pe7 kap goa2 e5
hia*-ti7 toa3 in e5 iu*5-kun5, gu5-kun5, kap it-chhe3 soo2-u7--e5, tui3
Ka-lam5 toe7 lai5; ta* ti7 Ko-san e5 toe7. 2). Iok-sek tui3 i e5
hia*-ti7 e5 tiong-kan keng2 goo7 lang5, chhoa7 in khi3 ki*3 Hoat-lo2.
3). Hoat-lo2 mng7 Iok-sek e5 hia*-ti7 kong2, Lin2 choe3 sim2-mih8
thau5-loo7? In ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, Li2 e5 loo5-pok8 pun2-sin, kap goan2
e5 choo2-kong, long2 si7 koo3-iu*5 e5 lang5. 4). In koh ka7 Hoat-lo2
kong2, Ka-lam5 toe7 ki-hng chin siong-tiong7, loo5-pok8 e5 iu*5-kun5 bo5
chhau2 thang chiah8; soo2-i2 goan2 lai5, si7 beh kia3-kha ti7-chia; ta*
kiu5 li2 iong5-un2 li2 e5 loo5-pok8 tiam3 ti7 Ko-san toe7. 5). Hoat-lo2
ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 kap li2 e5 hia*-ti7 lai5 kau3 li2
chia; 6). Ai-kip8 toe7 long2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5; hoo7 li2 e5
lau7-pe7 kap li2 e5 hia*-ti7 toa3 ti7 kok-lai7 te7 it ho2 e5 toe7; in
thang toa3 ti7 Ko-san e5 toe7; li2 na7 chai in tiong-kan khah u7
pun2-su7 e5 lang5, chiu7 phai3 in koan2-koo3 goa2 e5 cheng-si*. 7).
Iok-sek chhoa7 i e5 lau7-pe7 Nga2-kok jip8--khi3 khia7 ti7 Hoat-lo2 e5
bin7-cheng5; Nga2-kok chiu7 ka7 Hoat-lo2 chiok-hok. 8). Hoat-lo2 mng7
Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 it-seng e5 ni5-jit8 si7 joa7-choe7 ah? 9). Nga2-kok
ka7 Hoat-lo2 kong2, goa2 kia3-kha ti7 se3-kan e5 ni5-jit8 si7 chit8-pah
sa*-chap8 he3. Goa2 it-seng e5 ni5-jit8 iah8 chio2, iah8 kan-khoo2,
m7-tat8-tioh8 goa2 e5 liat8-choo2 kia3-kha ti7 se3-kan e5 ni5-jit8. 10).
Nga2-kok koh ka7 Hoat-lo2 chiok-hok; chiu7 tui3 Hoat-lo2 e5 bin7-cheng5
chhut-khi3. 11). Iok-sek chiau3 Hoat-lo2 e5 beng7-leng7, chiong Ai-kip8
kok te7-it ho2 e5 toe7, chiu7-si7 Lan5-sek e5 toe7, hoo7 i e5 lau7-pe7
kap i hia*-ti7 khia7-khi2, choe3 san2-giap8. 12). Iok-sek eng7 bi2-niu5
hong7-seng5 i e5 lau7-pe7, kap i e5 hia*-ti7, kap i e5 lau7-pe7
choan5-ke; long2 chiau3 in e5 lang5-giah8 lai5 kiong-kip in.

13). Ki-hng chin siong-tiong7, choan5-toe7 long2 bo5 bi2-niu5; sim7-chi3
Ai-kip8 toe7 kap Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 lang5, in-ui7 ki-hng e5 ian5-koo3, go7
kau3 hun7--khi3. 14). Iok-sek chu7-chip8 Ai-kip8 toe7 kap Ka-lam5 toe7
soo2 u7 e5 gun5, chiu7-si7 in tiah8 bi2-niu5 e5 gun5; Iok-sek chiu7
chiong hiah e5 gun5 toa3 kau3 Hoat-lo2 e5 keng. 15). Ai-kip8 toe7 kap
Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 gun5 long2 eng7-liau2; Ai-kip8 cheng3-lang5 long2 lai5
ki*3 Iok-sek kong2, Goan2 e5 gun5 long2 eng7-liau2 lah, kiu5 li2 hoo7
goan2 bi2-niu5; goan2 sia*2-su7 tioh8 si2 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5? 16).
Iok-sek kong2, Na7 si7 gun5 eng7-liau2, lin2 e5 cheng-si* thang
khan--lai5; goa2 ui7-tioh8 lin2 e5 cheng-si* beh hoo7 lin2 bi2-niu5.
17). In chiu7 chiong cheng-si* koa*2 kau3 Iok-sek hia; Iok-sek chiu7
eng7 bi2-niu5 oa*7 in e5 be2, iu*5-kun5, gu5-kun5, kap lu5; hit-ni5
ui7-tioh8 oa*7 in it-chhe3 e5 cheng-si*, chiu7 eng7 bi2-niu5 iu*2-chhi7
in. 18). Hit-ni5 i2-keng ke3; te7-ji7 ni5, in koh lai5 ki*3 Iok-sek, ka7
i kong2, Goan2 boe7 moa5--tit goa2 e5 chu2, goan2 e5 gun5 long2
eng7-liau2, cheng-si* iah8 long2 kui ti7 goa2 e5 chu2, goan2 ti7 goa2 e5
chu2 e5 bin7-cheng5, tu5 goan2 e5 sin-the2 kap goan2 e5 chhan5-toe7
i2-goa7, bo5 chhun chit8-hang7. 19). goan2 sia*2-su7 lang5 si2, toe7
pha-hng, ti7 li2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5 ah? kiu5 li2 eng7 bi2-niu5 boe2
goan2 kap goan2 e5 toe7; goan2 kap goan2 e5 toe7 choe3 Hoat-lo2 e5
loo7-eng7; koh eng7 cheng2-chi2 hoo7 goan2, hoo7 goan2 tit-tioh8 oah8,
bian2 si2, thoo2-toe7 iah8 bian2 pha-hng.

20). Tui3 an2-ni Iok-sek ui7 Hoat-lo2 boe2 Ai-kip8 soo2 u7 e5 toe7;
Ai-kip8 lang5 in-ui7 hoo7 ki-hng soo2 pek, tak8-lang5 long2 boe7 i e5
chhan5-toe7; hiah e5 toe7 chiu7 long2 kui ti7 Hoat-lo2. 21). Iok-sek
chiau3 chiah e5 sia*5-ip chhian-soa2 Ai-kip8 e5 peh-si*3 tui3 Ai-kip8
chit-peng5 kau3 ti7 hit-peng5. 22). Tok8-tok8 che3-si e5 toe7 Hoat-lo2
bo5 boe2--i; in-ui7 che3-si u7 tui3 Hoat-lo2 tit-tioh8 tia*7-tioh8 e5
niu5; in chiah8 Hoat-lo2 soo2 hoo7 in e5 niu5; soo2-i2 in bo5 boe7 in e5
toe7. 23). Iok-sek ka7 peh-si*3 kong2, Goa2 kin-a2-jit8 ui7 Hoat-lo2
boe2 lin2 kap lin2 e5 toe7; khoa*3 ah, ti7-chia u7 cheng2-chi2 hoo7
lin2, lin2 thang khi3 choh-chhan5; 24). kau3 siu-seng5 e5 si5, lin2
tioh8 chiong goo7-hun7-chit8 lap8 hoo7 Hoat-lo2; si3-hun7 kui lin2,
choe3 chhan5--nih e5 cheng2-chi2, iah8 choe3 lin2 kap lin2 ke-lai7 lang5
e5 chiah8-mih8, i2-kip8 lin2 e5 gin2-a2 e5 chiah8-mih8. 25). In kong2,
Li2 u7 kiu3 goan2 e5 si*3-mia7; goan7 goan2 ti7 goa2 e5 chu2 e5
bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, goan2 beh choe3 Hoat-lo2 e5 loo5-pok8.
26). An2-ni Iok-sek ui7 Ai-kip8 e5 toe7, siat-lip8 tia*7-tioh8 e5 le7,
kau3 ti7 kin-a2-jit8; Hoat-lo2 tit-tioh8 goo7-hun7 e5 chit8-hun7;
tok8-tok8 che3-si e5 toe7 bo5 kui Hoat-lo2.

27). I2-sek-liat8 lang5 khia7-khi2 Ai-kip8 kok, Ko-san e5 toe7, in
ti7-hia kian3-ti3 san2-giap8, koh si*-thoa*3 kek8-ki5 choe7. 28).
Nga2-kok tiam3 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7 chap8-chhit ni5. Nga2-kok it-seng e5
ni5-jit8 si7 chit8-pah si3-chap8-chhit he3. 29). I2-sek-liat8 si2 e5
jit8 kun7 lah; i chiu7 kio3 i e5 kia*2 Iok-sek lai5, ka7 i kong2, Goa2
na7 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8 un-tian2, chhia*2 li2 he7 chhiu2
ti7 goa2 e5 toa7-thui2-e7, eng7 chu5-ai3 kap seng5-sit8 khoan2-thai7
goa2; m7-thang bai5-chong3 goa2 ti7 Ai-kip8. Goa2 kap goa2 e5 pe7-kong
tang5-khun3 e5 si5, li2 tioh8 chiong goa2 toa3 chhut Ai-kip8,
bai5-chong3 ti7 in bai5-chong3 e5 toe7. Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 beh chiau3
li2 e5 oe7 lai5 kia*5. 31). Nga2-kok kong2, Li2 tioh8 tui3 goa2
chiu3-choa7; i chiu7 tui3 i chiu3-choa7. Tui3 an2-ni I2-sek-liat8 oa3
chhng-thau5 keng3-pai3 Siong7-te3.


[48] Chiah e5 tai7-chi3 liau2-au7, u7 lang5 ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Lin2
lau7-pe7 phoa3-pi*7 lah; i chiu7 chhoa7 i nng7 e5 kia*2 Ma2-na2-se,
I2-hoat-lian5, sa*-kap khi3. 2). U7 lang5 thong-ti Nga2-kok kong2, Li2
khoa*3, li2 e5 kia*2 Iok-sek lai5 beh chhe7 li2; I2-sek-liat8 chiu7
bian2-kiong2 khi2-lai5, che7 ti7 bin5-chhng5. 3). Nga2-kok ka7 Iok-sek
kong2, Choan5-leng5 e5 Siong7-te3 bat ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7 e5 Loo7-su tui3
goa2 chhut-hian7, su3-hok goa2; 4). ka7 goa2 kong2, Goa2 beh hoo7 li2
si*-thoa*3 choe7-choe7, chia*5-choe3 choe7-choe7 peh-si*3; iah8 beh
chiong chit e5 toe7 siu*2-su3 li2 e5 hoo7-e3, choe3 eng2-oan2 e5 giap8.
5). Goa2 be7 kau3 Ai-kip8 li2 chia e5 tai7-seng, li2 ti7 Ai-kip8 toe7
soo2 si* nng7 e5 kia*2, I2-hoat-lian5 Ma2-na2-se, si7 goa2-e5,
chhin-chhiu*7 Liu5-pian7 Se-bian7 si7 goa2-e5 chit8-iu*7. 6). Ti7 in
i2-au7, li2 soo2 si* e5 kia*2, chiu7-si7 li2 e5; in thang kui ti7 in
nng7 e5 hia* e5 mia5-e7, tit-tioh8 giap8. 7). Lun7-kau3 goa2, goa2 tui3
Pa-tan3 lai5 e5 si5, Lah8-kiat si2 ti7 goa2 e5 bak8-chiu-cheng5, ti7
Ka-lam5 toe7, ti7 loo7--nih e5 tiong-kan, li7-khui I2-hoat-tha iau2 u7
chit8-cham7; goa2 chiu7 ka7 i bai5-chong3 ti7 I2-hoat-tha e5 loo7.
(I2-hoat-tha chiu7-si7 Pek-li7-heng5).

8). I2-sek-liat8 khoa*3-ki*3 Iok-sek nng7 e5 kia*2, chiu7 kong2, Che si7
chi7-chui7? 9). Iok-sek ka7 in lau7-pe7 kong2, Che si7 goa2 e5 kia*2,
Siong7-te3 ti7-chia siu*2-su3 goa2--e5. Kong2, Chhia*2 li2 chhoa7 in
oa2-kun7 goa2; goa2 beh ka7 in chiok-hok. 10). I2-sek-liat8 ni5-lau7,
bak8-chiu hoe boe7 khoa*3-ki*3; Iok-sek chhoa7 in kun7-oa2 i e5
bin7-cheng5, i chiu7 ka7 in chim-chhui3 pho7 in. 11). I2-sek-liat8 ka7
Iok-sek kong2, Goa2 bo5 phah-sng3 oe7 ki*3-tioh8 li2 e5 bin7; ta*
Siong7-te3 koh hoo7 goa2 khoa*3-tioh8 li2 e5 kia*2. 12). Iok-sek chiong
nng7 e5 kia*2 tui3 i nng7 e5 kha-thau5-u-tiong chhoa7--chhut-lai5;
pun2-sin chiu7 phak-loh8 toe7 pai3. 13). Au7-lai5 Iok-sek koh khan in
nng7-e5, chia*3-chhiu2 khan I2-hoat-lian5 ng3 I2-sek-liat8 e5
to3-chhiu2, to3-chhiu2 khan Ma2-na2-se ng3 I2-sek-liat8 e5
chia*3-chhiu2, chhoa7 in kun7-oa2 i. 14). I2-sek-liat8 chhun
chia*3-chhiu2 hoa*7 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 thau5-khak, i si7 te7-ji7--e5, koh
phah-chhe eng7 to3-chhiu2 hoa*7 Ma2-na2-se e5 thau5-khak, Ma2-na2-se
pun2 si7 toa7-kia*2. 15). I chiu7 ka7 Iok-sek chiok-hok kong2, Goan7
goa2 e5 choo2 A-pek-lah8-han2, kap goa2 e5 pe7 I2-sat soo2 kia*5 ti7 I
bin7-cheng5 e5 Siong7-te3, chiu7-si7 it-seng po2-iu*2 goa2 kau3 ti7
kin-a2-jit8 e5 Siong7-te3, kiu3-siok8 goa2 thoat-li7 it-chhe3 e5
hoan7-lan7, hit e5 Su3-chia2, su3-hok hoo7 chi2 nng7 e5 gin2-a2; goan7
in kui ti7 goa2 e5 mia5-e7, kap goa2 choo2 A-pek-lah8-han2, goa2 e5 pe7
I2-sat, e5 mia5-e7; koh goan7 in ti7 se3-kai3-tiong si*-thoa*3
chin-choe7. 17). Iok-sek khoa*3 i e5 lau7-pe7 eng7 chia*3-chhiu2 hoa*7
ti7 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 thau5-khak, bo5 hoa*-hi2; chiu7 tha*2 i e5 lau7-pe7
e5 chhiu2, beh tui3 I2-hoat-lian5 e5 thau5-khak soa2 kau3 Ma2-na2-se e5
thau5-khak. 18). Iok-sek ka7 i e5 lau7-pe7 kong2, Goa2 e5 pe7 ah, m7-si7
an2-ni; chit-e5 si7 toa7-kia*2, kiu5 li2 eng7 chia*3-chhiu2 hoa*7 i e5
thau5-khak. 19). I e5 lau7-pe7 m7-than3 kong2, Goa2 chai, goa2 e5 kia*2,
goa2 chai; i iah8 beh chia*5-choe3 chit8-chok8, iah8 beh khoah-toa7;
chong2-si7 i e5 sio2-ti7 chiong-lai5 pi2 i khah-toa7; i e5 sio2-ti7 e5
hoo7-e3 beh chia*5-choe3 choe7-choe7 chok8. 20). Tng hit-jit8 chiu7 ka7
in chiok-hok kong2, I2-sek-liat8 lang5 beh ki2 li2 lai5 chiok-hok lang5
kong2, Goan7 Siong7-te3 hoo7 li2 chhin-chhiu*7 I2-hoat-lian5,
chhin-chhiu*7 Ma2-na2-se chit8-iu*7; tui3 an2-ni lip8 I2-hoat-lian5 ti7
Ma2-na2-se e5 tai7-seng. 21). I2-sek-liat8 koh ka7 Iok-sek kong2, Goa2
beh si2 lah; chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 beh kap li2 ti7-teh, beh chhoa7 lin2
to3--khi3 lin2 liat8-choo2 e5 toe7. 22). Goa2 cheng5 eng7 goa2 e5 keng,
goa2 e5 to, tui3 A-moo5-li7 lang5 e5 chhiu2 chhiu*2-lai5 hit te3-toe7,
goa2 ta* hoo7 li2, pi2 li2 e5 hia*-ti7 tit-tioh8 khah-ke.


[49] Nga2-kok kio3 i hiah e5 kia*2 lai5 kong2, Lin2 long2 chu7-chip8,
goa2 beh chiong lin2 jit8-au7 soo2 oe7 tu2-tioh8 e5 su7 ka7 lin2 kong2.

2). Nga2-kok chiah e5 kia*2, lin2 tioh8 chu7-chip8 lai5 thia*,

Tioh8 thia* lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 oe7.

3). Liu5-pian7 ah, li2 si7 goa2 e5 toa7-kia*2, goa2 e5 koan5-se3, goa2
e5 khui3-lat8 e5 khi2-thau5,

Ui-giam5 e5 tek8-sek--e5, koan5-leng5 e5 tek8-sek--e5.

4). Chong2-si7 li2 chhin-chhiu*7 chui2 teh-kun2, tek-khak boe7 tit-tioh8
ku thau5-ui7;

In-ui7 li2 peh-chiu*7 lin2 lau7-pe7 e5 bin5-chhng5;

Hit-si5 li2 phah la5-sam5 i; i peh-chiu*7 goa2 e5 phoo.

5). Se-bian7 Li7-bi7 si7 hia*-ti7;

In e5 to-kiam3 si7 hiong-ok e5 khi3-ku7.

6). Goa2 e5 sim-sin5 ah, li2 m7-thang kap in tang5 ke3-boo5;

Goa2 e5 sin5-hun5 ah, li2 m7-thang kap in e5 hoe7-chiong3 lian5-lok8.

In-ui7 in theng3-khi2 siu7-khi3, thai5-si2 lang5,

In chhut-chai7 i2-su3 koah-tng7 gu5-thui2 e5 toa7-kun.

7). In e5 siu7-khi3 so3-po7, thang chiu3-choo2;

In e5 hun7-khi3 chan5-jim2, iah8 si7 thang chiu3-choo2;

Goa2 beh pun-khui in ti7 Nga2-kok ke,

Si3-soa*3 in ti7 I2-sek-liat8 chok8.

8). Iu5-tai7 ah, li2 e5 hia*-ti7 beh o-lo2 li2;

Li2 e5 chhiu2 beh chhih8 tui3-tek8 e5 am7-kun2;

Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 kia*2 beh phak-pai3 ti7 li2 e5 bin7-cheng5.

9). Iu5-tai7 si7 soe3-chiah sai;

Goa2 e5 kia*2 ah, li2 tui3 soo2 jiau3--tioh8 e5 mih8, chiu7 chiu*7-khi3;

I khut-loh8, i thi*3-kha, chhin-chhiu*7 sai;

Iah8 chhin-chhiu*7 bu2 e5 sai, chi7-chui7 ka*2 jia2 i?

10). Koan5-peng3 bo5 li7-khui Iu5-tai7,

Ti7-li2--e5 bo5 li7-khui i nng7 ki kha e5 tiong-kan,

Kau3 Si7-lo5 lai5;

Liat8-pang long2 beh kui i.

11). Pak8 i e5 lu5-a2 ti7 phu5-to5-chhiu7,

Pak8 i e5 lu5-a2-kia*2 ti7 ho2 e5 phu5-to5-chhiu7;

Eng7 phu5-to5-chiu2 soe2 i e5 i-hok8,

Eng7 phu5-to5-chiap soe2 i e5 i-chiu*5.

12). I e5 bak8-chiu in-ui7 chiu2 lai5 ang5,

I e5 chhui3-khi2 in-ui7 leng lai5 peh8.

13). Se-poo3-lun5 beh khia7-khi2 hai2-khau2,

Beh choe3 pha-chun5 e5 hai2-khau2;

I e5 kai3 beh kau3 Se-tun3.

14). I2-sat-ka si7 iong2 e5 lu5,

To2 ti7 iu*5-tiau5 e5 tiong-kan;

15). I khoa*3 an-cheng7 choe3 ho2, khoa*3 thoo2-toe7 choe3 sui2;

A*3 keng-thau5 ta*-teh, chia*5-choe3 lo5-khoo2 e5 loo5-pok8.

16). Tan3 beh phoa*3-toan3 i e5 peh-si*3,

Chhin-chhiu*7 I2-sek-liat8 chi-phai3 e5 chit8-e5.

17). Tan3 beh choe3 loo7--nih e5 choa5,

Loo7-tiong e5 tok8-choa5;

Ka7 siong be2-toe5, khia7 e5 lang5 hia*3 tui3 au7-bin7 loh8--khi3.

18). Ia5-ho5-hoa ah, goa2 u7 theng3-hau7 Li2 e5 chin2-kiu3.

19). Ka-tek beh hoo7 kun-tui7 tui-pek,

Chong2-si7 i beh tui-pek in e5 kha-au7-ti*.

20). A-siat beh chhut ho2 e5 bi2-niu5,

Koh chhut ong5 soo2 chiah8 e5 ho2-mih8.

21). Na2-hut-tha-li7 si7 thau2-pang3 e5 lok8-bu2,

Chhut ho2-thia* e5 oe7.

22). Iok-sek si7 gau5 kiat ke2-chi2 e5 chhiu7-ki;

I e5 chhiu7-ki chhun-chhut chhiu*5-goa7.

23). Sia7-chi*3 e5 lang5 toa7 siong-hai7 i,

Eng7 chi*3 sia7 i, khun2-pek i;

24). Chong2-si7 i e5 keng iu5-gôan an5,

I e5 chhiu2 ia7 tit-tioh8 u7 lat8;

Che si7 tui3 Nga2-kok e5 Choan5-leng5--e5 e5 chhiu2,

(Tui3 che chiu7 u7 chhut bok8-chia2, I2-sek-liat8 e5 chioh8-poa*5),

25). Iah7 tui3 li2 e5 pe7 e5 Siong7-te3, I beh pang-chan7 li2;

Koh tui3 hit e5 Choan5-leng5--e5, I beh su3-hok li2;

Beh eng7 thi*-teng2 kang3-loh8 e5 hok-khi3,

Chhim-ian soo2 khng3 e5 hok-khi3,

I2-kip8 chiah8-leng seng-san2 e5 hok-khi3, long2 beh hoo7 li2.

26). Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 soo2 chiok e5 hok-khi3,

Ia*5-ke3 goa2 e5 pe7-kong soo2 chiok e5 hok-khi3,

Tit8-kau3 eng2 se3-tai7 e5 soa*-nia2 kek8-thau5 e5 pi*-kai3;

Chiah e5 hok-khi3 beh kang3-loh8 ti7 Iok-sek e5 thau5-khak,

Lim5-kau3 hit e5 kap hia*-ti7 tek8-piat8-e5 e5 thau5-khak-teng2.

27). Pian7-nga2-bin2 si7 gau5 peh-thiah e5 chhai5-long5;

Cha2-khi2-si5 chiah8 i soo2 jiau3--tioh8-e5,

E5-hng-si5 pun i soo2 chhiu*2--tioh8 e5.

28). Che it-chhe3 si7 I2-sek-liat8 e5 chap8-ji7 chi-phai3; che iah8 si7
in e5 lau7-pe7 tui3 in soo2 kong2 e5 oe7, ka7 in soo2 chiok-hok--e5;
long2 si7 chiau3 tak8-lang5 e5 hok-hun7, ka7 in chiok-hok. 29). I koh
hoan-hu3 in kong2, Goa2 beh to3-khi3 goa2 e5 liat8-choo2 hia, lin2 tioh8
chiong goa2 bai5-chong3 ti7 Hek-lang5 I2-hut-lun5 chhan5--nih e5 hiat8,
kap goa2 e5 pe7-kong siang5 soo2-chai7; 30). chiu7-si7 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7
Ban7-li7 e5 bin7-cheng5, Bek8-pi2-lah8 chhan5--nih e5 hiat8; hit e5
hiat8 kap chhan5 si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3 Hek-lang5 I2-hut-lun5 boe2
choe3 giap8, lai5 choe3 bong7-toe7 e5. 31). Ti7-hia bai5-chong3
A-pek-lah8-han2 kap i e5 boo2 Sat-lah8; koh ti7-hia bai5-chong3 I2-sat
kap i e5 boo2 Li7-pek-ka; goa2 iah8 ti7-hia bai5-chong3 Li7-a. 32). Hit
khu chhan5 kap hit lai7-bin7 e5 hiat8, si7 tui3 Hek-lang5 boe2--e5. 33).
Nga2-kok hoan-hu3 i hiah e5 kia*2 beng5-pek8, kha kiu-chiu*7 chhng5,
chiu7 khui3 tng7, to3--khi3 i e5 liat8-choo2 hia.


[50] Iok-sek phak ti7 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 bin7, thi5-khau3, chim--i.
Iok-sek hoan-hu3 su-hau7 i e5 i-seng, eng7 hiu*-liau7 koan3 i e5
lau7-pe7; i-seng chiu7 eng7 hiu*-liau7 koan3 I2-sek-liat8. 3). Koan3
sin-si tia*7-tioh8 e5 le7 tioh8 si3-chap8 jit8; hit e5 si3-chap8 jit8
moa2, koh Ai-kip8 lang5 ui7 i thi5-khau3 chhit-chap8 jit8.

4). Ui7-tioh8 i thi5-khau3 e5 jit8 i2-keng ke3, Iok-sek tui3 Hoat-lo2
ke-lai7 e5 lang5 kong2, Goa2 na7 ti7 lin2 e5 bin7-cheng5 tit-tioh8
un-tian2, chhia*2 lin2 thong-ti Hoat-lo2, ka7 i kong2, 5). Goa2 e5
lau7-pe7 kah goa2 chiu3-choa7 kong2, Goa2 beh si2 lah, li2 tioh8 chiong
goa2 bai5-chong3 ti7 Ka-lam5 toe7, ti7 goa2 ui7 pun2-sin soo2 kut8 e5
bong7; ta* kiu5 li2 chun2 goa2 chiu*7--khi3 bai5-chong3 goa2 e5
lau7-pe7, jian5-au7 goa2 beh to3-tng2--lai5. 6). Hoat-lo2 kong2, Li2
thang chiu*7--khi3 bai5-chong3 li2 e5 lau7-pe7, chiau3 i soo2 kah li2
chiu3 e5 choa7. 7). Tui3 an2-ni Iok-sek chiu*7--khi3 bai5-chong3 i e5
lau7-pe7; kap i sa*-kap chiu*7--khi3 e5, u7 Hoat-lo2 e5 cheng3
jin5-sin5, kap Hoat-lo2 ke-lai7 e5 tiong2-lo2, kap Ai-kip8 kok cheng3
tiong2-lo2. 8). Koh u7 Iok-sek choan5-ke, kap i hiah e5 hia*-ti7,
i2-kip8 i e5 lau7-pe7 e5 ke-koan3; chi2-u7 in e5 gin2-a2, kap iu*5-kun5
gu5-kun5, long2 lau5 ti7 Ko-san toe7. 9). Koh u7 chhia kap
khia5-be2--e5, hit-tin7 e5 lang5 put-chi2 choe7. 10). In kau3 Iok-tan3
ho5 goa7, A-tat8 e5 goo7-kak-tiu*5, chiu7 ti7-hia toa7 thi5-khau3, toa7
ai-siong; Iok-sek ui7-tioh8 lau7-pe7 pi-ai chhit-jit8. 11). Ka-lam5 toe7
khia7-khi2 e5 peh-si*3 khoa*3-ki*3 A-tat8 goo7-kak-tiu*5 e5 thi5-khau3,
chiu7 kong2, Che si7 Ai-kip8 lang5 chit8-tiu*5 e5 toa7 thi5-khau3;
in-ui7 an2-ni, hit e5 toe7 mia5 kio3 A-pek-bek8-se, si7 ti7 Iok-tan3 ho5
goa7. 12). Nga2-kok hiah e5 kia*2 chiu7 chiau3 lau7-pe7 soo2
hoan-hu3--e5 ka7 i choe3; 13). hiah e5 kia*2 chiong i un7 kau3 Ka-lam5
toe7, bai5-chong3 ti7 Ban7-li7 e5 thau5-cheng5, Bek8-pi2-lah8
chhan5--nih e5 hiat8, hit e5 hiat8 kap chhan5 si7 A-pek-lah8-han2 tui3
Hek-lang5 I2-hut-lun5 boe2 choe3 giap8, lai5 choe3 bong7-toe7 e5. 14).
Iok-sek bai5-chong3 in lau7-pe7 i2-au7, chiu7 kap cheng3 hia*-ti7,
i2-kip8 it-chhe3 kap i chiu*7-khi3 bai5-chong3 in lau7-pe7 e5 lang5,
long2 to3-tng2 Ai-kip8.

15). Iok-sek hiah e5 hia* khoa*3 in lau7-pe7 i2-keng si2, chiu7 kong2,
Kiam2-chhai2 Iok-sek beh oan3-hun7 lan2, chiau3 lan2 cheng5 khoan2-thai7
i long2-chong2 e5 phai*2, it-chin7 po3-eng3 lan2. 16). In chiu7 thok
lang5 khi3 ki*3 Iok-sek kong2, Li2 e5 lau7-pe7 be7 si2 e5 tai7-seng,
hoan-hu3 kong2, 17). Lin2 tioh8 tui3 Iok-sek an2-ni kong2, Cheng5 li2
chiah e5 hia* phai*2 khoan2-thai7 li2, kiu5 li2 sia3-bian2 in e5 ke3-sit
kap choe7-ok; ta* kiu5 li2 sia3-bian2 li2 e5 lau7-pe7 e5 Siong7-te3 e5
loo5-pok8 e5 ke3-sit. In tui3 Iok-sek kong2 chiah e5 oe7, Iok-sek chiu7
thi5-khau3. 18). I chiah e5 hia* koh lai5 phak ti7 i bin7-cheng5 kong2,
Goan2 si7 li2 e5 loo5-pok8. 19). Iok-sek ka7 in kong2, M7-bian2 kia*;
goa2 kiam2 thoe3 Siong7-te3 mah? 20). Cheng5 lin2 e5 i3-su3 si7 phai*2,
chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 e5 i3-su3 si7 ho2; beh po2-choan5 choe7-choe7
lang5 e5 si*3-mia7, chhin-chhiu*7 kin-a2-jit8. 21). Ta* lin2 m7-bian2
kia*; goa2 beh iu*2-chhi7 lin2, kap lin2 e5 kia*2-ji5. Tui3 an2-ni
Iok-sek eng7 chhin-ai3 e5 oe7 an-ui3 in.

22). Iok-sek kap in lau7-pe7 e5 ke-koan3 long2 tiam3 Ai-kip8; Iok-sek
chiah8 pah-it he3. 23). Iok-sek tit-tioh8 khoa*3-ki*3 I2-hoat-lian5
te7-sa* tai7 e5 sun; Ma2-na2-se e5 sun Ma2-kiat e5 kia*2, Iok-sek iah8
pho7 in ti7 kha-thau5-u. 24). Iok-sek tui3 i e5 hia*-ti7 kong2, Goa2 beh
si2 lah; chong2-si7 Siong7-te3 tek-khak khoa*3-koo3 lin2, chhoa7 lin2
tui3 chit soo2-chai7 chiu*7-khi3, kau3 I chiu3-choa7 eng3-un2 hoo7
A-pek-lah8-han2, I2-sat, Nga2-kok e5 toe7. 25). Iok-sek kah I2-sek-liat8
e5 kia*2-sun chiu3-choa7 kong2, Siong7-te3 tek-khak chiau3-koo3 lin2,
lin2 tioh8 chiong goa2 e5 kut-thau5 un7-chiu*7--khi3. Iok-sek si2,
tu2-a2 pah-it he3; lang5 eng7 hiu*-liau7 ka7 i koan3; chiong i siu-loh8
koan, theng5 ti7 Ai-kip8.
